Chapter 803: All-Out Fight Against Yun Zhi

“Attack, Third-in-Command!”

Under the hints of the duplicitous minister, Lu Yang, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s intelligence improved by leaps and bounds. She now understood the importance of sending someone to test the waters before a battle.

“Little Ling, Lianyi, the two of you must carefully observe Lass Yun’s combat style!”

The Everlasting Immortal initially wanted to refuse, but he was constrained by the Everlasting Dao Fruit that was controlled by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, making refusal impossible. He had to attack when duty called.

Seeing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy gather her subordinates with the resolve for a fight to the death, Yun Zhi’s eyes, calm as a lake, rippled slightly.

The Third-in-Command was the most valiant. Under the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s control, he launched the first attack.

“Great Carefree Palm!” With an unwavering gaze, the Third-in-Command delivered a palm strike. Brilliant light erupted, akin to a mountain deluge bursting forth, carrying the force of ten thousand bolts of lightning. Wherever it passed, space seemed to be violently torn asunder. Its might was shocking!

Yun Zhi likewise thrust out a palm. To onlookers, this palm strike seemed devoid of offensive power and produced no extraordinary phenomena. Only the Third-in-Command could clearly sense the terror contained within it.

Before Yun Zhi’s palm even touched the Third-in-Command, the latter’s raised right hand began to crack and shatter.

“Restore!” As the Third-in-Command shouted, his originally shattered soul reassembled itself piece by piece.

Yun Zhi gripped the Third-in-Command’s neck, and ice began to form, rapidly spreading.

Before the Third-in-Command could react, he was frozen into an ice sculpture.

Yun Zhi tossed the Third-in-Command aside and said calmly, “Next.”

Despite facing such a predicament, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy maintained her composure. She waved her hand, commanding her subordinates and troops.

“Attack together!”

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi lived up to their reputations as the two great immortals under the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Upon receiving her order, they charged forward first.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy embodied the spirit of a founding emperor leading a charge and breaking through the enemy’s lines, rushing ahead with greater fervor. Though she acted later, she arrived first, outpacing even Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi.

“Immortal Fairy Fist Technique!”

Lu Yang hid far away in the rear, witnessing the brutal battle of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s trio firsthand. They employed various combat techniques, dishing out immortal arts frequently, while Yun Zhi swept through all directions, dominating the field.

The air was thick with an atmosphere of slaughter and death. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy and her two aides fell one after another, as dead as they could be.

Lu Yang trembled as he watched the expressionless Yun Zhi walk toward him.

“Big Senior Sister, I’m not with them!” Lu Yang immediately declared his stance. My role as a duplicitous minister of the Great Dou Dynasty was merely a temporary expedient. My true allegiance lies with Big Senior Sister Yun Zhi!

“I know,” Yun Zhi said placidly, displaying neither joy nor anger. “Senior Immortal Fairy and the others will probably be dead for a while. Stay here with them. I won’t wait.”

“Oh.”

After half the time for an incense to burn, a miracle occurred. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s trio returned from death to the land of the living.

“Fortunately, this immortal was prepared and performed the Play-Dead Technique.”

The trio rejoiced over avoiding a situation that would shatter their Dao hearts.

Lu Yang thought, Even if you three had lost, your Dao hearts would be just fine.

“Second-in-Command, how are you? Are you hurt?”

“Uh, I didn’t fight Big Senior Sister.” Lu Yang felt that he needed to state his stance firmly. I can’t keep following the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s shenanigans every time she messes around.

“Then did Lass Yun hit you?”

“No, she didn’t.” If Yun Zhi had struck, Lu Yang would have been lying on the ground alongside the trio.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clapped. “Then it was also a draw for you! To think we fought Lass Yun to a draw! Let’s keep up the effort!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, isn’t your concept of a “draw” a bit too broad?

He then pointed at the Third-in-Command, who was frozen into an ice sculpture. “It wasn’t all draws. The Third-in-Command lost.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand dismissively. “No matter. We’ll kick him out of the Everlasting Lineage and just pretend he didn’t participate in the fight.

“This immortal has given it some thought. We were too hasty with our preparations for this battle. Next time, we should prepare properly in advance.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy began to reflect, striving to trip over the same stone repeatedly.

Lu Yang wondered, Do you mean preparing a grave in advance?

Then my epitaph should read: The Heavenly Court Young Creed Leader died in an internal conflict of the Heavenly Court.

“Oh right! We didn’t call the Little Herb Kings this time!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy remembered a group of crucial combatants.” The combat power of the Little Herb Kings shouldn’t be underestimated.

“Let’s go, let’s go, to the herb garden!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy urged Lu Yang.

“What about the Third-in-Command?”

“Don’t bother. The ice will melt on its own.”

~~~

Lu Yang led his two junior sisters to the herb garden.

At the entrance to the herb garden, Grandpa Ba was dozing off while contemplating how to teach his newly accepted disciple, Zhou Xing’er.

It’s been so long since I last taught that I’ve forgotten how.

“How did Junior Niece Yun Zhi teach Little Lu back then? I remember it started with juggling a giant vat?”

Just as Lu Yang reached the entrance, he heard Grandpa Ba recalling a past he would rather forget.

“Oh, it’s Little Lu...” Grandpa Ba opened his eyes and saw Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi standing behind Lu Yang. He was so startled that he tumbled right out of his rocking chair.

Why are the Dragon and Phoenix ancestors here?

“You’ve met Senior Lianyi before; I won’t introduce her. This is Senior Ao Ling, also a member of our Heavenly Court Creed.”

Grandpa Ba recalled the news from the East Sea, and his expression turned odd. I desperately want to know what kind of bewitching potion Lu Yang had fed the two ancestors with, first tricking the Phoenix Ancestor to the Heavenly Court Creed, and now the Dragon Ancestor.

“The three of us would like to stroll through the herb garden. That’s fine, right?” With two half-immortals standing behind him, Lu Yang spoke with more confidence than usual.

“To pluck herbs?”

“No, we’re just going in to chat with the Little Herb Kings.”

“Go on in then.”

At the moment, the Metamorphic Immortal Grass was being grown in the plot with the richest spirit energy in the herb garden.

“Let me tell all of you, don’t think arriving first makes you all special! We Little Herb Kings compete based on age, understand? Age!” the Metamorphic Immortal Grass announced to the Ginseng Doll and the others with an imperious air.

The Ginseng Doll and the others were all born after the ancient era, so their ages were considerably less than the Metamorphic Immortal Grass’s.

But the Ginseng Doll clearly didn’t accept this logic. It flexed its leaves and roots, sneering. “Attack! Let it experience what ‘strength reigns supreme’ means!”

The Little Herb Kings swarmed forward, some slapping with leaves, others whipping with roots, beating the Metamorphic Immortal Grass until it wailed in agony.

This was the scene Lu Yang’s trio witnessed upon arriving at the herb garden.

Lu Yang didn’t know whether he should intervene to stop this or wait until the Little Herb Kings finished before showing himself.

Soon, Lu Yang didn’t have to feel conflicted. The towering Dao Enlightenment Tree King spotted Lu Yang’s group and pulled the Little Herb Kings and the Metamorphic Immortal Grass apart.

“Human kid, you’re here?” The Ginseng Doll waved a root in greeting.

“What human kid? This is the Second-in-Command of the Everlasting Lineage. Show some respect, you little herb dolls!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy emerged to assert her authority.

“W-who are you?!” Seeing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy for the first time, the Metamorphic Immortal Grass stammered, terrified by her aura.

“Hmph, this immortal is the head of the Five Ancient Immortals, the Heavenly Court Ruler—the Everlasting Immortal Fairy!”

“An...an immortal?” The Metamorphic Immortal Grass was stunned, unable to believe a genuine immortal was hidden within Lu Yang’s body.

No wonder Lu Yang’s combat power is so high. It must be the result of an immortal’s tutelage.

“This immortal has brought two of the Heavenly Court’s Four Regents to visit you this time. I’ll also share some good news with you all!”

“What good news, what good news?” The three-inch-tall Little Herb Kings hopped in a circle around Lu Yang, welcoming the Everlasting Immortal Fairy atop his head on her inspection tour.

“Just now, the four of us fought Lass Yun and achieved a draw.”

“A draw? So impressive!” The Little Herb Kings gazed at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with worshipful admiration.

“This immortal believes that bringing all of you along next time might change the course of the battle. Are you willing to join?”

“We are willing!” The Little Herb Kings chorused in unison.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded, tremendously satisfied with the Little Herb King’s response. Their level of awareness alone is far better than the Third-in-Command’s.

Chapter 804: Advanced Nascent Soul Stage

The little herb kings had long been dissatisfied with Yun Zhi’s tyranny. Now that someone was finally willing to lead them in a crusade against her, they were naturally overjoyed.

Lu Yang felt that it was fortunate the Little Herb Kings were raised in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s herb garden, where the sect members harbored no ill intentions toward them. Otherwise, with their intelligence, who knows how many times they’d be hoodwinked in the outside world?

Even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could trick them, which goes to show just how gullible they are.

“Big Sis, when are we going to fight Yun Zhi?” The Ginseng Doll was quite excited.

Having followed Lu Yang for so long, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had learned one or two percent of his crafty schemes. She waved her hand. “As the art of war says, ‘those hasty cannot eat hot tofu’—haste makes waste. We just fought Yun Zhi once. She’s surely on guard now. Acting immediately isn’t the best choice. We need to strike when she least expects it.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy enjoyed extremely high prestige among the Little Herb Kings. They would listen to whatever she said. If she told them to pick another time to challenge Yun Zhi, they would pick another time.

Watching the Everlasting Immortal Fairy play with the Little Herb Kings, Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi whispered to each other.

“So this is the pure and innocent heart of a newborn; truly enviable.”

“This is where Everlasting-jiejie surpasses us.”

The Metamorphic Immortal Grass hadn’t yet adapted to the herb garden’s atmosphere, and neither was it very familiar with the Dao-Seeking Sect. It didn’t understand why the Little Herb Kings were so excited.

“Is this Yun Zhi you speak of really that difficult to deal with?”

The Ginseng Doll placed two root whiskers on its hips, finding the Metamorphic Immortal Grass arrogant. “If you can defeat the great devil Yun Zhi, we’ll let you be the big boss of this herb garden!”

The Metamorphic Immortal Grass sneered. Don’t look down on me just because of the beating I suffered earlier. I actually have a trump card. Not only can it boost one’s cultivation and increase the age of spirit plants, but I can also use this feature on myself to elevate my own age! This way, I can smoothly achieve human form and possess the strength of a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator right from the start!

The last spirit plant with such heaven-defying capabilities was called the Jianmu!

“It's a deal!”

The Metamorphic Immortal Grass charged furiously toward Heaven’s Gate Peak to challenge Yun Zhi and establish its authority in the garden.

“Hey, are you Yun Zhi? I’ve come to challenge you!”

Yun Zhi had invited Gan Tian over to drink tea and comprehend the Dao with her, also using this opportunity to clarify some questions regarding Gan Tian’s cultivation path.

A red clay stove warmed a pot where Wudao Enlightenment Tea leaves tumbled within. The fragrant aroma of fine tea wafted up. Just smelling it gave one a sense of enlightenment.

Hearing the Metamorphic Immortal Grass’s haughty tone, she pondered for a moment, then grabbed the Metamorphic Immortal Grass and stuffed it into the teapot, letting it steep alongside the Wudao Enlightenment Tea leaves.

Yun Zhi poured the tea. Its fragrance was richer than before. She pushed a red clay teacup toward Gan Tian. “Drink this. It can increase your cultivation.”

~~~

Ao Ling had stayed at the Dao-Seeking Sect for half a month. During this period, she not only studied the current division of factions but also visited Incarceration Peak, frightening both the prisoners and the child-like Grand-Shifu. She also met the Innate Daoist Priest, similarly scaring him out of his wits.

Lu Yang also accompanied Ao Ling to the scripture library, where she saw shelves lining the walls, full of cultivation manuals.

During their time at the scripture library, Lu Yang was quite nervous, worried that his shifu might have hidden a copy of Dragon Phoenix Transformation there. If Ao Ling found it, he would have no choice but to tearfully inherit the position of sect leader.

As the saying goes, “scourges live for a thousand years.” Ao Ling did not find Dragon Phoenix Transformation.

~~~

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was running a fortune-telling stall when he suddenly sneezed.

“Who’s thinking of me?”

He went over all the people he had provoked. It seems anyone could be thinking of me.

“Come to think of it, ever since Little Jin went home to visit family, my luck has improved quite a bit.”

~~~

Half a month later, Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi left the Dao-Seeking Sect together. Lu Yang didn’t know whether Ao Ling wanted to see the outside world or intended to unify the East Sea and present it to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

After the Dragon and Phoenix ancestors departed, Lu Yang concentrated on his cultivation.

After their journey to the East Sea, he was fully cognizant of how low his cultivation was, and that he wasn’t qualified to participate in battles at the immortal level.

Lu Yang became incredibly obedient, spending most of his time on cultivation or sparring with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

After enduring one-sided beatings over time, Lu Yang’s combat techniques became increasingly refined. He could now exchange a couple of moves with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul before suffering a beating.

“Jiayou, Second-in-Command! Soon you’ll be able to defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy encouraged Lu Yang, disregarding facts and relying purely on feelings.

~~~

In a flash, over a year passed.

The cultivation world was calm and uneventful. No major incidents as eye-catching as the East Sea affair occurred again.

The only topic worthy of repeated discussion was the growing momentum for unifying the East Sea after the Dragon Ancient Ancestor’s revival. People speculated whether the Dragon Ancient Ancestor was acting under the Heavenly Court Creed’s directive to unify the East Sea in preparation for the Battle of the Great Era.

Ao Ling led the sea tribes, bringing Penglai Island under her control and cracking down severely on its rampant piracy problems.

The Dreamlike Bubble Mirages production, Gourd Dolls Wreak Havoc in the Sea, received widespread acclaim. The scenes where the Kunpeng Tribe was taught a lesson were repeatedly watched by the sea tribes.

At the same time, Gourd Dolls Wreak Havoc in the Sea played a role in promoting the East Sea. Great Xia cultivators noticed massive, underdeveloped areas of the East Sea hiding all sorts of valuable natural treasures, and the number of cultivators heading to the East Sea steadily increased.

Lu Yang didn’t pay much attention to the matters outside. He properly devoted himself to cultivation and didn’t leave the Dao-Seeking Sect. During his breaks from cultivation, he simply wandered around places he had yet to visit within the sect.

Fortunately, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord didn’t go looking for trouble with Lu Yang. Lu Yang hadn’t seen a trace of the Vast Sea Daoist Lord. According to his little junior brother Qi Tongtian, aside from guiding him in cultivation, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord would use the Space Incipient Dao Fruit to travel to the East Sea’s Dragon Palace.

Out of his obligation as a good sworn brother, Lu Yang instructed Qi Tongtian to inform Meng Jingzhou about this.

Currently, he was opening his mouth like a whale. Boundless spirit energy from the outside world surged into his body, once again expanding his meridians, which had already swelled to their limits. Lu Yang’s skin rapidly turned red, a sign that his meridians were on the verge of shattering.

He gritted his teeth. Although the pain made him want to writhe on the ground, he never cried out.

Boom!

As the swallowed spirit energy hit a critical threshold, it was as though a door had been opened. Lu Yang’s body underwent visible changes. His meridians became more resilient, capable of containing even more spirit energy.

“Whew... I have broken through.”

Lu Yang exhaled a turbid breath and stood up with a smile. I’ve finally broken through to the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage. With my remarkable Sword Spirit Root, cultivating until the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage is merely a matter of time; there are no bottlenecks.

“With my current methods, even an Advanced Divine Transfiguration cultivator can’t do anything to me.” Lu Yang was referring to conventional methods, excluding the Spirit Medium Technique and the Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist.

“And Void Refinement cultivators don’t act recklessly. In other words, as long as I don’t encounter a Fusion cultivator, I can strut around the outside world without a care!”

Lu Yang cackled out loud. I’m now finally worthy to be called a “Nascent Soul old monster.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy yawned in the mental space. “But Second-in-Command, the enemies you encounter outside aren’t below the Fusion Stage, though.”

Lu Yang’s smile stiffened. That seems to be true.

Chapter 805: The Radiant Sun Creed’s Research Results

The exhilaration Lu Yang just felt from reaching the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage was thoroughly doused by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s bucket of cold water.

Seeing this, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hurriedly comforted him. “Aiya, reaching the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage is already impressive. Think about it, you don’t encounter Fusion Stage enemies every single time you go out.”

Lu Yang recalled the enemies he had faced: the Yu Emperor Wu Youdao, the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord, the Nightmare Supreme Lord, Hui Doudou... Indeed, none were at the Fusion Stage.

Just as Lu Yang reminisced about his past battle achievements, he suddenly felt a token at the front of his chest grow warm. He pulled out and saw it was the Radiant Sun Creed contacting him.

The token's message stated that the Radiant Sun Creed had recently achieved some results in their solar energy research and hoped that Young Creed Leader Lu would grace them with a visit to guide them. The location would be the same as before—the barbeque shop headquarters at Yanjiang Commandery. It also mentioned presenting the barbeque shop’s annual dividends to the Heavenly Court Creed.

Lu Yang had nothing better to do, so he agreed. Holy Son Long Jingzhou is still in seclusion, with no indication of when he will emerge. Such a minor matter doesn’t warrant troubling Big Senior Sister.

He informed several Heavenly King protectors of the matter, and they all readily agreed.

The Heavenly Court Creed set out in grand style.

~~~

At the barbeque shop headquarters, Creed Leader Chi of the Radiant Sun Creed and Mu Baiyi of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed were both nervous. It seemed less like welcoming colleagues and more like receiving their superiors for an inspection.

The two creed leaders’ fear was understandable. The impact of the immortal battle in the East Sea was enormous. It demonstrated that there were gradations of strength even among immortals, and Creed Leader Yun’s power surpassed the other immortal’s.

Furthermore, with Ao Ling displaying her might in the East Sea, Dou Heavenly Sovereign’s fame spread far and wide.

Every one of these events pointed to one fact—the Heavenly Court Creed was the world’s number one faction.

“Haha, it’s been a while, creed leaders,” Lu Yang greeted them jovially.

Seeing neither Creed Leader Yun, Dou Heavenly Sovereign, nor the Dragon and Phoenix ancestors, both Creed Leader Chi and Mu Baiyi quietly exhaled a sigh of relief, their psychological pressure easing significantly.

But facing Young Creed Leader Lu, the Heavenly Court Creed’s successor, they still dared not be careless.

Young Creed Leader Lu took his seat, and the five Heavenly King protectors stood behind him with cold, aloof expressions, while the two creed leaders personally bent to pour tea.

“Young Creed Leader, this is the barbeque business’ revenue over the past year, along with the income and expenditure ledgers.” Mu Baiyi cautiously pushed a storage ring toward Lu Yang. The spirit stones stored within were as vast as the ocean. Giving away so many spirit stones pained Mu Baiyi’s heart.

Lu Yang gave a meaningful look. Fifth Elder, the Myriad Treasures Heavenly King, accepted the storage ring and scanned it with his spiritual consciousness before bowing respectfully to report to Lu Yang. “Young Creed Leader, everything checks out.”

Lu Yang yawned with boredom. “Keep it then.”

Mu Baiyi sighed inwardly. As expected of the Heavenly Court Creed. They don’t even care about this paltry sum of money and don’t even ask how many spirit stones are in the storage ring.

“Creed Leader Mu, I believe you sought me out not just for a trifling matter like spirit stones, right?” Lu Yang took a sip of tea and smiled, as if he had seen through Mu Baiyi’s thoughts.

Mu Baiyi smiled obsequiously. “Young Creed Leader, you have clear discernment. Actually, there’s a matter I don’t understand. Please enlighten me.”

“What is it?”

Mu Baiyi deliberated over his choice of words, observing Lu Yang’s reaction as he spoke, fearing he might touch upon some taboo. “I heard your esteemed creed’s Ancient Ancestor Ao Ling once said this at the Old Dragon Emperor’s birthday banquet. ‘The world no longer knows of the Heavenly Court and the Underworld.’ I wonder what exactly this ‘Underworld’ is...”

Lu Yang had already anticipated this question from Mu Baiyi. A hint of a smile flickered in his eyes. “What, have you forgotten my words? I told you long ago that the affinity between our Heavenly Court Creed and your Nine-Netherworlds Creed originates from ancient times.”

Hearing this, Mu Baiyi’s heartbeat slowed for a few beats, his face unable to conceal his excitement. “Then this Underworld is indeed...”

“The place that governed the netherworld and the cycle of reincarnation in ancient times. After all living things between heaven and earth died, their souls would enter the Underworld to go through the Six Paths of Reincarnation.”

Lu Yang wasn’t lying to Mu Baiyi. This was what Ao Ling had told him.

Mu Baiyi and even Creed Leader Chi, who had always been at odds with the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, widened their eyes.

They weren’t the only ones who had noticed Ao Ling mentioning the “Underworld.” Many in the cultivation world were speculating about its meaning. But no one could clearly explain what the Netherworld actually was.

Now, they had finally received confirmation from Young Creed Leader Lu that the Underworld was the ancient Nine Netherworlds!

The five Heavenly King protectors were also hearing this explanation for the first time, but knowing Lu Yang was lying, they didn’t have such dramatic reactions.

Mu Baiyi’s face flushed with excitement. Fortunately, the Heavenly Court cherishes old ties; otherwise, such a good assignment as the barbeque shop business wouldn’t have fallen to our Nine-Netherworlds Creed.

And Young Creed Leader Lu once said that to display our capabilities in the Battle of the Great Era, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed must proceed step by step, “allying externally with the Demon Region and the East Sea!”

Now, with the Dragon Tribe unifying the East Sea, his words will be realized soon! In fact, they’re gradually coming to pass!

Is it divine foresight or premeditated planning?

Whichever it is, it’s enough to showcase how terrifying Young Creed Leader Lu is!

“Creed Leader Chi, let me see what your creed has been researching,” Lu Yang said with keen interest.

Taking over a year to produce results wasn’t considered slow progress. Things like solar lamps and solar water heaters were completely unprecedented in the cultivation world. The Radiant Sun Creed not only had to develop them but also reduce costs for widespread adoption among the populace. These were all challenges.

Under Lu Yang’s expectant gaze, Creed Leader Chi took out a scroll from his storage ring.

The scroll was unfurled, revealing a painting of a sun and several panels of unknown material. Considering the sun’s size, the area of these panels was terrifyingly massive.

The panels were engraved with numerous complex arrays. Lu Yang was not well-versed in arrays and had no idea what they were for.

Grandpa Ba, the Hundred Herbs Heavenly King, was proficient in arrays. He discerned something and let out a soft exclamation of surprise.

“Creed Leader Chi, this is...” Lu Yang saw no need to pretend he understood. The array’s complexity was probably something only a Fusion cultivator would figure out.

Posed with a question regarding his area of expertise, Creed Leader Chi grew excited. “Young Creed Leader Lu, after you spoke to me about solar energy, our entire creed was greatly shaken. Everyone has been researching how to harness solar energy fully.

“But halfway through the research, we discovered a problem. The continent has six sides, and our Central Continent is just one side. That is to say, no matter how we fully utilize solar energy, we can only harness one-sixth of it. The remaining five-sixths are wasted.”

“So?” Lu Yang vaguely guessed what was depicted on the scroll.

“So we planned to assemble an array on the sun’s surface that is capable of absorbing solar energy. Ideally, it should envelop the sun, such that no solar energy is wasted. Then, we’ll transmit the solar energy collected by the array down here.

“It’s just that researching this array was rather challenging. Fortunately, the entire sect worked as one and finally overcame the technical barriers.

“The array on the scroll is the result of our research.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Aren’t you all taking a bit too big a step?

Chapter 806: The Research Is Well Done, Just That the Direction Is a Bit Off

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, You Radiant Sun Creed folks really dare to imagine—installing an entire array around the sun.

Solar energy includes both light and heat. If your Radiant Sun Creed monopolizes solar energy, what will the Demon Region, the East Sea, and the Buddhist Kingdom use? Aren’t you afraid they’ll wipe you out?

And there’s also the Extreme North. Although the population is sparse, it doesn’t mean there are no cultivators. The Extreme North is cold to begin with, yet you still want to strip away their sunlight.

You are setting yourselves up to be the enemy of the whole world.

Moreover, this is such a massive project. Can your Radiant Sun Creed even handle it?

Hearing Lu Yang’s soft sigh, Creed Leader Chi grew tense. “Young Creed Leader Lu, is there a problem with our plan?”

“There are immortal-tier arrays on the sun that seal it off, preventing anyone from approaching. Do you know who created those immortal-level arrays?”

Creed Leader Chi shook his head. We've investigated for a long time, and countless colleagues have died without discovering the source of the immortal-level arrays.

Lu Yang lowered his voice, revealing a secret. “According to our Creed Leader’s investigations, those arrays were set up respectively by the founding Qian Emperor, the MidHeaven Emperor-Lord, and the founding Yu Emperor, Wu Yao. This is a contest between two immortals, separated by a hundred thousand years. It involves deeper matters that you should not learn of.

“If you set up another array around the sun, do you intend to get implicated in a conflict between immortals?”

In the past, when the Radiant Sun Creed dispatched people to the sun, the founding Qian Emperor paid no attention. However, if the Radiant Sun Creed truly set up a layer of array around the sun, it would be akin to a blatant provocation, a slap in the face.

If the Radiant Sun Creed were eliminated by the founding Qian Emperor, so be it; Lu Yang didn’t care. After all, that would make one less diabolic creed.

What Lu Yang worried about was that the founding Qian Emperor would act without restraint, unleashing overly powerful moves that would harm the innocent. Judging from the Mountain-River Lord’s actions, I can’t exclude the possibility of his superior doing such a thing.

Creed Leader Chi was shocked, his back drenched in cold sweat. There are actually two types of immortal-level arrays on the sun! With the Radiant Sun Creed’s strength, if we get entangled in a conflict between immortals, even total annihilation without our corpses and bones remaining would be considered fortunate!

“Did you get any other results from your research?”

“Yes, yes, we did,” Creed Leader Chi hurriedly replied, continuing to rummage through his storage ring. As he searched, he said, “While researching how to set up arrays around the sun, we incidentally developed some by-products.”

Lu Yang thought, By-products should be fine.

Before he could clearly see what Creed Leader Chi had pulled out, his vision went black. The entire room was plunged into darkness, making Lu Yang suspect that Creed Leader Chi was trying to take advantage of the chaos to harm him.

The three creeds held their meeting at night, after the barbeque shop closed, and the hall was lit with lamps.

When Creed Leader Chi produced the research result, it was as if a sinister wind swept through, extinguishing all the lamps.

Fortunately, none among those attending the three diabolic creeds’ interim meeting were weaklings. All of them could use their spiritual consciousness and didn’t need light to see their surroundings.

“What’s the deal with this candle of yours?” With his spiritual consciousness, Lu Yang observed that Creed Leader Chi had taken out a large red candle. Once this candle appeared, all other candles in the room went out.

“This is a solar-powered candle. During the day, the candle absorbs solar energy, and at night, it can be lit.”

“Then why has this room suddenly turned dark?”

“This thing can absorb the surrounding light and heat. Once it absorbs all the light and heat, the surroundings naturally have no more light,” Creed Leader Chi explained matter-of-factly.

“...Isn’t the absorption efficiency of your candle a bit too high?”

And this is just a by-product of researching arrays for the sun. If you actually set up arrays around the sun, wouldn’t the cultivation world simultaneously plunge into an ice age and a dark age?

“Isn’t higher efficiency better?” Don’t they all say that the higher the efficiency, the better? Creed Leader Chi had expended considerable effort to achieve peak efficiency.

“You should lower it.”

“Alright then.”

“Old Chi, give our Nine-Netherworlds Creed a box of these candles with high solar absorption efficiency.” Mu Baiyi looked at the candle with keen interest.

This is good stuff! With candles like this, we wouldn’t have to worry about lacking the right ambience for future meetings.

Lu Yang couldn’t quite understand the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s aesthetic tastes.

“Any other research results?”

“Yes. We also discovered we can use solar energy to boil water.”

Lu Yang nodded. Solar water heater. I’ve seen that. It works well.

Creed Leader Chi lit the candle, and the room was illuminated once more.

He produced a large wooden bucket, another one of their research results. It had already absorbed solar energy during the day. He filled it with water. Within a few breaths, the water in the bucket began bubbling vigorously. As usual, it was highly efficient.

Seeing this, Creed Leader Chi said excitedly, “We also discovered that the steam produced after boiling water contains immense power. Perhaps we could use steam to do something!

“But we’ve only conducted preliminary research in this area and haven’t achieved significant results yet.”

Lu Yang, “...”

This is the first time I’ve seen someone develop steam engines from solar energy.

“Stop researching steam. Focus on researching solar energy properly.”

“Any other research results?”

Creed Leader Chi scratched his head sheepishly. For over a year, they had mainly researched how to set up arrays around the sun. Unfortunately, Lu Yang had vetoed that. The solar candle and water heater were merely by-products.

“Although we don’t have other research results, after our two creeds collaborated, we discovered we could establish a new business.”

“What new business?”

This time, it was Mu Baiyi’s turn to elaborate. “You see, some places have water burial customs, right? They cast the corpses into rivers, lakes, or seas for fish to consume, signifying a return to nature.

“We can broaden our scope of thinking to cremation, casting the corpse onto the sun. According to the mortality statistics Old Chi provided, even a Fusion cultivator would be reduced to ashes on the sun.

“Don’t you think this principle is similar or even more thorough than that of water burial?

“Considering that a person’s soul doesn’t dissipate until seven days after death, we could schedule the cremation to be after the seventh day, preventing the soul from contacting the sun and directly melting.”

Clearly, Mu Baiyi had given this deep thought, even accounting for the folk custom of the first seven days after death.

“Young Creed Leader Lu, do you think this business is feasible?”

Lu Yang remained silent for a long while before slowly asking, “Putting aside other considerations, what would customers think about a barbeque shop operating a funeral service, and a cremation one at that?”

The two creed leaders contemplated. It does seem a bit off.

“Never mind. I can see that your two creeds have put great effort into cooperating and achieving a win-win situation. It’s just that your line of thinking has deviated slightly. Keep working hard!” Like a big brother, Lu Yang gave both creed leaders firm pats on the shoulder, his tone encouraging.

“If the candles and buckets can be mass-produced, they’ll likely be well-received.”

~~~

On the way back to the Dao-Seeking Sect, Lu Yang suddenly asked, “Elders, what are your views on the Radiant Sun Creed’s research results?”

Fifth Elder earnestly replied, “Suitable for joining our Artifact Refinement Peak.”

Chapter 807: High Efficiency

Lu Yang wondered if everyone on Artifact Refinement Peak had a similar kind of thinking. How exactly did they rely on patent royalties to make money for the Dao-Seeking Sect?

He felt that he was a person with a steadfast Dao heart. Though I’m surrounded by a bunch of lunatics, I’ve never been influenced by them. My way of thinking is normal.

Lu Yang’s inner thoughts prompted a nod of approval from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who pointed at the five elders. “Yes, yes, they are lunatics. Only the two of us have a normal way of thinking.”

“Look at what the Radiant Sun Creed has been researching. They haven’t fully utilized solar energy at all. If it were up to this immortal, I would just push the sun a bit toward the Extreme North, melt the glaciers there, revive the plants, and make the climate pleasant.”

Lu Yang thought to himself, Immortal Fairy, are you intending to turn the Extreme North into the Extreme North Sea?

When Lu Yang returned to Heaven’s Gate Peak and prepared to hand over the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s tribute to Yun Zhi, he chanced upon her speaking with Meng Jingzhou.

“Little Junior Brother is here too. Perfect. Both of you are clever; you two are suited to handle this matter.” Yun Zhi beckoned Lu Yang over.

Originally, Yun Zhi wanted Lu Yang to handle it. But at the time, Lu Yang was at the barbeque shop hoodwinking the two creed leaders, so Yun Zhi had to settle for the next best option, summoning Meng Jingzhou, who had just emerged from seclusion.

“Big Senior Sister, what’s the matter?”

“You also know that the Founding Ancestor has been with our sect for a year now. He has smoothly cultivated to the Foundation Establishment Stage. According to the rules, after reaching the Foundation Establishment Stage, every disciple must complete two missions annually.

“Originally, I was of the opinion that the Founding Ancestor need not go on sect missions. He had enough experience from when he was young. But the Founding Ancestor is very obstinate. He said he couldn’t have special treatment and insisted on doing missions. A few days ago, he just completed his first mission, during which an incident occurred.”

“What kind of incident?” Lu Yang asked curiously.

“He got lost.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“I’m worried he might encounter danger again, so I planned to find someone clever and quick-witted to accompany him.”

“So that’s how it is.” Lu Yang nodded. This is very much in line with the Founding Ancestor’s character.

“Don’t worry, Big Senior Sister. Leave it to Old Meng and me. We guarantee we’ll protect the Founding Ancestor properly!”

Meng Jingzhou thought of another problem. “But the Founding Ancestor doesn’t seem very willing to have people follow him. If we tail him secretly and only act when danger arises, wouldn’t we be exposed?”

Yun Zhi had selected both Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou because the two had interacted with the Innate Daoist Priest before. Even if they were discovered, the Innate Daoist Priest wouldn’t say much for the sake of face.

Lu Yang pondered for a bit. “This problem isn’t hard to solve. We just need to add one item to the redeemable items at the Great Mission Hall.”

~~~

“Before setting out, I need to redeem some life-preserving items,” the Innate Daoist Priest mumbled to himself.

Despite his childish face, he had a plethora of jianghu experience. He wouldn’t set off without preparation. It was just that he had no spare spirit stones and couldn’t redeem anything too good.

“Let me see... Spring Breeze Restoration Pill—it can quickly restore spirit energy. One hundred twenty contribution points. A bit expensive.

“Heart Wrencher—a highly toxic substance. Ten contribution points... Wait, why does the sect sell poison, and so cheap at that?

“Triple Yang Power Pill—consuming it grants Triple Yang Power, greatly enhancing combat power for a short time. No side effects after consumption. One hundred contribution points.”

The Innate Daoist Priest contemplated. It seems like a pill for temporarily boosting combat power. It’s very helpful for me, and the price is suitable.

“This will be the one.”

After the Innate Daoist Priest finished his preparations, he set off for his destination.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou tailed him covertly. Both were now at the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage, while the Innate Daoist Priest was only at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage. He couldn’t possibly detect them.

“By the way, what mission did the Founding Ancestor accept?” Lu Yang asked Meng Jingzhou.

“It says there’s a small village called Wangjia Gully in Ji Province, located in the old forest deep in the mountain. It takes two hours to walk down and reach the small town at the foot of the mountain. Several disappearances have occurred in Wangjia Gully. All missing individuals were young, strong men. It seems those men had their minds bewitched by something and were lured away.

“The local authorities have sent people to investigate, but unfortunately, they found nothing. Wangjia Gully is surrounded by mountains. It’s not easy to find those missing persons, even if one spreads their spiritual consciousness. Not to mention, that place doesn’t have any formidable cultivators; being able to cultivate spiritual consciousness at all is already an achievement. They can’t count on using it to locate people.

“The senior brother at the Great Mission Hall deduced from the intelligence that these disappearances were likely the work of a demonic being that smuggled itself into Great Xia, and its strength hasn’t reached the Golden Core Stage.”

Although the Innate Daoist Priest was at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage, he possessed combat power comparable to the Basic Golden Core Stage. It could be said that no one at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage was stronger than him. This was the advantage of dispersing his cultivation and cultivating anew.

Lu Yang mulled it over. “This mission sounds like it’ll take a long time. The Founding Ancestor will have lots to busy himself with.

“All those who went missing are young, strong men. I’m not sure if the demonic being fancies their masculine yang energy for a blood sacrifice or their bodies for dual cultivation.”

Meng Jingzhou nodded. “That demonic being is cautious. It made the missing persons leave the small village voluntarily, leaving almost no clues. Moreover, with so much time passed, it’ll be more difficult to find any leads.”

The two analyzed the mission. If it were them, they also wouldn’t have a good solution. They could only start with door-to-door investigation, study what common traits the missing persons had, then disguise themselves as ordinary people, hoping the demonic being would kidnap them.

Going through that whole process would take at least half a month.

That wasn’t even counting the travel time of the round trip.

The Innate Daoist Priest boarded a flying vessel, resting his eyes closed. He continuously ran simulations in his mind to figure out how to complete the mission.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou secretly flew behind, nearly getting spotted by the captain. If they were discovered, they would surely be suspected of being plundering cultivators planning to rob the flying vessel.

Fortunately, both were experienced, and no mishaps occurred.

The Innate Daoist Priest estimated he was close to his destination. He opened an umbrella and leaped, landing in the old forest deep in the mountain. Releasing his right hand, the umbrella closed and flew back to the flying vessel with a whoosh.

“This should be near Wangjia Gully,” the Innate Daoist Priest murmured to himself, surveying his surroundings. Noticing it was desolate and uninhabited, he felt a bit apprehensive.

“Should be, right?”

He walked into the mountain according to the mission’s description and his own intuition.

After walking for about two hours, he finally saw a place with signs of human habitation.

It was a cave. At the entrance was an extinguished fire pit, which looked like it had gone out less than a day ago.

The Innate Daoist Priest entered the cave. Hearing sounds from inside, he happily quickened his pace, then called out in a resonant voice. “Excuse me, may I know how I could get to Wangjia Gully?”

Noticing the situation in the cave, he froze.

Inside the cave was an alluring woman, completely naked and flicking a snake-like tongue. She was intimately entwined with several well-built men.

Spotting the Innate Daoist Priest, the woman also froze.

“A cultivator? How did you find this place?”

Chapter 808: Triple Yang Power

The snake demon couldn’t understand. My hiding place is extremely well-hidden, with no way to trace it. How did this person find me?

“Ah? I found what place?” The Innate Daoist Priest was baffled by the snake demon’s question. If I’d found the place, why would I be asking for directions?

In the shadows, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged glances with each other. How did we skip the entire process in between and directly run into the enemy’s lair?

All four people were dumbfounded.

“Little cultivator, come play with jiejie.” The snake demon had smooth, white hair, her eyes as alluring as silk. She exhaled a soft, orchid-like breath and extended a finger, seducing the Innate Daoist Priest.

The snake demon was extremely confident in herself. I’m a beauty to begin with, and coupled with my allure arts, no Foundation Establishment cultivator can withstand such temptation.

She could tell that the other party was merely a little cultivator who had just reached the Foundation Establishment Stage. With his delicate features, he’s perfect to keep as a male pet.

The snake demon’s allure arts were superb. Even the Innate Daoist Priest nearly succumbed. But as a former great Fusion cultivator who dispersed his cultivation to start anew, he had his own methods to counter allure arts.

“Epoch Eyes!” He rubbed his eyes, and the allure arts no longer affected him.

“What’s ‘Epoch Eyes?’” Lu Yang was stunned. He hadn’t heard of it, but judging by the name, it was related to time. Could it be eyes that can foresee the future and predict the opponent’s movements?

Meng Jingzhou shook his head; he hadn’t heard of it either.

Lu Yang had no choice but to ask the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

With a rare solemn expression, she said, “It’s a type of eye related to time. It can see what the other person will look like when they are old.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Do you know it then, Immortal Fairy?” Although the effect of this move is...hard to describe, it can indeed resist allure arts.

“No, I don’t know. Don’t learn it,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stated flatly.

The Innate Daoist Priest flipped his palm, revealing a small golden magical seal. Engraved on the seal were the characters “Innate Dao-Seeking.”

This was his life-bound magical treasure, originally a Fusion-level artifact. Given that he couldn’t fully activate it at his current cultivation, he had to seal most of its functions, suppressing the magical treasure to a level he could wield.

“Go!” the Innate Daoist Priest shouted, hurling the small seal at the snake demon.

The small seal flashed with golden light, dazzling the snake demon for a moment. She tried to twist her waist to dodge but was a beat too slow. It grazed her wrist and cut a large gash, causing blood to flow profusely.

“Puny human cultivator, you’re courting death!”

The snake demon used her bloodline power to stop the bleeding temporarily, but the wound didn’t fully heal. She transformed into a giant white serpent as thick as a bowl, baring her venomous fangs. Opening her maw wide, she lunged at the Innate Daoist Priest.

“Just a puny cultivator who has reached the Foundation Establishment Stage recently, yet you dare come alone!” The snake demon’s expression turned vicious. Since you won’t become a male pet, you shall stay here forever!

The Innate Daoist Priest had immense experience in combat. He calmly took a huge leap backward. The spot where he had been was smashed into a large crater by the snake demon.

From the brief exchange, he discerned that his opponent was at the Basic Golden Core Stage.

Seeing that the snake demon still wanted to bite him, the Innate Daoist Priest formed a hand seal with his right hand. The Innate Dao-Seeking Seal enlarged, wedging itself in the snake demon’s mouth.

“Demon-Subduing Talisman!”

He brought two fingers together and swiftly traced a talisman in the air, striking the snake demon’s vital point. The snake demon would have shrieked in pain, but her mouth was covered by the Innate Dao-Seeking Seal, which prevented her from screaming.

“Shuang’er, I’m here to help you!” A sharp cry came from deep within the cave.

It was another snake demon that had assumed form, and she looked exactly like the one before them.

“Twins?” The Innate Daoist Priest hadn’t expected there would be an accomplice, and one at the Basic Golden Core Stage at that.

“For you to be able to find us sisters hiding here, you probably have some skill. Stay and have fun with us too!”

“You’re hiding in such an obvious place, yet you blame me for being able to find you?” The Innate Daoist Priest also registered what was happening. These snake demons are the targets of my mission. The robust men lying scattered across the ground are the missing people from Wangjia Gully.

The problem is, this is a place that I could find just by wandering around. Why would you sisters think it is well-hidden?

The older snake demon slapped the snake demon named Shuang’er, forcing her to spit out the magic seal. The elder sister then transformed into a giant white serpent. Sharing a tacit understanding, the snake demon sisters attacked simultaneously, circling the Innate Daoist Priest.

The Innate Daoist Priest tried several times to break through the encirclement, but all his attacks were deflected by the smooth snake scales. Even he himself was almost ensnared a few times.

He stopped targeting their vital points. The sisters were already guarding against that, so success was impossible. Seizing the moment they were distracted, the Innate Daoist Priest gripped the seal and delivered a palm strike toward Shuang’er’s dantian area.

This was a common combat technique among Golden Core cultivators, called ‘Shaking Golden Core.” It could make the golden core vibrate, temporarily severing its connection to the body, thereby creating an opening.

“Ah, you can fight like that too?” Lu Yang was astonished. Why hadn’t anyone taught me to fight like this against Golden Core opponents?

If not for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s commentary, he wouldn’t have known about the “Shaking Golden Core” method.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rolled her eyes. “How many of your opponents have been at the Golden Core Stage?”

Lu Yang thought about it. It does seem like I haven’t fought many Golden Core cultivators.

“Wait, when I was at the Advanced Golden Core Stage, I went to the jungle at the border and fought a group of Golden Core demon beasts.” That was a whole horde of Golden Core demon beasts! The Immortal Fairy never mentioned the Shaking Golden Core method.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand, looking like she was concerned for Lu Yang. “Shaking Golden Core is a combat technique that relies on clever tricks. If you had used this method, you wouldn’t have been able to cultivate an Unbeatable Momentum, much less an Unbeatable Golden Core.”

“...I wasn’t exactly pursuing an Unbeatable Golden Core either.”

Although the snake demon sisters were caught off guard by Shaking Golden Core, they weren’t novice cultivators. They quickly stabilized their dantian to prevent the Innate Daoist Priest from launching another sneak attack.

Shuang’er suddenly spun and lashed out with her tail, attempting to strike the Innate Daoist Priest. The latter had anticipated it, leaping upward to dodge the blow.

However, he hadn’t expected the older snake demon sister to seize this opportunity while he was midair and unable to dodge, also extending her tail and sweeping it toward him.

“Gah—” The Innate Daoist Priest crashed into the stone wall, ending up covered in dust.

In a one-on-one fight, the Innate Daoist Priest feared neither demon. But with two demons joining forces, especially sisters with linked hearts, he was constantly placed at a disadvantage.

Several gashes appeared on the Innate Daoist Priest’s body. He tried several times to leave the cave and fight in an open area, but was blocked by the snake demon sisters.

The Innate Daoist Priest panted heavily, putting some distance between himself and the snake demon sisters. It appears that winning with my own methods alone would be challenging.

He whipped out a pill exuding warmth from the front of his robes—the Triple Yang Power Pill he had redeemed for one hundred contribution points!

After he swallowed the pill, a warm current flowed through his body, permeating his limbs and bones.

“It really works.” He was overjoyed, feeling an endless stream of energy surge within his body.

But immediately afterward, the Innate Daoist Priest lost that power, leaving him utterly flabbergasted. The warm current flowed out of his body through his limbs, dripping onto the ground and forming a large array.

Above the array, thick smoke billowed. Two indistinct figures appeared within the smoke.

As the smoke dissipated, the two figures revealed their true appearances—it was Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“Founding Ancestor, you were looking for us?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou pretended to be oblivious to the course of events, his gaze vacant with confusion.

“Why are you two here? Where’s my Triple Yang Power?” The Innate Daoist Priest was floored. How does consuming a pill result in two people appearing?

“We two are.”

Lu Yang pointed at himself. “I’m one yang.”

Then he pointed at Meng Jingzhou beside him. “He has two pure yang nascent souls, so he’s two yang.”

Chapter 809: Not A Single One Can Get Away

“Is this what the Triple Yang Power is supposed to be? Why does it seem a bit different from what I’d imagined?” The Innate Daoist Priest was puzzled, but upon careful contemplation, he felt that Lu Yang’s explanation was reasonable.

Lu Yang explained, “Other sects give their pills very exaggerated names, whereas our sect is more traditional—we don’t go for flashiness but focus on actual substance. Whatever effect the pill has, that’s the name it’ll get. I once used a Ten-Buffalo Strength Pill before, and it summoned ten buffalo demons.”

He cited his personal experience to prove the Triple Yang Power Pill was a summoning-type pill. We definitely weren’t waiting for the pill to emit smoke before we sneaked over.

“So that’s how it is.” The Innate Daoist Priest nodded, feeling quite gratified. I didn’t expect the Dao-Seeking Sect to be so traditional.

For an old fellow like him with rigid thinking, he liked tradition most, though in his era, there hadn’t been such realistic pills.

“Demonic fiends, surrender now!” Meng Jingzhou shouted angrily. Two nascent souls brimming with yang energy flew out, radiating waves of heat.

“N-Nascent Soul Stage?!” The snake demon sisters were stupefied, frozen in fear.

Even if Great Xia has many cultivators, it shouldn’t be to the extent that we can casually run into Nascent Soul cultivators, right?

Also, why does he have two nascent souls?

Lu Yang felt regretful. Old Meng shamelessly stole my chance to show off. The Triple Yang Power Pill was clearly my idea.

But then again, I can’t casually release my nascent soul as I please, like Old Meng.

The snake demon sisters quickly regained their composure. “Don’t think only you have people backing you; we have too!” We’re no match for Nascent Soul cultivators, but it’s not like we have no backing.

Lu Yang was curious to see what kind of backing these sisters had. He let them call for help.

The older snake demon sister took out a scale and snapped it forcefully.

Before long, a rumbling sound came from deep within the forest, as if some colossal creature was moving through the woods, colliding with boulders.

“Who dares bully my daughters?!” A gigantic head of a snake blocked the cave entrance, its frosty slit-like pupils fixed on Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

“We are from the Dao-Seeking Sect. Your two daughters have broken the law and need to come with us.” Lu Yang displayed his identity jade tablet.

The giant white serpent revealed a human-like smile, or to be exact, a sneer. Is the Dao-Seeking Sect that impressive? I can’t beat you, but can’t I hide?

With a bang, she transformed into a mature woman in white robes, retaining her charm despite her age. She charged into the cave entrance, intending to rely on her Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage cultivation to rescue the snake demon sisters.

Such cultivation was insignificant before Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. The latter performed Three Heads Six Arms, and six powerful arms directly pressed the white-robed woman to the ground.

“Please show mercy!” Another snake demon arrived belatedly; it was the white-robed snake woman’s husband.

“Fellow Daoists, I hope you can be lenient.” This snake demon assumed human form and kept smiling apologetically. He knew this was Great Xia territory—opposing the Dao-Seeking Sect would lead to no good end.

“A small token of appreciation. Please accept it.” This snake woman was savvy, knowing not to use force. He produced a storage ring containing three hundred thousand spirit stones.

“Dad, no need to give them spirit stones. They have no reason to capture us. It’s not like we sisters forced these people!” The snake sisters had evidently been in Great Xia for a long time and were aware of its rules—one couldn’t arrest people arbitrarily.

“You didn’t force them?” The Innate Daoist Priest pointed at the men lying scattered around. The fight earlier was so intense, yet these men didn’t react at all. Obviously, their minds are addled, and they’ve lost perception of the outside world.

“That’s just a playful kink.”

The snake demon sisters used their demonic arts to release control over these men, restoring their mental clarity.

Although they had returned to their senses, upon seeing the snake demon sisters, they still wore infatuated expressions. When the Innate Daoist Priest asked if they had been forced by the snake demons, they all said they had been willing.

“But you harvested yin to supplement yang, which also violates the law!” The Innate Daoist Priest thought of another reason. Balancing yin and yang is the righteous path, but the snake demon sisters are both at the Basic Golden Core Stage. How could they achieve mutual complementation with mortals?

“Who said we harvested yin to supplement yang?” The snake demon sisters seemed to have anticipated this question from the Innate Daoist Priest.

The Innate Daoist Priest carefully examined the men’s conditions and found they indeed hadn’t been harvested. They looked weak because of excessive indulgence over the past few days.

Excessive indulgence leading to kidney deficiency did not violate the law.

“Then why did you two sleep with so many men?” The Innate Daoist Priest was confused.

“High sex drive.”

The Innate Daoist Priest, “...”

“But you crossed the border illegally.”

“Ridiculous! We came through proper procedures!” Their family lived in the mountains, but that didn’t mean they had sneaked into Great Xia. They were simply accustomed to living in mountain forests.

This stumped the Innate Daoist Priest. As for kidnapping, that’s even less applicable. These men clearly came willingly. At most, they didn’t inform the villagers when they left.

They really didn’t commit any crime?

The snake demon sisters sneered. Don’t think just because we’re demons, we don’t understand the law. We’ve studied it carefully. We don’t even charge money, so it can’t even count as prostitution.

Lu Yang pulled out chains and tied up the snake demon sisters without a word, throwing them into a panic.

“On what grounds are you tying us up?!”

Lu Yang curled his lip. “You make it sound like there’s no crime committed. Isn’t this the classic crime of ‘group licentiousness?’”[1]

Once the snake demons were sent to the nearby authorities and a document of proof was issued, the mission would be considered complete.

Meanwhile, Meng Jingzhou tied up these men. The crime of group licentiousness only punished the organizers, but as participants, although these men were not criminally liable, they couldn’t avoid administrative punishment[2]—a detention for at least ten days.

“And you, you also need to come with us to the authorities.” Lu Yang bound the white-robed woman with chains.

“Why are you binding me? I didn’t sleep with these men. Even if you’re from the Dao-Seeking Sect, you can’t arrest people randomly,” the white-robed woman lashed out angrily.

Lu Yang rolled his eyes, too lazy to bother with such legal ignorance. “I already said we’re from the Dao-Seeking Sect and carrying out official duties, yet you still tried to snatch people away right in front of the three of us. That’s purely ‘obstruction of official duties.’”

He turned to the white-robed woman’s husband. “Are you planning to come with us voluntarily, or shall we bind you?”

“What did I do?” The snake demon husband was perplexed. I didn’t even intend to make a move from start to finish.

“Attempted bribery.”

Lu Yang then looked at the Innate Daoist Priest, who was frozen in place. “And you.”

Lu Yang suddenly remembered that the snake demon named Shuang’er had tried to force the Innate Daoist Priest to be her male pet. The Innate Daoist Priest refused, and Shuang’er attacked him. This might constitute attempted rape or attempted indecent assault. He wanted to remind the Innate Daoist Priest that he shouldn’t be surprised if the authorities asked for a victim impact statement.

The Innate Daoist Priest watched as Lu Yang convicted each person of their crime. Seeing Lu Yang turn to him, he grew tense and asked in a tremulous voice, “Is it too late for me to turn myself in?”

1. This is an offense in China that is punishable up to 5 years. ☜

2. This is less for criminal justice but to maintain order and ensure compliance. ☜

Chapter 810: Emulating Juniors

“What crime did you commit?” Lu Yang didn’t understand why the Innate Daoist Priest suddenly wanted to turn himself in for no reason. Moreover, the Innate Daoist Priest appeared quite nervous.

Did the Founding Ancestor commit some crime without my knowledge?

The Innate Daoist Priest pondered for a long while. Even during the Great Yu era, I had been the honest type. After dispersing my cultivation to cultivate anew, I haven’t made any mistakes.

He said somewhat uncertainly, “Uh, does founding the Dao-Seeking Sect count...?”

Meng Jingzhou was so startled that he lunged forward like an arrow, covering the Innate Daoist Priest’s mouth. “You mustn’t say things like that carelessly.”

Wangjia Gully fell under the jurisdiction of Jinniu City.[1] Lu Yang needed to send the snake demon family and the several infatuated, robust men from Wangjia Gully to the Jinniu City authorities to see how they would handle it.

Lu Yang’s trio escorted these demons and humans down the mountain. Upon reaching Jinniu City and declaring their identities to the authorities, the city lord put aside his tasks and received them personally.

“Two Divine Transfiguration snake demons and two Golden Core snake demons?” The city lord was flabbergasted by Lu Yang’s haul. He was the Divine Transfiguration cultivator in Jinniu City, at the Intermediate Divine Transfiguration Stage.

I’ve been the City Lord of Jinniu City for over a decade and have only encountered one case involving a Divine Transfiguration cultivator as the perpetrator. Yet these Dao-Seeking Sect disciples just arrived and delivered two?

“Don’t wrong a good demon! I never bribed anyone at all!” The snake demon husband cried injustice, insisting Lu Yang and the others were framing him. He hadn’t taken out any spirit stones for bribery.

At the time, the men from Wangjia Gully were still delirious and couldn’t testify. The snake demon family’s statements would surely favor the husband. Overall, only the trio’s testimonies were unfavorable to the snake demon husband. However, testimonies of this level couldn’t form a complete chain of evidence for a conviction.

Meng Jingzhou had anticipated the snake demon husband’s reaction. He was always meticulous, so how could he let a mere snake demon find a loophole?

Meng Jingzhou calmly fished out a recording orb. It recorded the entire process from the Innate Daoist Priest summoning them brothers to capturing the snake demon family, leaving the snake demon husband utterly speechless.

With irrefutable evidence, the white-robed demon couldn’t deny anything and had no choice but to obediently accept punishment.

Just as Lu Yang had expected, the authorities invited the Innate Daoist Priest to give a statement as a victim, while Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou gave statements as witnesses.

“Thank you so much.” The city lord shook hands with the trio. The Dao-Seeking Sect disciples are extraordinary. Not only did they help to solve the Wangjia Gully disappearance case, but they also captured two Divine Transfiguration snake demons. This would count toward my performance metrics too.

Considering he couldn’t subdue the snake demon couple alone, the city lord hastily summoned three Divine Transfiguration cultivators from nearby cities while Lu Yang’s trio was giving their statements. Only then could he relax.

Afterward, following Lu Yang’s request, he issued a document of proof stamped with Jinniu City’s official seal, proving the Innate Daoist Priest had completed the mission.

With the mission concluded, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou wanted to take the Innate Daoist Priest back to the Dao-Seeking Sect. However, the Innate Daoist Priest felt that since they had come such a long way, they should buy some local specialties as gifts.

Although Lu Yang felt that no one in the Dao-Seeking Sect would dare accept gifts from the Founding Ancestor, he couldn’t dissuade the Innate Daoist Priest and could only tag along.

~~~

“What do you think of this little golden ox...” Lu Yang pointed at a small golden ox statue in a shop.

But when he turned his head, the Innate Daoist Priest had already disappeared.

“Where is he?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou exchanged a glance.

How did we lose him just from walking?

If we lose the Founding Ancestor, that would be disastrous!

Meng Jingzhou was more optimistic. “We shouldn’t think that way. Since we found the Founding Ancestor, and now we lost him, one merit cancels out one fault. They balance out.”

“...Do you believe that yourself?”

“No.”

“Then spare the nonsense and start searching!”

~~~

The two searched for over an hour and finally found the Innate Daoist Priest eating noodles at a noodle stall.

“How did you end up here eating noodles?” Lu Yang exhaled in relief. I can avoid a beating now.

The Innate Daoist Priest scratched his head, somewhat embarrassed. “I don’t know what happened earlier, but while we were walking, I somehow lost track of you two.” He looked around, gesturing for Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to sit down for some noodles. “I wanted to find a teahouse to rest. While drinking tea, I overheard the neighboring table discussing the Heartless Creed.”

“Heartless Creed?” Lu Yang’s eye twitched. Founding Ancestor, your luck is truly absurd. Even I don’t have intel on the Heartless Creed, yet you just got lost once and found a lead.

The Innate Daoist Priest nodded. “Yes. I overheard the cultivators at the neighboring table say there’s a Heartless Creed base nearby, seeming to be recruiting members. Those cultivators wanted to go there.

“Originally, I wanted to tell you two. But I couldn’t get away to find you, so I chose to tail them instead.”

He pointed at a shop not far away. “Those two are inside.”

It was a tailor shop. Two plainly dressed cultivators emerged—precisely the cultivators who wanted to join the Heartless Creed.

“Follow them.” The Innate Daoist Priest quickly finished his noodles, even drinking the broth. Wiping his mouth, he beckoned Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to follow him.

The two cultivators they were tailing were only at the Foundation Establishment Stage. With Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s help and protection, the Innate Daoist Priest didn’t need to worry about being detected.

“Founding Ancestor, do you intend to follow them all the way to the base? You can just leave this kind of thing to Old Meng and me,” Lu Yang advised.

Scouting diabolic creeds and whatnot? Old Meng and I are extremely familiar with that.

The Innate Daoist Priest shook his head, saying earnestly, “I heard you two once went undercover in the Everlasting Creed for months and ultimately wiped out their main base in one fell swoop, uprooting all their forces. You two are the pride of our Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Lu Yang wanted to say they hadn’t actually uprooted all their forces. After all, the higher-ups are working hard for the barbeque business in our sect.

“Although I founded the Dao-Seeking Sect, I haven’t contributed much to its current achievements. You two have also treated me so well; I feel ashamed.

“I want to learn from you two—go undercover in the Heartless Creed and uproot it!”

Lu Yang had heard of people emulating predecessors and sages, but never heard of people emulating juniors.

“Ah, that’s too dangerous!” Meng Jingzhou was shocked. Founding Ancestor, you really are bold! If anything goes wrong, it wouldn’t be a simple beating waiting for us when we return to the sect.

The Innate Daoist Priest waved his hand, expressing his resolve. “What isn’t dangerous? I have made up my mind. Don’t talk me out of it anymore.”

Seeing the Innate Daoist Priest’s determination, Lu Yang had no option but to agree. With Old Meng and me secretly protecting him, nothing major could go wrong. It’s not like a Heartless Creed higher-up would pop up in this place.

Even if a Heartless Creed higher-up does appear, it won’t be a problem. It’s not like the Dao-Seeking Sect lacks higher-ups.

Thinking about it this way, the Founding Ancestor seems quite safe.

The trio tailed their targets, passing through six cities before they finally arrived at the Heartless Creed base.

1. “Jinniu” translates directly to golden ox. ☜

Chapter 811: The Heartless Creed’s Entrance Trial

The Heartless Creed was said to consist entirely of heartless individuals. Their recruitment criteria were extremely stringent, which was why they had the fewest members among the Four Great Diabolic Creeds.

Of course, in terms of follower count, they still couldn’t compare to the Heavenly Court Creed, which had been established for only two years yet possessed a history of four hundred thousand years.

It was unknown whether the Heartless Creed’s philosophy truly had some merit or if they had other methods, but their members’ cultivation levels were generally high.

Lu Yang recounted the intelligence on the Heartless Creed to the Innate Daoist Priest. “The Heartless Creed’s philosophy is that only those bereft of compassion and righteousness can attain the Great Dao and become a supreme immortal. Worldly relationships are shackles to them. Kinship, love, friendship—these emotions are poison to them and not to be touched. Even if such ties exist, they must be severed as soon as possible.”

The Innate Daoist Priest didn’t know much about the Heartless Creed, just like Lu Yang had only known the name of the Everlasting Creed when he reached the Foundation Establishment Stage.

The Lu Yang today was different. On the surface, he had excellent relations with Dai Bufan, who was in charge of the intelligence network. Behind the scenes, he relied on his status as the young creed leader to gather considerable intelligence from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and the Radiant Sun Creed.

However, the Heartless Creed was inherently insular, treating the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and the Radiant Sun Creeds with indifference. Therefore, these two creeds couldn’t fully understand the Heartless Creed’s situation either.

“Is that the Heartless Creed’s base over there?”

Lu Yang and the others were in a forest. The two they had been tailing knocked on the bark of a certain large tree before getting sucked into the tree, vanishing from sight.

Through his spiritual consciousness, Lu Yang discovered that the tree’s interior was hollow. With its roots as channels, it transported people to an underground cavity beneath the roots.

“That’s the fifth cultivator going underground, right?” Meng Jingzhou transmitted an auditory message to the other two. They weren’t clear about the situation here and were in the middle of observing. Aside from the two cultivators who just entered, three more cultivators individually entered the underground cavity.

“Then it can’t be wrong. It’s the Heartless Creed’s recruitment day today.” The Innate Daoist Priest was certain he hadn’t misheard. “I’ll go down first.”

“Wait, wait.” Lu Yang hurriedly pulled the Innate Daoist Priest back. “We brothers have some experience in this area. How about letting the two of us accompany you down?” He was worried about letting the Innate Daoist Priest go to the Heartless Creed alone.

The Innate Daoist Priest thought it over and felt that Lu Yang’s words made sense. Although my cultivation experience surpasses these two juniors, my infiltration experience can’t compare.

“That works too.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou put on masks, altered their appearances, and suppressed their cultivation to the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage. As long as the Heartless Creed below didn’t have any Divine Transfiguration cultivators, no one would see through their cultivation levels.

Following the steps they had observed previously, the trio knocked on a specific patch on the giant tree’s bark. A suction force pulled them into the tree, and they slid down to the underground cavity.

~~~

“Oh, more people, and three of them at that?” The Heartless Creed member who saw Lu Yang’s trio was puzzled. Typically, heartless people rarely traveled in groups—two together was already rare, and three together was even rarer. But it wasn’t unheard of, so he didn’t suspect much.

“Come with me,” the Heartless Creed member guarding the entrance said expressionlessly.

From the corner of his eye, Lu Yang surveyed this underground cavity, which looked like a large restaurant that had been buried in the earth. He wondered how long this base had been built.

This area belonged to Ye City, so this base should be called the Heartless Creed’s Ye City Branch.

The Heartless Creed follower leading the way was nearly at the Golden Core Stage. Along the way, several other Heartless Creed followers were patrolling, all at the Golden Core Stage.

The follower led the trio to the deepest part of the cavity. At this point, seven other cultivators had already arrived, wanting to join the Heartless Creed. Their cultivation levels varied—the highest was at the Golden Core Stage, while the lowest was only at the Level Three Qi Training Stage. However, judging by the Heartless Creed’s reaction, they didn’t place much importance on cultivation level.

“Three Basic Foundation Establishment cultivators? Got it. You may leave.” The cultivator responsible for selecting new followers nodded, his expression cold. His eyes were like those of a dead fish, looking at everyone as if they were corpses.

Lu Yang noted that he had the highest cultivation here, at the Intermediate Nascent Soul Stage.

“How did you all find this place?” this Intermediate Nascent Soul cultivator asked.

Lu Yang replied in a similar tone. “We tailed certain people here. The three of us have long wanted to join the Heartless Creed. Now that we finally found an opportunity, we decided to come.” Regarding how we found the place, there’s no need to lie. If anything, tailing others here has more of a diabolic cultivator flair.

The Intermediate Nascent Soul cultivator didn’t respond to Lu Yang’s answer, but based on the fact that he didn’t chase them away, he likely didn’t suspect them. Or perhaps, he didn’t need to suspect them at all. He only believed in the test results.

After Lu Yang’s group arrived, they waited another four hours. Seeing no new cultivators came to join the Heartless Creed, the Intermediate Nascent Soul cultivator announced frostily, “Alright, enough waiting. Even if more people come, they have no fate with our creed. My name is Niu Qianshan, the Branch Leader of this branch. The purpose for which you have all gathered here goes without saying—it’s to join our Heartless Creed.

“Our creed doesn’t care about your backgrounds or your cultivation levels. As long as you can be bereft of compassion and righteousness and uphold the Heartless Dao, you are all members of our creed.”

Niu Qianshan took out a stack of yellow papers, drawn with arrays that Lu Yang couldn’t understand. He gestured for his subordinates to distribute the yellow papers to all the cultivators.

“Hmm? What an ingenious array. Whoever designed this is a talent.” A rare compliment came from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

Niu Qianshan continued, “Our creed’s entrance trial isn’t as fussy as the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s or the Radiant Sun Creed’s. Our creed’s trial only has one component to it—prove that you are individuals bereft of compassion and righteousness!

“What you need to do next is sit in meditation on this yellow paper.

“Once you’re in meditation, the array on the yellow paper can peer into your hearts and identify the person closest to you in the deepest part of your heart—be it your parents, elders, or friends—and manifest them.

“Moreover, you will forget your circumstances, forget this is a test, and believe it is reality. You must kill the person you see!”

At the end, Niu Qianshan’s visage turned deranged and fearsome, his entire expression twisted. To join the Heartless Creed, he had personally killed his wife and child.

“Of course, considering the other party’s cultivation might exceed yours, making it hard to kill them, the person manifested by the array will have cultivation equal to yours.

“The trial begins!” Niu Qianshan announced coldly.

The ten test-takers, including Lu Yang, sat in meditation on the arrays. They were all heartless individuals with steadfast Dao hearts and quickly entered meditation.

~~~

When Lu Yang woke again, his mind felt muddled, as if he had forgotten something. Soon, he regained clarity with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s help.

“I remember now. I’m currently participating in the Heartless Creed’s trial. I need to kill the person who appears in the illusion. Since I’m already awake, passing the trial shouldn’t be difficult...”

Before Lu Yang finished speaking, he saw two familiar, graceful figures approaching. One was Yun Zhi, and the other was Huang Doudou.

Lu Yang, “...”

If I could win this fight, it would be a damned miracle!

Chapter 812: Joining the Heartless Creed

When Lu Yang saw these two individuals, he was so terrified that he began to tremble uncontrollably, feeling like his heart had stopped beating.

What’s wrong with your Heartless Creed? If you don’t want me to join, you could just say so directly. There’s no need to go to such lengths.

And “suppressed to the same cultivation realm?” Why don’t you suppress Big Senior Sister’s cultivation to the Golden Core Stage and let me witness what a sky full of golden cores is like?

Lu Yang could even sense the Unbeatable Nascent Soul growing restless...restless with the urge to flee.

If he had to deal with just one of them, Lu Yang felt that it might be worth fighting, though victory or defeat was a separate matter.

However, if he had to face both, Lu Yang felt that he could compete with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul to see who could flee faster.

“Little Junior Brother, what’s wrong?” Big Senior Sister asked with a slight frown, her tone the same as usual.

It was only then that Lu Yang noticed this wasn’t an empty, white space, but at Heaven’s Gate Peak of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Right. For a complete simulation, the environment naturally has to be replicated as well.

“N-nothing.”
