“Second-in-Command, why do you look so dazed? Did cultivation fry your brains?” As always, Huang Doudou was giggling and poking Lu Yang’s cheeks.

“...Immortal Fairy, I don’t think you’re in any position to say that about me.”

“Hmm? I get to challenge Lass Yun again?” The real Everlasting Immortal Fairy darted out of his mental space.

Beating a fake one still counts as a win.

She directly possessed the illusory Huang Doudou and self-detonated right away.

“Holy crap! Immortal Fairy, wait—”

Before Lu Yang could dissuade her, he saw the Everlasting Immortal Fairy self-detonate without a word.

Boom!

In the real world, the array couldn’t withstand such power and exploded outright.

Niu Qianshan raised an eyebrow. “Failed so quickly?”

The array exploding signified a failed challenge. Furthermore, with how fast it had exploded, it could only mean the “killing” had failed, and the challenger had instead been “killed.”

For a heartless person to kill the person closest to them, it was akin to an assassination. If even an assassination failed, it was clear the person had wavered, moved by compassion during the act.

“It looks like this kid is not suited for our Heartless Dao.”

~~~

Halfway through her flight, Yun Zhi’s brow furrowed slightly. “I can’t detect it anymore?”

She had sensed an image of herself appearing somewhere and was flying over to investigate. But now, halfway there, it seemed that image had dissipated, and she could no longer detect its source.

“Strange.”

~~~

Lu Yang woke up groggily, his mind still yet to recover from the aftermath of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s self-detonation.

Niu Qianshan walked up to Lu Yang and stated coldly, “You have failed. Return to wherever you came from.”

Before Lu Yang could say anything, he heard an explosion from Meng Jingzhou’s direction. His array had also shattered.

Meng Jingzhou cursed loudly, so incensed that he wanted to tear the entire base apart. “Who the hell could kill that?!”

Niu Qianshan watched Meng Jingzhou icily. Not only has he failed, but he’s also enraged—an emotion a Heartless Creed member should not possess.

“You are also not suited for our Heartless Dao. Both of you, leave.”

Those who walked different paths couldn’t make plans together; keeping them here was pointless. The Heartless Creed did not believe in making exceptions or granting special admissions.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou communicated through auditory messages.

“What do we do?”

“Leave for now. Even if we don’t leave willingly, this Niu Qianshan will probably throw us out. That seems to be the personality type in the Heartless Creed.”

“Alright.”

Watching Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou depart, Niu Qianshan summoned a subordinate at the Advanced Golden Core Stage.

“These two know the location of our base. They cannot be left alive. Go and get rid of them both; be quick and clean.”

Although Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou displayed cultivation at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage outwardly, Niu Qianshan was always prudent. He would send the most capable person available. If not for the vice branch leader being occupied, he would have had the vice branch leader, a Basic Nascent Soul cultivator, handle it.

~~~

While leaving the Ye City Branch, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou continued to discuss the earlier trial.

“What made you take action inside the array?” Lu Yang asked curiously. With the Immortal Fairy’s help, I could regain clarity within the array and understood that killing a close person was the key to passing. Old Meng hadn’t regained clarity, so why would he attack someone close to him?

Meng Jingzhou’s face darkened. “The one who appeared in the array was you, you grandson. I simply wanted to spar with you.”

Lu Yang perked up with interest. “Oh? So, since you lost in the array, you should admit I’m stronger than you, right?”

At the mention of this topic, Meng Jingzhou’s face grew darker. “In the array, you immediately used the Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist! How the hell was I supposed to fight that?”

The array couldn’t possibly simulate Yun Zhi stepping in, but the Animal Form Fist inherently possessed the ability to borrow a trace of power from its prototype. It was just that Lu Yang seldom used it that way.

The Lu Yang in the array borrowed a sliver of power from Yun Zhi, so Meng Jingzhou naturally found him unbeatable.

“Someone’s been following us.”

“I know. The Heartless Creed probably sent someone to kill us.”

“That works out perfectly. We can disguise ourselves as him and continue infiltrating the Heartless Creed.”

The two of them acted simultaneously, capturing the Heartless Creed member before he even had a chance to react.

“You guys are not at the Foundation Establishment Stage!” the man said coldly.

Without a word, Lu Yang stepped forward and slapped him. “Too much chatter. Stay put obediently.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou dragged the man to a hidden spot. Lu Yang wanted to check on how the Innate Daoist Priest was faring below.

He saw the Innate Daoist Priest still sitting in meditation on the array. Judging by his relaxed expression, he was likely immersed in it, unable to see through the array’s illusion.

“Given the Founding Ancestor’s temperament, if he doesn’t see through the array’s illusion, he’ll never pass the trial.

“Immortal Fairy, could I trouble you to intervene?”

After all, this is the Founding Ancestor’s wish. Lu Yang naturally wanted to fulfill it to the best of his ability.

“Hmph, you still have to count on this immortal, don’t you?” Since it was Lu Yang’s request, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t mind lending a small hand.

Activating a faint trace of immortal power, she made the Innate Daoist Priest wake up from the array.

~~~

At the moment, the Innate Daoist Priest was in the bamboo forest in the Dao-Seeking Sect, engaged in a pleasant conversation with the River Spirit, Little Green.

If one had to identify the closest person to him, it would naturally be Little Green, who also hailed from the Great Yu era.

Suddenly, he paused, remembering this was a trial. The Little Green before me is fake.

He sighed softly. Even if this was an illusion, he was unwilling to raise a hand against Little Green. However, he also knew that if he didn’t kill this fake Little Green, he wouldn’t be able to join the Heartless Creed.

Little Lu and Little Meng have eradicated a diabolic creed. As their senior, I can’t afford to hold them back.

Then kill I shall!

Catching the River Spirit Little Green off guard, who was also at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage, the Innate Daoist Priest killed her.

The Innate Daoist Priest woke up to see Niu Qianshan standing before him.

Niu Qianshan patted the Innate Daoist Priest on the shoulder. “Not bad. You passed the trial so quickly. It shows that you are suited for Heartless Dao. From today, you are one of us.”

~~~

Lu Yang, who had been observing with his spiritual consciousness, exhaled in relief. This way, the Founding Ancestor has successfully infiltrated the Heartless Creed.

Just as he was about to turn and say a few words to Meng Jingzhou, he saw a group of people flying from the distance, approaching with fierce and imposing momentum. They directly uprooted the great tree that concealed the base and swarmed into the underground cavity.

Their leader announced his identity. “Nobody move! Get down on the ground, hands on your heads! I am the Chief Constable of Ye City. You are all under arrest!”

The chief constable’s gaze fell upon the Innate Daoist Priest. “New recruit? You’re under arrest too!”

~~~

Heaven’s Gate Peak.

Yun Zhi had her eyes closed, comprehending the Great Dao of heaven and earth.

Suddenly, she sensed two figures rushing toward her.

“Little Junior Brother, Junior Brother Meng, what happened?”

Lu Yang was so out of breath he could barely speak. “B-Big Senior Sister, it’s terrible! The Founding Ancestor...he joined the Heartless Creed...so he has been arrested by the authorities.”

Yun Zhi, “...”

Little Junior Brother, do you hear what you’re saying?

Chapter 813: Who in the Dao-Seeking Sect Doesn’t Go to Prison?

Yun Zhi vaguely recalled that she had been worried about the Innate Daoist Priest encountering some mishap while completing his mission outside. This was why I had specifically asked my clever Little Junior Brother and Junior Brother Meng to assist him in secret.

Three days passed in the blink of an eye. How is it that you two returned safe and sound, while the Founding Ancestor ended up behind bars?

“What happened?”

The two scratched their heads. This matter really isn’t easy to explain.

Lu Yang tried to summarize the situation as concisely as possible. “Here’s what happened. The Innate Daoist Priest had successfully completed his mission. However, on the way back, he coincidentally came across a lead on the Heartless Creed. They were conducting their entrance trials at the time, so he wanted to go undercover in the Heartless Creed and emulate us in wiping out a diabolic creed.

“We were worried about the Founding Ancestor’s safety, so we also went to participate in the trial. The test required killing the person closest to you in an illusion. Both Old Meng and I failed; only the Founding Ancestor succeeded.”

A rare flicker of curiosity arose in Yun Zhi, and she temporarily set aside the matter of the Innate Daoist Priest’s predicament. “Little Junior Brother, who did you encounter in the illusion?”

Meng Jingzhou was also curious about this. Lu Yang was eliminated even earlier than I was. Exactly what kind of enemy—or rather, person closest to him—did he face?

“Wel, it was...you know...that person...”

“Which person?”

Lu Yang hemmed and hawed, too embarrassed to say it in front of the person in question.

“What’s there to ask? Who else could it be but this immortal?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy emerged from his body, boasting to Yun Zhi with a smug expression. “Our Everlasting Lineage is united as one!”

Yun Zhi showed no reaction. “Oh. Little Junior Brother, please continue.”

“Right after the Founding Ancestor passed the trial and joined the Heartless Creed, the authorities raided the creed’s base. They arrested all the Heartless Creed followers, including the Founding Ancestor, who had just joined. Seeing the situation turn dire, we hurried back to the sect to report.”

“Wait, how did the Founding Ancestor pass the trial?” Yun Zhi spotted a logical inconsistency. Although I haven’t interacted much with the Founding Ancestor, I know that he is a deeply compassionate and righteous person. How could he have passed the Heartless Creed’s trial?

Lu Yang didn’t dare to bring himself to meet Yun Zhi’s gaze. “Um, well, I saw that the Founding Ancestor really wanted to join the Heartless Creed. Big Senior Sister, you know I’m a filial disciple; I try to fulfil the wishes of elders as much as possible. Thus, I asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to help break the Founding Ancestor’s perceptual barriers, allowing him to realize it was an illusion.”

Yun Zhi looked at Lu Yang, who guiltily lowered his head. Then she looked at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who wasn’t afraid of Yun Zhi and spoke with conviction. “The Second-in-Command asked for my help. How could I refuse?”

Yun Zhi sighed and continued questioning. “Then didn’t the Founding Ancestor reveal that he was from our Dao-Seeking Sect and explain that he was going undercover in the diabolic creed?” Surely, the authorities wouldn’t arrest a spy.

In fact, upon seeing the Innate Daoist Priest arrested, Lu Yang had immediately transmitted an auditory message to him, urging him to explain the circumstances.

“No, he didn’t. He felt that it was too shameful and was embarrassed to admit he was from the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Lu Yang felt that entering prison as a Dao-Seeking Sect member wasn’t a big deal, considering that his shifu, the Taciturn Daoist Priest, had entered and exited prison multiple times with ease, setting multiple historical records within Great Xia’s prison cells. Shifu doesn’t wear it as a badge of shame, but of honor. He even authors books about his experiences, becoming a legendary figure in Great Xia’s prison cells.

But the Innate Daoist Priest couldn’t overcome this psychological hurdle.

Yun Zhi was placed in a difficult spot. I can naturally explain the situation to the local authorities and have them release the Founding Ancestor. However, judging by the Founding Ancestor’s current state, he is unwilling to reveal that he’s from the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Junior Brother Dai often handles matters of this nature. Go ask him if he has any good solutions.”

“Yes.”

~~~

Following Yun Zhi’s orders, the two jogged all the way to the Great Mission Hall to find Dai Bufan.

Seeing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, Dai Bufan was momentarily taken aback. “Shouldn’t you two be protecting the Founding Ancestor? What are you doing here?”

Since advancing to the Intermediate Fusion Stage, his mental state had undergone a transformation, making it hard for external events to shake him. Even seeing Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou no longer evoked the previous feeling of encountering the black and white Heibai Wuchang (Black and White Impermanence envoys)[1] coming for his soul.

Meng Jingzhou said seriously, “The court authorities have mobilized forces to protect the Founding Ancestor. He is currently extremely safe and does not require our protection for the time being. It’s Big Senior Sister who sent us to seek your counsel for a solution.”

“Oh? What trouble have you encountered?” Dai Bufan grew interested. I didn’t expect there to be something Big Senior Sister can’t resolve; to think she needs my wisdom.

“The Founding Ancestor wanted to join the Heartless Creed, and then he got arrested by the authorities.”

Dai Bufan coughed violently, nearly hacking up a lung. “You...you two, explain the whole sequence of events in detail.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou recounted most of the events faithfully, omitting the parts involving the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Oh, so it was just going there as a spy. You almost scared me to death.” Dai Bufan breathed a sigh of relief. I knew the Founding Ancestor couldn’t possibly have such poor eyesight and judgment to forsake the Dao-Seeking Sect for some Heartless Creed.

“Wait, going undercover is also dangerous! Is this how you two should be protecting the Founding Ancestor?!”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou nodded. Indeed, it is dangerous. I mean, didn’t he get arrested?

“How long will the Founding Ancestor be imprisoned?” This was Dai Bufan’s primary concern.

“The authorities said that since the Founding Ancestor had just joined the Heartless Creed, had no prior criminal record, and demonstrated sincere remorse, fifteen days of detention would suffice.”

“Thank goodness it’s only fifteen days,” Dai Bufan remarked. If it were over two months, I would have to find a way to rescue the Founding Ancestor no matter what. “In that case, either you two visit him in prison frequently, or get yourselves imprisoned alongside him. Just ensure the Founding Ancestor doesn’t suffer any grievances in his cell.”

Without exposing the Innate Daoist Priest’s identity, the only way Dai Bufan could think of to get him out was to have him impersonate a member of one of the four other immortal sects, claiming he had gone in as a spy. But this method is somewhat underhanded.

Besides, how is it proper to have the Founding Ancestor impersonate someone from another sect?

Fifteen days is neither long nor short. We could simply treat it as the Founding Ancestor gaining some experience in the mundane world.

“Understood.”

~~~

“Which option should we choose? Frequent prison visits, or accompanying the Founding Ancestor in prison?”

“I’m more inclined to the second option. It allows us to take care of him more comprehensively.”

“How about we first visit the Founding Ancestor in prison to check on his condition before deciding?”

“That works too.”

After discussing their plan, they rushed from the Dao-Seeking Sect to Ye City’s prison, carrying two large meal boxes.

“He should be around here.”

Ye City had many prison cells. Using spiritual consciousness here was inconvenient and could easily arouse suspicion, so the two searched the cells one by one.

Lu Yang overheard a conversation between two people not far away.

“Founding Ancestor, I never expected you to come here and keep me company.” The speaker’s tone was filled with complex emotions and tinged with a hint of joy.

“Neither did I expect that. As the sect leader, you didn’t evade your responsibility after making a mistake. Instead, you voluntarily allowed yourself to be imprisoned here. You are truly an exemplary role model for our sect.”

Lu Yang saw the Innate Daoist Priest imprisoned together with his shifu. Next to them was Chieftain Jin.

He fell into a long silence.

How did these three end up together?

1. Heibai Wuchang are two underworld deities in charge of escorting the souls of the dead to the underworld. Bai Wuchang is dressed in white (bai) and is tall and thin, with a tongue sticking out. Hei Wuchang is dressed in black (hei) and is short and plump. ☜

Chapter 814: The Omnipresent Taciturn Daoist Priest

“Little Lu, Meng boy, over here, over here.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest beckoned them over. He had heard Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s footsteps long ago.

“Shifu, why are you here?” Lu Yang’s eyelid twitched. How should I put it? I’m not at all surprised to encounter Shifu in a prison cell.

Although his great shifu had altered his appearance, Lu Yang recognized him at a glance.

“And Chieftain Jin, you...”

On the other hand, Chieftain Jin hadn’t changed his appearance.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were unaware that after the Demon Kingdom’s founding ceremony, Chieftain Jin had acknowledged the Taciturn Daoist Priest as his big brother to hone his eloquence.

Lu Yang still remembered Chieftain Jin’s high spirits when they met in the Qiongqi Tribe, maintaining his composure in the face of Supreme Lord Zhu Tian’s oppressive pressure. How had he sunk to the same level as Shifu in the blink of an eye?

The speed of this downfall is too alarming.

“I’m here to learn from Big Brother Taciturn.” Chieftain Jin tittered, somewhat abashed about meeting acquaintances in such a place for the first time.

Lu Yang genuinely couldn’t think of what there was to learn from his shifu.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest laughed heartily, feeling not the least bit embarrassed. “Aiya, I was teaching Little Jin the principle that those who deceive will eventually be captured in the net. To help him adapt to prison life in advance and learn how to live comfortably in a prison cell, I deliberately left a small flaw, allowing the Ye City authorities to arrest both me and Little Jin.”

He patted Chieftain Jin on the shoulder, imparting precious knowledge. “Be more confident! In our line of work, the most important thing is self-assurance. Your appearance stems from your mind and heart. With inner confidence, your face will glow, and only then will the other party believe your lies!”

Lu Yang facepalmed. Why wasn’t Shifu this earnest when teaching me... Oh, right, there’s no need to teach me such things.

“Who would have thought there would be an unexpected bonus, running into the Founding Ancestor? I heard the Founding Ancestor was arrested because he wanted to go undercover in the Heartless Creed?”

Lu Yang nodded, recounting what he had previously found out. “The Ye City’s yamen received intelligence about the Heartless Creed’s base and coordinated with several nearby cities to raid that base. The Founding Ancestor was consequently captured.”

“So that’s what happened.”

“We bought some dishes from the Blessed Fortune Restaurant. I’m not sure if they suit your taste, Founding Ancestor.”

Meng Jingzhou opened the two large meal boxes, and a fragrant aroma wafted out. Although the Innate Daoist Priest had long passed the stage of craving gustatory pleasures, his current body was at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage and reacted instinctively.

“So fragrant.” The Innate Daoist Priest’s nose twitched as he accepted the chopsticks and began digging in.

“What about my chopsticks?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest pointed at himself. As secular cultivators, we don’t adhere to concepts like grain abstinence; savoring delicious food is the true Dao for us.

“There’s only one pair of chopsticks,” Meng Jingzhou replied. Sect Leader, how was I supposed to know that you were also imprisoned here?

Of course, even if he had known the Taciturn Daoist Priest was here, he wouldn’t have brought extra chopsticks.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest had no choice but to use his spirit energy to materialize a pair of chopsticks to pick up the food and eat.

The Ye City prison contained arrays that restricted cultivation and spirit energy. Even for Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, using spirit energy here was immensely difficult, akin to being mired in a swamp.

Ye City was considered a major city. Its city lord was at the Void Refinement Stage, and the arrays were also at the Void Refinement level. However, Void Refinement-level arrays were nothing before the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

As a Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, the arrays of a mere local prison couldn’t possibly restrain him. He could employ spells at will. Not to mention, even Chieftain Jin, a Fusion cultivator, could freely cast spells.

Considering that revealing his true identity might attract a group of old friends to come and gawk at him, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had used a false identity when entering the prison, posing as a Foundation Establishment cultivator.

The same went for Chieftain Jin.

“Speaking of which, it’s fortunate the Founding Ancestor didn’t join the Heartless Creed. I spent some time there myself in the past. That was truly no place for normal folk.” Not even eating could shut the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s mouth. “Back then, I came across the Heartless Creed’s recruitment. There was no time to inform others, so I said I’d test the waters first and ended up joining them.”

“Ah?” No one expected the Taciturn Daoist Priest to have such a past.

“Isn’t the Heartless Creed’s trial about killing the person closest to you? How did you pass the trial?”

“Simple. The person closest to me is myself. I encountered another me with identical strength in the array. Since the array makes you forget your circumstances, I thought I had accidentally stumbled into some secret domain where I had to defeat myself to pass. Then, I broke through on the spot and eliminated myself.

“After passing the trial, the Heartless Creed would investigate who the person closest to you, as manifested in the array, was. You would need to kill that person in reality to truly become a member.

“They discovered the closest person to me was myself, but they couldn’t possibly ask me to commit suicide, so they let me pass.

“After I joined the Heartless Creed, I realized the Heartless Creed was researching the Heartless Dao. To study it, they would marry, attempt to walk the Heartful Dao, then kill their wives to prove their Dao, thereby strengthening the heartlessness in their hearts.

“I thought this wouldn’t do. If the Heartless Dao continued this way, how many innocent women would suffer?

“Therefore, at the time, I suggested to the Heartless Creed’s higher-ups that the way of killing one’s wife to prove their Dao was incorrect. Does killing your wife truly prove you are a heartless person? What if you killed your wife in a moment of impulse and regretted it later?

“The Heartless Creed’s higher-ups thought my words held some merit and asked me if I had better ideas.

“I said that one must be long-sighted to prove the Heartless Dao. You can’t just keep killing. Once you’ve killed all those close to you, how will you continue to prove your Heartless Dao later?’

“I proposed that instead of falling in love with your wife and then killing her, it would be better to fall in love with your wife and then let her sleep with someone else.

“Common sense dictates that letting your wife sleep with another person would evoke either rage or agitation. However, neither of these is an emotion a Heartless Creed member should display.

“Furthermore, witnessing your wife sleep with someone else would maximize feelings of rage or agitation. Hence, I further recommended that Heartless Creed followers observe the whole process of themselves being cuckolded from the sidelines.

“Having your wife cuckold you but still showing no reaction—that is the mark of a qualified Heartless Creed follower!

“The Heartless Creed higher-ups felt that my words made some sense and widely promoted it within the Heartless Creed.

“My theory also exposed many followers who couldn’t achieve heartlessness. Those who wanted to defect were all executed.

“It was also good that they died. After all, these people had blood on their hands when they joined. They deserved to die.

“Later, I discovered that the Heartless Creed’s fundamental doctrine wasn’t heartless but using any means necessary to become stronger.

“Moreover, the Heartless Creed had a strict internal promotion system. You could say that every radish had a hole—there was only one position per person. Each promotion significantly increased the resources one could obtain. It’s similar to the system of outer and inner disciples in other sects.

“At the time, I told them that since having people above prevented those below from being promoted, if we got rid of those above, wouldn’t there be a chance to rise?

“They thought I had a point, so they secretly killed several superiors, successfully climbing the ranks.

“Other branches noticed this and followed suit. The Heartless Creed was quite chaotic during that period.”

Chapter 815: Three Generations Gathered in Prison

“After the Heartless Creed was thrown into chaos, the higher-ups killed many people to suppress the situation.

“Normally, slaughtering a chicken to scare the monkeys would suffice—killing a few to warn the others, but that wouldn’t work in the Heartless Creed. Heartless people have no fear; they only see profit. Killing a few doesn’t serve as a deterrent. The higher-ups must kill a large number of people and show their resolve to those below, forcing them to weigh the pros and cons. Only then would these people below understand the predicament they were in and back down.”

Recalling that scene from his youth, the Taciturn Daoist Priest clicked his tongue in wonder. It was his first time seeing killing carried out so cleanly and efficiently.

“However, the situation wasn’t quickly suppressed. The Heartless Creed’s higher-ups also had their own hierarchy. Influenced by those below, they began infighting too. I heard the creed leader suffered more than one assassination attempt.

“After the internal strife was quelled, the Heartless Creed started settling old scores. They traced the source to me and prepared to execute me. I suspect there was also dissatisfaction with my improved version of killing the wife to prove one’s Dao.

“Fortunately, I was at the Divine Transfiguration Stage then and had a life-preserving magical treasure from my shifu. That’s how I narrowly escaped from the Heartless Creed.

“What a pity. I was planning to remain undercover in the Heartless Creed, investigate their headquarters, and dig up their deepest secrets. Who would have thought the Heartless Creed would be so impatient, insisting on killing me? My every action clearly conformed to the tenets of their creed.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest shook his head. Given my understanding of the Heartless Dao, the Heartless Creed should have made me their creed leader.

“Although I didn’t uncover their deepest secrets, I found out the Heartless Creed has two vice creed leaders and one creed leader. The creed leader’s cultivation is unknown. The two vice creed leaders are respectively at the Basic and Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation Stage.”

Lu Yang drew a sharp breath. The Radiant Sun Creed and the Nine-Netherworlds Creed weren’t even aware of this intelligence. Furthermore, the intelligence signified that the Heartless Creed had at least three Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, stronger than these two creeds.

“What happened afterward?” The Innate Daoist Priest had been listening intently and pressed eagerly.

“Afterward, I ran away.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest curled his lip. “I saw they couldn’t handle the game, so I stopped pretending. I directly contacted my sect and Great Xia and raided all the Heartless Creeds I knew about, killing those who deserved to be killed and saving those who deserved to be saved.

“First an internal strife, then eradication by the righteous path—under these two successive blows, the Heartless Creed was severely weakened, and they lay low for a few centuries.”

“Didn’t the Heartless Creed take revenge on you after that?” Lu Yang asked.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest pointed out the error in Lu Yang’s thinking. “They have no ‘hatred.’ Why would they take revenge on me?

“But you’re right, many did want to take revenge on me. Using hatred to prove one’s Dao is also a path of the Heartless Dao. Among them was someone called Su Moran, who harbored the most hatred toward me. He was the vice creed leader and at the Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation Stage. I reckon it’s because I sabotaged him pretty badly then.

“That said, Su Moran wasn’t too willing to let people know he wanted to take revenge on me.”

“Why’s that?”

“Because wanting to take revenge on me meant that he harbored hatred toward me, temporarily deviating from the Heartless Dao. And temporarily deviating from the Heartless Dao implied that his cultivation had hit a bottleneck. And hitting a bottleneck would suggest that his cultivation had stalled, lowering his standing and appraisal within the Heartless Creed.”

“The Heartless Creed is that dangerous?” The Innate Daoist Priest felt a wave of lingering fear. Thank goodness I got caught. If I’d entered the Heartless Creed, I’d probably have been exposed within days.

“Founding Ancestor, it’s fortunate that you didn’t join the Heartless Creed.” Chieftain Jin was worried on the Innate Daoist Priest’s behalf.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest shot Chieftain Jin a glance. “Shoo shoo. You’re not from our Dao-Seeking Sect. Who are you calling the Founding Ancestor?”

“Don’t say that, Big Brother. I think our Qiongqi Tribe and your Dao-Seeking Sect may have potential for cooperation. If our two families join forces in the future, wouldn’t contending for a position in the top ten during the Battle of the Great Era be a walk in the park?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest thought of his excellent disciple, Yun Zhi. I don’t think our Dao-Seeking Sect needs to team up with your Qiongqi Tribe to rank among the top ten.

Originally, Lu Yang thought the Innate Daoist Priest would be quite safe in prison; he and Meng Jingzhou could just visit frequently. However, now that he discovered the Innate Daoist Priest was imprisoned with the Taciturn Daoist Priest, he grew uneasy.

Lu Yang discussed with Meng Jingzhou through an auditory message. “How about we go to prison to protect the Founding Ancestor?”

“Do we have to go that far? Although the Founding Ancestor looks young and inexperienced, he’s still a former Fusion expert who dispersed his cultivation to cultivate anew. Having tempered his Dao heart over a long period, he shouldn’t be so easily influenced by the Sect Leader.” Meng Jingzhou felt that Lu Yang might be overestimating the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s influence.

Before Lu Yang could speak, he heard the Taciturn Daoist Priest teaching the Innate Daoist Priest.

“Founding Ancestor, you may not be aware, but our Dao-Seeking Sect has a tradition of residing in prisons. Do you know that in the mortal world, there’s a profession where people go to inns daily to sleep, test the accommodation environment, and suggest improvements?

“Our Dao-Seeking Sect has a similar profession. Look at me, I wander the streets all year round and get imprisoned in various cities just so that I can investigate the prison conditions. This task isn’t suitable for the authorities. When the superiors come for inspection, the subordinates will temporarily improve prison conditions. What could be inspected then? This is why I’m needed.

“And it’s not just me. Two years ago, the Minister of Justice also got imprisoned with me to inspect the prison conditions. This isn’t something I made up. Go inquire in the imperial city; everyone knows about it. Even His Majesty often mentions it in court as a positive anecdote.”

“So that’s how it is.” Initially, when the Innate Daoist Priest heard Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou mention that Dao-Seeking Sect disciples often entered prison, he hadn’t quite believed it. After the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s explanation, realization dawned upon him, and his sense of guilt about being in prison somewhat lessened.

Meng Jingzhou felt that letting the Innate Daoist Priest stay with the Taciturn Daoist Priest was indeed dangerous.

“Let’s just move in together.”

“What crime should we commit?”

There was an art to getting imprisoned. The Innate Daoist Priest would only be locked up for half a month. If the two committed a minor offense, they might not be detained. If they committed a serious offense, getting locked up for two or three months would be costly.

“How about we steal something? That’s simplest,” Lu Yang proposed seriously.

~~~

At the City Lord Estate, the city lord looked at the two plaintiffs below with a conflicted expression.

“You are saying you’re Lu Yang, and that you stole two thousand nine hundred spirit stones from Meng Jingzhou, refusing to return them?”

The city lord then shifted his gaze to the other person.

“You are saying you’re Meng Jingzhou, and that you also stole two thousand nine hundred spirit stones from Lu Yang, refusing to return them?”

The two nodded earnestly.

They had done their homework. In this region, the criminal threshold for theft for Nascent Soul cultivators was three thousand spirit stones. If the sum was below that, it could only be handled as an administrative case, and the maximum penalty for administrative cases was fifteen days of detention.

They would steal from each other, refuse to return the items, and refuse reconciliation. The city lord could then only apply the maximum penalty, detaining them for fifteen days.

Treating it as if nothing happened by offsetting the two thefts also wouldn’t work because cases were independent and couldn’t be combined to be handled as a single case.

The city lord hissed. I’ve long heard that Dao-Seeking Sect disciples like to comprehend the Dao in prison. Could the rumor be true?

Chapter 816: The Formidable Chieftain Jin

“Founding Ancestor, we’ve come to visit you.” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou smiled, looking at the Innate Daoist Priest sitting cross-legged on the floor.

The light from the oil lamp cast their shadows long, making them appear exceptionally tall.

The Innate Daoist Priest was stupefied as he saw Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou entering with bedclothes.

Didn’t we bid goodbye just an hour ago? How did you manage to get into the same cell as me so quickly?

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was deeply moved. I didn’t expect my dear disciple to be so concerned about my prison life, specifically coming to live with me.

“This place is actually quite suitable for you two to cultivate,” the Taciturn Daoist Priest said seriously.

The prison arrays could restrict spirit energy, but Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had exceedingly high cultivation with extremely solid foundations, so they couldn’t be completely restrained. Cultivating here was similar to martial artists training with weights. If they could adapt to the environment here, it would greatly benefit their future cultivation.

“There’s such a good thing?” Lu Yang was delighted. Good things indeed happen to good people.

“Your shifu isn’t wrong about this,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked.

At the moment, Lu Yang’s mental space underwent a major transformation. A row of thick pillars divided it in two. Lu Yang was on one side, while the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was on the other side.

As the First-in-Command, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was rather loyal, sticking by the principle of sharing hardships. She had also imprisoned herself, donning old, tattered prison clothes, and endured the suffering alongside Lu Yang.

“...Wait, Immortal Fairy, isn’t your living environment a bit too good?”

Lu Yang looked at his side—he had straw on the ground, tattered clothes as a pillow, manacles on his hands and legs.

In contrast, on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s side, she had an expensive, soft bed, a wardrobe displaying clothes, a tea table, chairs, and a teapot. Hanging on the wall was a painting drawn by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, depicting a chicken pecking at insects on the ground. This was the Dragon-Phoenix Contention Painting.

Combined with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s prison attire, she looked like a prisoner with special privileges who had come to the prison to enjoy life.

On the other hand, Lu Yang looked like a nobody, the type bullied by the jailer.

“This immortal has a delicate body. How could I sleep on straw? Shoo shoo, go cultivate. I even deliberately suppressed your spiritual consciousness so that when you cultivate, you can train your spiritual consciousness simultaneously.”

After putting on the manacles, Lu Yang did feel that he couldn’t employ his spiritual consciousness with as much ease as before.

In the real world, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou sat in the lotus position and followed the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s instructions to meditate and cultivate.

At the same time, to temper their Dao hearts, the Taciturn Daoist Priest continuously disturbed their cultivation by talking with the Innate Daoist Priest.

Fortunately, the two had high cultivation and entered meditation quickly, unaffected by the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s interference.

~~~

In the blink of an eye, five days passed.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou could feel a slight improvement in their cultivation. Moreover, they believed that without the array’s suppression, their control over spirit energy could reach a new level.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest watched as the two opened their mouths wide and swallowed spirit energy from heaven and hearth, finding it novel.

“So this is the legendary Taotie Tribe’s life-bound divine ability, Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth? This is much more efficient than Spirit-Energy Gathering Arrays. Furthermore, it allows one to cultivate anytime, anywhere.”

Chieftain Jin’s expression turned odd. Is this how the Taotie Tribe’s Swallowing Heaven Devouring Earth is supposed to be like? Why does it seem different from the version I’d seen?

Just as the Taciturn Daoist Priest wanted to chat a bit more with the Innate Daoist Priest, his expression suddenly changed.

With a boom, the ceiling of the prison cell was lifted like opening the lid of a box. The prisoners inside looked up at the pitch-black sky and the figure in the curtain of the night, who was radiating a terrifying aura.

“Oh no, an enemy attack!” The jailer shouted, his face shifting dramatically. He was fully alert and held a halberd, flying into the air and glaring fixedly at the silhouette.

The figure seemed as if he hadn’t seen the jailer at the Nascent Soul Stage, coldly scanning the prisoners.

The residents nearby lit oil lamps and peered through the window paper, trembling as they watched the figure, contemplating whether to hide indoors or run for their lives.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou broke free from their meditation state and gazed at the figure. They were unable to sense his cultivation, which meant he was a Fusion cultivator!

“Where are the Heartless Creed members?” The figure demanded coldly.

A jailbreak!

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were stunned. They hadn’t expected the Heartless Creed to be so bold as to attempt a prison break.

The captured Heartless Creed members were locked up deep within the prison, far from where Lu Yang and the others were detained. The Heartless Creed followers were considered serious criminals. Those who wanted to join the Heartless Creed also had criminal records and were strictly guarded by the Ye City authorities.

But no matter how strictly they were guarded, it couldn’t stop a Fusion cultivator from breaking them out of prison!

“Brazen scoundrel! Halberd Dance!”

The jailer hollered angrily, brandishing his halberd. The gleaming halberd was especially dazzling against the night sky, looking like another streak of moonlight.

The Halberd Dance was a form of Dance Dao created under moonlight. If used at night, its power could double.

The figure didn’t even glance at the jailer, casually raising a hand to catch the halberd that resembled moonlight. The jailer exerted all his strength but couldn’t move the halberd an inch.

“Boring.”

He casually threw the jailer away, along with the halberd. Extending a finger, he shot a black beam, aiming to pierce the jailer.

Whoosh!

A strange wind blew over from somewhere, dispersing the black beam.

“Who’s there?!”

The figure’s eyes sharpened. A majestic qiongqi had appeared in the air. Its eyes flickered with a bloodthirsty, red glow. Every breath carried frigid air and baleful energy, demonstrating ancient and terrifying power.

“The Nine-Netherworlds Creed!!” Chieftain Jin roared like the Buddhist Lion Roar, the sound shaking the heavens and shattering space.

“The Nine-Netherworlds Creed has a qiongqi at the Fusion Stage?” The figure knitted his brows, greatly puzzled.

Chieftain Jin’s gaze burned into the figure. According to Big Brother, capturing this person would be a great meritorious deed!

“It seems someone knew I was bored in prison and specially came to entertain me!” Chieftain Jin didn’t take the figure seriously at all. Unlike the Dijiang Tribe that is well-versed in song and dance, the Qiongqi Tribe has been renowned for combat prowess since ancient times!

A giant tiger claw swiped down. The air was instantly filled with tearing sounds. The figure’s eyes grew lethal. Lightly tapping his feet, he traversed through the wind like a phantom, easily dodging the strike.

“The Qiongqi Tribe is nothing special.” The figure sneered. Suddenly, he sensed something and looked down. Three claw marks had somehow appeared on his chest, and blood was flowing profusely.

“The Heartless Creed only has this bit of skill; no wonder they voluntarily get cuckolded.” Chieftain Jin burst out laughing, pouncing at the figure again.

The figure seemed to be provoked by Chieftain Jin’s words, or perhaps some unpleasant memory was triggered. Black energy surged endlessly from his sleeves, transforming into ghostly shadows.

“Ghost-Driving Technique?” Chieftain Jin was amused, revealing snow-white tiger fangs. With a flap of his wings, he stirred the surrounding airflow. The ghostly shadows trembled, showing signs of becoming uncontrollable.

“It appears that because our Qiongqi Tribe rarely acts, it has caused the world to forget our Tiger-Henchman Ghost Technique!”

Hearing “Tiger-Henchman Ghost Technique,” Lu Yang’s eyelid twitched slightly. He recalled his reason for joining the Everlasting Creed was to eliminate a tiger demon that knew the Tiger-Henchman Ghost Technique.

“No, something’s not right. The Heartless Creed shouldn’t be here to rescue people.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest frowned, muttering to himself. Based on my understanding of the Heartless Creed, they get no benefit from rescuing people.

Moreover, Great Xia is full of hidden dragons and crouching tigers. A city may seem to lack experts, but who knows if some powerhouse is living reclusively there? Looking at the situation now, forget rescuing people—this person is about to get himself dragged in too.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest spread his spiritual consciousness, searching for anomalies in Ye City. Suddenly, his expression hardened. Transforming into a ray of sword light, he rushed straight toward the City Lord Estate.

“Oh no! There’s trouble at the City Lord Estate!”

Chapter 817: Turmoil at the City Lord Estate

Ye City, City Lord Estate.

City Lord Duan Xiu emerged from his meditation chamber, his brows tightly furrowed as he looked toward the direction of the prison.

“Who is so audacious as to come here and break prisoners out?!”

He was once a military general before being transferred to Ye City as the city lord. His experience in the military had tempered him to remain unflustered in crisis. He calmly analyzed the situation and summoned his subordinates. “Someone who dares to attempt a jailbreak in the city must be at least at the Basic Fusion Stage. Quickly seek aid from the four neighboring cities and have them notify the army stationed nearby!”

“Roger!”

Duan Xiu donned his old black battle armor from the days of his campaigns and put on his helmet, feeling like he had returned to his time in the military over a hundred years ago.

“Hubby, what exactly is this...”

“Dad, what happened?”

Duan Xiu’s wife and son noticed the commotion and emerged from their rooms. Seeing Duan Xiu in armor, their visages were plagued with worry.

Duan Xiu’s steadfast gaze softened. He took his wife’s hand and said earnestly, “It’s just a bunch of vermin thieves. Don’t you know my strength? Nothing will happen. Besides, Ye City still has an unused secret weapon.”

“Then you must be careful.”

His wife and son were deeply concerned for Duan Xiu.

Without looking back, Duan Xiu waved and shouted, “Alright, go back and rest.”

After bidding goodbye to his wife and son, he headed to the estate’s underground secret chamber.

Hardly anyone was aware of the Fusion-level city defense great array that lay beneath Ye City. Once activated, even if it couldn’t defeat the invaders, stalling them until reinforcements arrived was not a problem.

He rotated a book on the bookshelf. With a clatter, the shelf moved aside, revealing a stone door. He infused spirit energy into the door, which opened, revealing a long tunnel.

As he passed through the tunnel, oil lamps nailed to the stone walls lit up one by one, all the way to the deepest part of the secret chamber.

“What?!”

When he reached the secret chamber, he was stunned. The city defense array’s core, which was originally engraved on the walls, had been thoroughly destroyed, with no possibility of repair!

“How is this possible?”

Without my spirit energy as the key, no one could have breached this place!

“City Lord Duan, are you very startled?” A ghostly voice came from behind Duan Xiu.

“Who’s there?!” City Lord Duan whirled around. He had been channeling spirit energy outwardly the entire time, yet he hadn’t noticed anyone approaching. This person’s strength surpasses mine!

The other party stated a name City Lord Duan hadn’t heard before. “Wu Lei, Heartless Creed.”

“So it really is the Heartless Creed!” City Lord Duan stared at Wu Lei warily, secretly touching his storage ring and retrieving a red-tasseled spear. “It appears that you’ve split your forces two ways—one side goes to rescue the prisoners, while the other side comes to stall me!”

Wu Lei shook his head lightly, saying insipidly, “Rescuing the prisoners is merely a cover. Our goal this time is to kill you!”

“Bold indeed!”

The red-tasseled spear soared like a dragon ascending to the nine heavens. Its tip gleamed with blazing light, flames surging skyward. Although City Lord Duan Xiu was at the Void Refinement Stage, he currently possessed combat power at the Fusion Stage. I don’t fear this Wu Lei from the Heartless Creed!

Wu Lei’s hands opened slightly. Sparks of lightning danced at his fingertips, stirring a violent thunderstorm within the narrow chamber.

City Lord Duan was at the center of the thunderstorm, where lightning raged. Before the red-tasseled spear could reach Wu Lei, City Lord Duan was electrocuted until he lost control, and the spear fell to the ground with a clang.

“City Lord Duan, didn’t you know that among Fusion cultivators, there are still gradations of strength?” Wu Lei said this without a trace of mockery in his tone, but with the current situation as a backdrop, the sarcasm felt stronger.

“How is this possible?!” City Lord Duan’s body was numb from the electrocution; he couldn’t even curl his fingers into a fist. He stared at Wu Lei incredulously. Even if there are gradations of strength among Fusion cultivators, a single move shouldn’t be able to decide the outcome. The thunderstorm just now had targeted all my weak points!

“What’s impossible about it?” A familiar voice sounded behind Wu Lei.

“Wenwu?!” City Lord Duan’s eyes widened as he watched his son Duan Wenwu step out from behind Wu Lei.

“You’re a Heartless Creed spy?!”

The secret chamber’s existence, my weak points—if my son had leaked all of this, everything makes sense!

Duan Wenwu looked at his immobilized father and smiled. “I haven’t truly joined the Heartless Creed yet. Only after killing you will I be officially counted as a member.”

To join the Heartless Creed, one must kill the people closest to them.

And the people closest to Duan Wenwu were his parents.

However, his cultivation was too low. Even if City Lord Duan stood there and let him attack, he wouldn’t be able to harm a hair on him. As the city lord, Duan Xiu had life-preserving magical treasures bestowed by the imperial court. This was why Duan Wenwu needed to request the Heartless Creed’s higher-ups to step in.

The Heartless Creed’s higher-ups wouldn’t assist him for nothing. As such, he promised to help open Ye City’s treasury, allowing Wu Lei to take whatever he wanted.

“Why?!” City Lord Duan’s eyes were bloodshot as he desperately resisted the rampaging lightning within.

“Why? How do you have the face to ask why?!” The question seemed to have struck a nerve in Duan Wenwu, and his expression distorted into that of a maniac.

“You neither used your special privileges to exchange benefits with sects to get me into S-class sects or first-class sects, nor did you let me use the treasures in the treasury to boost my cultivation. Because of this, I’m twenty-five this year, yet my cultivation is still stuck at the Golden Core Stage!

“I’m the city lord’s son! But you never used your special privileges for me even once!

“Mother simply comforted me, saying that I was inherently unsuited for cultivation and that I could pursue an official career.

“Official career, official career, official career! So that I can become as rigid as you?!

“Have you ever considered my feelings?! You gave me the name Wenwu—civil and martial—but where’s the ‘wu’ for martial?!”

Golden Core Stage at twenty-five years old wasn’t considered slow. However, this wasn’t the result of Duan Wenwu’s own cultivation—it was City Lord Duan using his own accumulation to help his son improve.

This was the limit. Duan Wenwu’s aptitude was too poor. Advancing further would require natural treasures beyond City Lord Duan’s means.

“Exchanging for benefits would harm the people of Ye City. The treasury belongs to the imperial court; it is not your father’s personal property. How could I give it to you—”

“Enough! Stop talking!” Duan Wu flared with anger. “Since you insist on keeping up your airs as a city lord, don’t blame me for being heartless!”

There was a method to enhance one’s aptitude in the Heartless Creed, and it required family members’ heart-blood as a medicinal primer. The higher the family member’s cultivation, the better the medicinal primer’s effect would be.

Since Father is a Void Refinement cultivator, it means I can transform into a genius with a Dual Spirit Root!

“Wenwu...” City Lord Duan’s eyes grew misty. Seeing this unfamiliar Duan Wenwu, scenes from his memories flashed through his mind: his son’s birth, his son babbling his first words, his son learning to walk, his son climbing trees to rob birds’ nests, his son getting his palms slapped by the teacher, his son crying while memorizing texts, his son getting his spirit root tested, his son drawing qi into his body... How did a good child become like this?

Seeing his father like this, Duan Wenwu’s tone suddenly softened, and he sighed. “Dad, I love you and Mother. But I want to become even stronger. For that, I have no choice but to sacrifice you two. I hope you can understand me.

“True Lord, I’d have to trouble you to take action!” Duan Wenwu bowed to Wu Lei, a glint of killing intent in his eyes. “My parents and everyone in the City Lord Estate, please kill all of them!”

If the imperial court learned that he joined the Heartless Creed, they would surely use this as a lead for their investigation, causing endless trouble.

Hence, he reported the Heartless Creed’s Ye City Branch and had all its members arrested. After that, Wu Lei and another Heartless Creed higher-up used this as a reason to take action—breaking the prisoners out and killing his father and everyone in the City Lord Estate.

That way, he would appear on the casualty list. Duan Wenwu would cease to exist in this world. He could smoothly join the Heartless Creed without worrying about the imperial court’s investigations.

The Heartless Creed prioritized profits and self-interest. With all the benefits I’ve given True Lord Wu Lei, I’ll naturally receive his guidance once I join the Heartless Creed.

Wu Lei made no comments. Lightning erupted from his body, coalescing into a lightning bolt in his palm.

“City Lord Duan, farewell.”

Swish!

A ray of sword light descended from the sky, carving a bottomless gash between Wu Lei and City Lord Duan. The secret chamber, along with the study above, was similarly cleaved.

Wu Lei jerked his head up, glaring at the old Daoist priest holding a sword overhead. He squeezed out three words from between his teeth.

“Taciturn Daoist Priest!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest scrutinized Wu Lei, gradually matching him to someone in his memory.

“You’re Wu Lei? It’s been over a thousand years since we last met, hasn’t it? I remember that when I joined the Heartless Creed back then, you were at the Advanced Fusion Stage. How come you’re still at the Advanced Fusion Stage now?

“Your Heartless Creed’s cultivation methods aren’t effective, huh?”

Chapter 818: The Heartless Creed’s Revenge

All the higher-ups in the Heartless Creed knew that Wu Lei always wore a deadpan expression, never smiling nor showing any emotional fluctuations, having walked far on the path of the Heartless Dao.

But right now, Wu Lei was truly struggling to keep his heart as calm as water.

Back then, the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s actions had practically crippled the creed fortune of the Heartless Creed, dealing it a severe blow.

When the Heartless Creed recovered from the damage, many privately wanted to seek revenge on the Taciturn Daoist Priest. These were people who had their mental states messed up by the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

But by then, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had advanced from the Divine Transfiguration Stage to the Fusion Stage, even becoming a sect leader. Killing him wouldn’t be easy.

Moreover, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had too many enemies. When the Heartless Creed members wanted to kill him, a Fusion cultivator from the righteous path might suddenly appear, also intending to seek revenge on the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

The problem was that if someone from the Heartless Creed was present, the righteous Fusion cultivator would definitely deal with the Heartless Creed first before finding trouble with the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

However, the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s improved version of killing the wife to prove one’s Dao had gained the creed leader’s approval—or rather, lavish praise. Even after the Taciturn Daoist Priest defected, the Heartless Creed continued to use the improved version he proposed. As a result, many in the Heartless Creed no longer considered proving their Heartless Dao through marriage.

At the thought that the purpose of marriage and love was to send their wives to others... who the hell could carry on with that?

In cultivation, the higher one’s cultivation, the higher the demand on one’s mental state. After the incident with the Taciturn Daoist Priest, many Heartless Creed higher-ups’ cultivation stagnated. It took them several centuries of convalescence to finally restore their original mental states.

Now, Wu Lei looked like he might soon fail to maintain his mental state.

“You’re the old Taciturn... Sect Leader?” City Lord Duan hadn’t expected the Taciturn Daoist Priest to appear and save the day. Did he just happen to be in Ye City?

The Taciturn Daoist Priest scratched his chin. “Actually, I’ve been in your Ye City prison recently. However, I was worried old friends might come to gawk at me and disrupt the order in our Ye City prison, so I considerately used a fake name and changed my appearance.

“Well, seeing our Ye City in crisis, I figured I’d render meritorious service to atone for my crimes, so I came out to fight.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest wore an expression that read, “You must reduce my sentence after I render meritorious service.”

Hearing the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s words, Wu Lei’s heart stirred. He secretly crushed a jade slip.

Following this, the Taciturn Daoist Priest began reminiscing with Wu Lei. “I see that you have little future staying in the Heartless Creed. Why not come to our Dao-Seeking Sect’s Incarceration Peak? It’s full of mighty cultivation experts, more than enough to guide a mere Fusion cultivator like you.

“Let me tell you, I don’t even let others know that our Dao-Seeking Sect has such a great place. It’s only because we know each other that I’m telling you.”

“Shut up!” Wu Lei growled.

He pressed his palms together. Thunder light blazed around him, instantly summoning a thundercloud. Amidst thunderous roars, countless lightning bolts shot from the cloud like spirit snakes, aimed at the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

We're both at the Advanced Fusion Stage. What’s more, I’ve been at the Advanced Fusion Stage for two thousand years—I’m a bona fide veteran Advanced Fusion cultivator. I can just kill you!

A long sword left its sheath. Sword qi crisscrossed like a Milky Way waterfall, resembling a flowing ink painting. The sword qi waterfall surged backward into the sky, colliding with the thundercloud.

The thundercloud seemed like paper and was pierced through by the sword qi waterfall.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest flicked his wrist, and the sword tip lifted slightly, as if it was resonating with heaven and earth, triggering the sword intent drifting about in the surroundings. Sharp sword intent condensed on the blade, refined to the extreme and swift to the extreme.

The sword intent erupted, illuminating Wu Lei’s terror-stricken face.

Wu Lei hastily formed an armor from lightning, protecting his vital spots. However, this still couldn’t withstand the condensed sword intent, which penetrated his shoulder blade.

Wu Lei retreated repeatedly, putting distance between himself and the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“We’re both at the Fusion Stage. How come you can’t even withstand one of my moves? The gap between us is even bigger than I’d imagined?”

“Little Taciturn scoundrel!” Wu Lei could no longer suppress his anger. In terms of seniority, he belonged to the same generation of cultivators as the Grand-Shifu. The Taciturn Daoist Priest was merely a junior!

The Taciturn Daoist Priest shook his head gently. Concerned for Wu Lei’s future. “Look at you, your mental state is lacking. How can you survive in the Heartless Creed like this?”

Wu Lei formed hand seals and softly changed lightning incantations. Instantly, clouds in the sky churned, and thunder rumbled. Several thick lightning bolts answered his summons, crashing down violently.

Sword light and lightning interwove, illuminating the entire city and erupting with deafening roars.

As the light faded, Wu Lei spat a mouthful of blood. His right arm was severed, and sword light flickered at the amputation point, preventing the wound from healing.

Wu Lei hadn’t expected the gulf between him and the Taciturn Daoist Priest to be so massive, despite both of them being Advanced Fusion cultivators. It was just a few exchanges, and I’m already injured to this extent!

The Taciturn Daoist Priest narrowed his eyes. He had been wary of Wu Lei fleeing, but the other party seemed to have the intention of stalling him, keeping him occupied.

What is he waiting for?

Suddenly, a terrifying oppressive pressure enveloped the Taciturn Daoist Priest. As he was flying in the air, he couldn’t withstand this pressure and nearly plummeted from the sky.

The oppressive pressure’s aftershocks ravaged Ye City. The civilians felt as if they had been plunged into an ice cellar, their bodies shivering and their teeth chattering.

“Little Taciturn brat, I didn’t expect you to be here.

“I hereby establish the rule: [No information may leave Ye City.]

“I hereby establish the rule: [No person may leave Ye City.]”

After these two rules were established, a curtain darker than the night sky appeared above that figure, rapidly spreading in all directions until it encased all of Ye City.

“Now, it’s time to settle our scores.” A cold, middle-aged man looked at the Taciturn Daoist Priest. His voice was like thunder; his mere words could cause space to shake.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest looked up at the middle-aged man and laughed out loud. “I wondered why that trash Wu Lei never fled. So it’s because he wanted to buy time until you come, Great Creed Leader Su.”

The Heartless Creed Vice Creed Leader, Su Moran, was at the Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

With Su Moran backing him, Wu Lei’s confidence surged immediately. “Little Taciturn scoundrel, today is the day you die!”

Earlier, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had mentioned that no righteous cultivators knew he was here. Furthermore, Ye City had been sealed by Vice Creed Leader Su, allowing entry but no exit.

Given the immense gap in cultivation and the lack of reinforcements, this was a once-in-a-millennia chance to kill the Taciturn Daoist Priest!

Su Moran was also a victim of that incident back then; he could even be said to have the highest cultivation among the victims. He hated the Taciturn Daoist Priest to the core, but he was always cautious. Unless certain of a one-hit kill, he wouldn’t act.

If they let the Taciturn Daoist Priest escape, killing him next time would only be harder!

“Great Creed Leader Lu, you old thing, why are you like that idiot Wu Lei? Over a thousand years have passed, yet you’re still stuck at the Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation Stage?

“Has your cultivation peaked? Or... has your mental state developed flaws?”

Su Moran was unperturbed. He took out two axes and said solemnly, “Little Taciturn brat, stalling for time is useless. You won’t find loopholes in the rules to escape Ye City.

“I have waited over a thousand years for this opportunity today.”

If he didn’t kill the Taciturn Daoist Priest, his mental state would always be flawed, entangled by hatred. To advance his cultivation, he must kill the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Other methods won’t work!

The Taciturn Daoist Priest wanted to stay more, buying time to seek a glimmer of hope. After all, although he possessed combat power at the Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he couldn’t contend with a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, let alone a veteran Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation opponent.

Su Moran had been investigating the Taciturn Daoist Priest. He knew that if he allowed the latter to speak more, finding a loophole was indeed possible.

The best way to deal with the Taciturn Daoist Priest was to not let him speak.

Clang!

Su Moran’s muscles tensed. Two giant axes slammed down. The axes were broad, their blades incomparably sharp. These were supposed to be two-handed axes, but Su Moran held one in each hand.

The giant axes smashed toward the Taciturn Daoist Priest. He blocked it with his sword, but the force was beyond what he could withstand.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest spat blood and directly crashed into the City Lord Estate’s rockery, forming a “大” character with his limbs splayed out.

“If you try to escape, Ye City’s three million civilians will all join you in death,” Su Moran threatened coldly, knowing this was the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s weak point.

“Escape? Why would I escape?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest slowly raised his head. Half his face was stained with blood, appearing exceptionally ghastly. His lips curled into an eerie smile.

“Do you know why I never advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?”

He exerted force with both arms, shattering the rockery. Step by step, he walked toward Su Moran, his imposing aura rising like bamboo shoots.

“I was afraid that if I advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, you old thing wouldn’t dare to come look for me!”

Chapter 819: The Taciturn Daoist Priest Advances to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage

From afar, Lu Yang heard his shifu’s words and suddenly recalled what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had said when she first met the Taciturn Daoist Priest. She mentioned that Shifu could have advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, but for some reason, he has been suppressing his cultivation.

So it was for today?

Su Moran’s gaze sharpened as he stared at the Taciturn Daoist Priest, then he suddenly relaxed.

As a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, I know best how difficult it is to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Mental state, cultivation, condition, comprehension, pills—all are indispensable.

Back when he aimed to advance to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he didn’t scruple to offer a small town as a blood sacrifice and used natural treasures to temper his body. Unfortunately, he still didn’t succeed. Due to his failure, he was severely wounded and pursued by Great Xia, fleeing all the way to the Demon Region. He convalesced for over a century, then offered an entire demon race as a blood sacrifice before finally succeeding in advancing to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. The whole process had been fraught with twists and turns.

For over a thousand years, he had been monitoring the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s activities. For instance, over a decade ago, the Dao-Seeking Sect announced that the Taciturn Daoist Priest had gone missing. It was only after ten years that the Taciturn Daoist Priest reappeared in the public eye.

Those ten years of disappearance must be the little Taciturn brat failing his tribulation and secretly recuperating!

Having failed his tribulation and been injured just ten years ago, it’s impossible for him to attempt the breakthrough again in a mere ten years!

“Advancing to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage? Mere bluffing.”

“Whether it’s mere bluffing or not, you old thing just have to try and find out!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest shouted, no longer suppressing himself. His gradually ascending aura now skyrocketed. Although it was not as terrifying as Su Moran’s oppressive pressure, it wasn’t an aura a Fusion cultivator could exude either.

This was an aura only a Basic Transcendent Tribulation cultivator could possess. The Taciturn Daoist Priest hadn’t even reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, yet he already had an aura at that level.

Boom!

Unleashing all his aura, the Taciturn Daoist Priest summoned a lightning tribulation that filled the sky, dispersing Su Moran’s oppressive pressure. Curved purple-gold lightning rampaged between heaven and earth, connecting the sky and the ground. The earth shook, and Ye City’s inhabitants, whether mortals or cultivators, felt fear grip their hearts, not daring to look up at this terrifying heavenly tribulation.

“Oh yo? Purple Heaven Destruction Lightning; your shifu’s aptitude isn’t bad.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy only needed a glance at the lightning tribulation to recognize its type. She smugly boasted to Lu Yang, “Of course, it can’t compare to the lightning tribulations this immortal faced.”

Before the Heaven Mandate Immortal achieved immortalhood, lightning tribulations had already existed in the world. The Heaven Mandate Immortal’s Dao Fruit allowed him to control the original lightning tribulations and create new ones.

According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, after the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s ascension, the types of lightning tribulations increased more than tenfold, becoming complex and numerous, able to satisfy all cultivators’ needs except for those who didn’t desire tribulations.

“There really is a lightning tribulation.” Su Moran felt that things seemed to be somewhat beyond his expectations.

Unfortunately, during a tribulation, no one could interfere. Anyone who interfered would also have to undergo the tribulation.

He considered retreating, slowly moving toward the edge of Ye City. There’s no need for me to gamble on whether the little Taciturn brat can break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

However, the Taciturn Daoist Priest clearly didn’t want Su Moran to leave.

As Su Moran approached the city’s periphery, the Taciturn Daoist Priest dragged the lightning tribulation toward Su Moran. If Su Moran dared to leave Ye City, the Taciturn Daoist Priest would dare to rapidly close in on him before he could leave. Both of us can undergo the tribulation together!

The Taciturn Daoist Priest dared to bet that he could survive the lightning tribulation, but Su Moran didn’t dare to.

Seeing this, Su Moran had no choice but to abandon the idea of leaving Ye City.

Facing the millions of purple-gold lightning snakes ravaging everywhere between heaven and earth, the Taciturn Daoist Priest slowly exhaled a clear breath. With a thought, he willed countless spirit swords to emerge from the ground.

One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords!

He pointed two fingers skyward. The countless spirit swords sprang from the ground like fish leaping over the dragon gate, their blades agile as they met the millions of lightning snakes.

Swords and lightning clashed once more. The brilliant collision instantly illuminated Ye City as bright as day, its intensity far surpassing the battle with Wu Lei!

One after another, more violent lightning strikes followed, each more ferocious than the last. The Taciturn Daoist Priest held a spirit sword horizontally before him, its surface reflecting his calm eyes.

Beneath the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s feet, a broad path of Sword Dao unfurled. With each step, a spirit sword materialized beneath his feet. These all belonged to the sword cultivators whom the Taciturn Daoist Priest had defeated. With his Sword Heart, he imprinted his opponents’ swords into his own Sword Dao, making them part of it.

Some of these spirit sword phantoms came from Foundation Establishment opponents, others from Divine Transfiguration opponents, and some were even from the entire wall of the Sword Tower... Now, under the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s enhancement, all these spirit sword phantoms had risen to a level capable of resisting the heavenly tribulation.

Faced with the endless heavenly tribulation, the Taciturn Daoist Priest casually picked up a sword from beneath his feet. After blocking one lightning strike, it cracked in the middle. The Taciturn Daoist Priest casually tossed it beneath his feet, and it was absorbed and restored by the Sword Dao. He then picked up another sword, repeating the series of actions.

Within the horrifying heavenly tribulation, the three-chi space around the Taciturn Daoist Priest seemed like a pure land, unaffected by the tribulation.

However, the Taciturn Daoist Priest wasn’t purely resisting with the Sword Dao. In reality, each spirit sword couldn’t completely block the lightning tribulation. A portion of the lightning tribulation was still transmitted to the Taciturn Daoist Priest through the spirit swords, and he used the tribulation to temper his spirit and flesh. During this process, his cultivation continuously rose, while his aura grew increasingly restrained, appearing weak to outsiders.

When the strongest, final lightning strike of the tribulation fell, the Taciturn Daoist Priest dispersed the Sword Dao beneath him.

Crack!

The Taciturn Daoist Priest seemed to have become a sword himself. Boundless, vast sword intent was stored within him. He was like a sheathed immortal sword, hidden yet ready to be unleashed. When the final lightning tribulation strike was about to hit his head, the immortal sword unsheathed, severing this lightning tribulation!

The lightning tribulation split in two. The lightning glow dissipated. The clear night sky reappeared in people’s sight.

“So this is how the Transcendent Tribulation Stage feels like? It’s truly more comfortable than the Fusion Stage.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest sensed the changes brought by his breakthrough and grinned.

Ordinary cultivators who had just advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage would need to consolidate their cultivation. However, he had deliberately suppressed himself at the Advanced Fusion Stage for decades, rendering seclusion no longer necessary.

He abruptly raised his head and stared at the cold Su Moran, saying slowly, “Great Creed Leader Su, you have waited over a thousand years for an opportunity to kill me, right?

“What a coincidence. I’ve also waited over a thousand years for the opportunity today.

“I can’t eat or sleep in peace if I don’t kill you.”

“Bumptious! You think just advancing to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage makes you qualified to fight me?” Su Moran’s tone remained as flat as ever. You’ve just advanced, lack combat experience, and there’s an obvious cultivation gap between us—how do you think you can fight me?

The Taciturn Daoist Priest revealed a mocking smile. He violently swung his sword, catching Su Moran off guard. The sword broke through his defense, leaving a scar on his face.

Seeing this, the Taciturn Daoist Priest directly pressed forward, staring into Su Moran’s eyes.

“In my sect, I had my shifu spar with me. After leaving the sect, I had Senior Jiesha exchange blows with me. Why would you think I lack experience fighting Transcendent Tribulation cultivators?”

Chapter 820: Someone Wants Your Life

“Our sect leader planned this far ahead?” Meng Jingzhou was utterly floored. Could his usual habit of provoking everyone all be for today’s battle?

Lu Yang said faintly, “No, I think it’s simply my shifu’s nature to make enemies everywhere.”

“The little Taciturn brat has reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?” The Heartless Creed Fusion cultivator above Lu Yang noticed the commotion at the City Lord Estate. Clearly, he also had a grudge against the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“You still have the energy to care about others?” Chieftain Jin’s eyes were blood red. Fanning demonic flames, he opened his maw wide, swallowing all the ghostly shadows summoned by his opponent and refining them into tiger-henchman ghosts within his stomach for his own use.

The Qiongqi Tribe was born for battle. Once they entered combat mode, they would focus solely on their opponent, ignoring the external environment.

According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s assessment, this was called a “one-track mind.”

“Who will win?” The Innate Daoist Priest watched the skies above the City Lord Estate nervously. Even when he was at the Fusion Stage, he had rarely seen battles at the Transcendent Tribulation level. He didn’t expect a battle of this level to erupt just days into his prison stay.

~~~

Beneath the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s feet, the broad Sword Dao unfurled once more. Countless sword shadows emerged, the killing intent shocking the world. Sword rays shot skyward unpredictably like soaring dragons and dancing phoenixes.

The spirit swords breathed out iridescent sword qi that was sharp and blinding, capturing one’s soul.

Su Moran’s hair stood on end. Before he contacted the sword qi, his body felt a piercing pain, as though millions of needles were pricking him. He vigorously raised his two giant axes. Behind him, countless phantom images of shattered mountains appeared—all mountains his axes had cleaved.

“Five Sacred Mountains Split!”

A continuous range of mountain phantom images crashed down alongside the axes, as if the heavens were collapsing and the earth were sinking.

The Ye City civilians trembled. If this strike had landed on Ye City, it would have been reduced to ruins, with not a single survivor.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest sat in the lotus position with one leg. Using his sword as a qin, he plucked it while singing. His song was bold and heroic, stirring the soul. Ten thousand swords chimed in unison. Sword qi rushed into the clouds, disrupting heaven and earth, crushing the mountain phantoms.

Lu Yang suddenly remembered Gan Tian saying she was proficient in music, having learned from their shifu.

“I hereby establish the rule: [You are not allowed to call out the names of your moves.]” The Taciturn Daoist Priest established a temporary rule for the first time as a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

Su Moran swung his axes. Just as he wanted to call out the name of his move, he was nearly choked to death by the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s rule.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s rule constrained only a minor matter, so its binding power was exceedingly strong. Moreover, Su Moran had previously laid down two [Rules] to seal Ye City, leaving him with no strength to resist the Taciturn Daoist Priest in terms of rules.

“Don’t randomly shout the names of moves during battle; it’s bad for your throat... One Sword Transforms Into Ten Thousand Swords!”

Tens of thousands of spirit sword phantoms flew from the broad Sword Dao, resonating with each other. Sword rays fused, transforming into a divine sword that was three chi long.

“This is Ten Thousand Swords Return to One!” With repeated provocations from the Taciturn Daoist Priest, it was useless even if Su Moran chanted Heart-Purifying Incantations a hundred times in his heart. Finally, Su Moran could no longer contain his anger.

Not letting me call the names of my moves is one thing, but you can shout them out and deliberately get them wrong!

“Is your brain not working due to old age? Why do you believe whatever I shout?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest looked at Su Moran disdainfully. You can be the vice creed leader with a level like this?

Suddenly, just as the three-chi divine sword that had coalesced from ten thousand swords was about to pierce Su Moran, it exploded, transforming back into ten thousand swords. Su Moran was caught off guard by this move, and his body became riddled with sword holes.

“I told you it was One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords. Why didn’t you guard against it?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest laughed, his eyes full of mockery.

Watching from afar, Lu Yang thought to himself, Shifu, these moves of yours probably aren’t the experience you gained from sparring with Grand-Shifu and Master Jiesha, right?

For the past thousand years, Su Moran had been paying attention to the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s activities and fighting style. However, the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s combat style was varied and inexhaustible. It was impossible to grasp the patterns and counter them just by observation.

The battle rapidly intensified. Sword light and axe shadows interwove, and the air was pervaded with sparks from the fierce combat.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s figure was as agile as a specter. His sword begot numerous sword shadows, shifting from complex to simple, then simple to complex, the variations endless. The twin axes were powerful and heavy. Swung like the wind, it provided offensive and defensive capabilities and was impervious to water.
