Watching from the side, Wu Lei dared not intervene in a battle of this level. With his cultivation, even suffering one hit could mean death or grievous injury.

Suddenly, the Taciturn Daoist Priest found an opening. Flicking the tip of his sword, he employed skillful force to pry apart the crossed axes, exposing Su Moran’s vital point at his chest.

“Oh no!” Su Moran cursed. He wanted to resume a defensive stance, but the Taciturn Daoist Priest had forced him to reveal this opening step by step through his series of attacks. The Taciturn Daoist Priest had anticipated this situation long ago and charged up power for a while. How could he give Su Moran a chance to react?

“Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate!”

The sharp sword slashed down like a cascading silk ribbon. The sky curtain trembled, carrying boundless killing intent toward Su Moran.

When the Taciturn Daoist Priest had executed his move at the Advanced Fusion Stage, it could already force the Dawnbreaker Venerable Lord, an Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, to dodge. Now that he had advanced to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, the power of this strike far surpassed anything before!

Heaven’s Gate opened wide. The sword qi, which resembled a ten-thousand-zhang cascading silk ribbon, buried Su Moran underneath.

Su Moran suddenly appeared at another location. The Death-Substitution Talisman on his chest suddenly burned, signifying that he had died just now.

“Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest strode forward. Without a second thought, he delivered another sword strike at Su Moran, who had just escaped.

The firmament shook. With exposed sharpness and rainbow-like resplendence, it cleaved at Su Moran.

This time, Su Moran had no more Death-Substitution Talismans. The sword struck its target, splitting his body in two!

Su Moran activated a mystic art, burning his essence blood to heal his body. Although he was healed, his vitality was severely damaged. A clear line was still visible down the middle of his body.

He desperately tried to flee Ye City.

Bang!

His head slammed against an invisible wall surrounding Ye City.

He had previously established the rule: [No person may leave Ye City.]

And that included himself.

He was about to revoke this rule when the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s voice sounded from behind. “[You are not allowed to leave Ye City.]”

Su Moran had established rules, so the Taciturn Daoist Priest had the authority to establish two rules. He had waited until now to use the second rule!

“Wait—”

Su Moran still wanted to say something, but the Taciturn Daoist Priest didn’t even listen. He penetrated Su Moran’s spirit platform with his sword, stepped on his body, and descended from high above, heavily smashing into the ground.

“Wait, spare my life! We can go to the Demon Region and have Supreme Lord Zhu Tian use his Incipient Dao Fruit to turn me into your slave!” Su Moran hastily shouted.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest revealed two rows of white teeth, looking particularly terrifying in the darkness.

He shook his head gently. “Regrettably, I’ve accepted a commission. Someone wants your life.”

Who? Who is it? I can give you double—no, triple the benefits!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was smiling, though it was frigid. “Over a thousand years ago, I led the Dao-Seeking Sect and imperial court forces to eradicate your Heartless Creed bases. We rescued many people—men and women, young and old—countless victims you all had tortured until they were beyond recognition.

“When they saw me, they cried, beseeching me to kill all you Heartless Creed members.

“Great Creed Leader Lu, what benefits are you planning to give me to make those people forget their hatred toward your Heartless Creed?”

Chapter 821: Let’s Not Trouble Yun Zhi Over a Minor Matter Like This

“I...”

Su Moran still wanted to defend himself, but the Taciturn Daoist Priest twisted the spirit sword embedded in Su Moran’s forehead, directly shattering his spirit platform.

Killing a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator was exceedingly difficult. A wisp of a soul flew out from Su Moran’s spirit platform, desperately fleeing at the cost of exhausting its origin energy.

“Trying to run?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest sneered. With a single thought, sword qi crisscrossed, occupying every inch of space. Any object attempting to move within this field of sword qi would be sliced to smithereens.

Su Moran’s soul was too terrified to move. The Taciturn Daoist Priest took out a red wine gourd, uncorked it, and sucked Su Moran’s soul inside.

A matter like soul searching has to be left to someone like Shifu, a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator with powerful soul strength. If I attempt it carelessly, it could easily lead to backlash from Su Moran’s soul.

“What a pity, those people rescued back then can’t witness this.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest sighed inwardly. That was over a thousand years ago. Only Void Refinement cultivators could live until now. The people rescued back then hadn’t cultivated to the Void Refinement Stage.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest looked up, casually shooting a streak of sword qi that pierced Wu Lei, who was preparing to take to his heels.

Meanwhile, Chieftain Jin’s battle with the Heartless Creed Fusion cultivator was also nearing its end. Witnessing Su Moran’s defeat, the Heartless Creed Fusion cultivator was frightened out of his wits and lost the will to fight, wanting to escape the battlefield.

But how could Chieftain Jin give him such a chance? Flapping his wings, the metal Jinwu Wind immobilized him for a moment. Before the latter could even react, Chieftain Jin opened his cavernous maw and swallowed him whole.

“See, this is how battles should be fought—one-track minded. Only then can one unleash their full combat power.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy praised the Qiongqi Tribe’s combat style lavishly and had repeatedly instructed the Barbarian Tribe to learn from them.

“It’s...it’s over?” City Lord Duan didn’t dare to believe he had witnessed the Taciturn Daoist Priest breaking through mid-battle and killing the Heartless Creed’s vice creed leader.

“It’s over. I’ll have to trouble you with the subsequent cleanup, City Lord Duan. I shall return to the prison first to check on my cellmates.”

“All settled.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest returned to the prison cell and patted the red gourd, showing off his trophy to Lu Yang and the others.

He elatedly did his calculations. “Catching one Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation cultivator and one Advanced Fusion cultivator—if I convert it to contribution points, how many days could I be the acting sect leader... Oh wait, I am the sect leader.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest suddenly remembered his own identity.

“So impressive.” The Innate Daoist Priest looked at the Taciturn Daoist Priest with admiration. Breaking through mid-battle and challenging beyond one’s level—this is a scene worthy of leaving an indelible mark on history, a tale that would be passed down with approbation through future generations.

“Su Moran undoubtedly wields much intelligence. Now that we have captured one of their vice-creed leaders, we must guard against the Heartless Creed coming to snatch him back.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest knew this matter was not yet truly over. Only after Su Moran’s soul had been delivered to the Dao-Seeking Sect would it be properly concluded.

“Should I call Big Senior Sister over?” Lu Yang volunteered, ready to employ the Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest waved a hand. “No need to trouble her with such a minor matter. Just ask Founding Ancestor Vast Sea to come.”

He lowered his head and asked the Innate Daoist Priest, “Founding Ancestor, you should have a way to summon Founding Ancestor Vast Sea, right?”

“Yes, I do.” The Innate Daoist Priest was both a senior and junior to the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, so he should have a way to contact him.

He took out a Teleportation Talisman from the front of his robe, and the talisman ignited on its own. A spatial gate opened, and a figure stepped out.

The figure had his eyes tightly closed and arms spread wide, his clothes in disarray. “Come, Ya-er, let’s kiss... Huh? Where is this?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord sensed a change in his spatial location, shifting from the East Sea to land.

Everyone watched silently as the Vast Sea Daoist Lord emerged from the spatial gate, trembling with fear and not daring to speak. Before a half-immortal wielding the Space Incipient Dao Fruit, it was unlikely anyone present had the ability to escape.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord glanced around. There were mostly familiar faces—the Innate Daoist Priest, the Taciturn Daoist Priest, Lu Yang, and Meng Jingzhou—and an unfamiliar qiongqi. He surmised that the Innate Daoist Priest had used the Teleportation Talisman, which was meant for emergencies.

He cleared his throat and asked seriously, “I was in seclusion. May I know why you all are looking for me?”

Judging by the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s earlier behavior, everyone found it hard to believe he was just in seclusion.

The Innate Daoist Priest pointed at the Taciturn Daoist Priest. “It’s like this. He captured a vice creed leader of the Heartless Creed and was worried about possible mishaps during transit, so he wanted to trouble you to teleport the vice creed leader’s soul back to the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Captured a vice creed leader of the Heartless Creed?!” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord was astonished. The Heartless Creed members were always cautious, and it was extremely challenging to catch a high-level cultivator.

“Good, good, good. Leave this to me. I’d like to see which Heartless Creed member dares to snatch someone from me!” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord was overjoyed, his tone naturally carrying a trace of arrogance.

~~~

Back at the City Lord Estate, City Lord Duan personally apprehended his son.

Looking at his son, who was still struggling, he sighed. How did my good son become like this?

His son’s transgressions were too grave, exceeding the authority of a city lord. This matter would have to be handed over to the imperial court... I’m afraid death is inevitable.

The city lords from nearby cities arrived with large contingents, along with military troops stationed nearby. They rushed to City Lord Duan’s location immediately, only to find the battle already concluded.

“What? The Taciturn Daoist Priest captured a vice creed leader from the Heartless Creed?”

Everyone was astounded. This was a major matter, far beyond their purview. They needed to be reported to the imperial court right away, requesting the dispatch of a high-ranking official to preside over the matter.

~~~

Imperial city.

It was already late at night. In principle, officials should have already gone to rest, but high-level cultivators had the advantage of being able to work around the clock.

The Minister of Justice wearily reviewed a document. Usually, he didn’t work overtime this late. However, with the recent focus on the East Sea, Great Xia cultivators were teaming up to go there, which had triggered numerous extraterritorial cases; managing them was troublesome. Moreover, with the increasing variety of extraterritorial cases, previous laws were proving inadequate, necessitating the creation of new legislation.

Furthermore, the Demon Kingdom had the intention of establishing diplomatic relations with Great Xia. Matters concerning legal coordination fell under his responsibility, another troublesome affair.

“Why are there so many things happening? Previously, it was the Demon Kingdom, and now, it's the East Sea. These two places were perfectly fine and quiet before, but they’ve both become lively in the last two years. Is it because of the Battle of the Great Era? Isn’t it said that the Battle of the Great Era would recreate the glory of antiquity, with contention between prodigies and battles everywhere?”

The Minister of Justice finished reviewing the final document and prepared to return home to rest.

A subordinate hastily pushed open the door and reported, “Your Excellency, an urgent report from Ye City in Ji Province—one of the heads of a diabolic creed has been captured.”

“That’s good news!” The Minister of Justice’s spirits instantly lifted, all signs of drowsiness vanishing. He hadn’t expected such favorable tidings to arrive late at night.

“Which fellow Daoist captured him?!”

“Uh...it was the Taciturn Daoist Priest.”

“I’m asking who captured them, not who got captured.”

Chapter 822: All Cellmates Have Left

After listening to the detailed report from his subordinate, the Minister of Justice verified that he wasn’t mistaken.

It’s indeed the Taciturn Daoist Priest, this grandson who captured Su Moran.

“Let’s go, we’re heading to Ye City. Also, call the Luoshui Guard. Remember not to be too conspicuous, lest we alert the Heartless Creed to our movements!”

The Minister of Justice led a small contingent of elites toward Ye City. Recalling scenes from his youth of being tricked by the Taciturn Daoist Priest in the imperial city, he seethed with indignation.

“Even he could become a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator? Is there no justice in this world?!

“So much administrative work—let His Majesty handle it from now on. I’m going to cultivate!”

~~~

On the way to Ye City, the Luoshui Guard personnel joined the Minister of Justice. The leader of the squad was Luo Changhe,[1] an Intermediate Transcendent Tribulation cultivator and one of the Nine Palaces of the Luoshui Guard.

Unfortunately, they arrived a step late. The Vast Sea Daoist Lord had already teleported Su Moran’s soul back to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Nevertheless, it wasn’t all too late. The Taciturn Daoist Priest and his cellmates were still serving their sentences here.

“Old Xu, over here, over here!” The Taciturn Daoist Priest waved from below, greeting the Minister of Justice, Xu Xin.

Xu Xin realized he really couldn’t see through the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s cultivation level now, confirming the latter had genuinely reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, rather than defeating Su Moran through some secret art that endowed him with a temporary spike in power.

The moment the Xu Xin landed, he heard the Taciturn Daoist Priest speak in an aged and patronizing tone. “Little Xu, you’re a veteran. You understand the rules of the cultivation world without me having to explain. In the cultivation world, the strong reign supreme. Considering that we were once peers, you can just call me Senior Taciturn.”

Xu Xin rolled his eyes, unwilling to engage with the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

Only then did he notice the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s cellmates.

“Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, what are you two doing here as well?”

Back when he had been tricked into prison by the Taciturn Daoist Priest, he had seen Lu Yang visiting.

As for Meng Jingzhou, how could he not recognize someone from the Meng Family? They were another major faction driving the improvement of Great Xia’s legal system.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou opened their mouths, but they were too embarrassed to say they had mutually stolen from each other so that they could come in to accompany the Innate Daoist Priest.

Seeing them like this, Xu Xin understood. They must have been sabotaged by the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“Where is Su Moran?” Xu Xin remembered the purpose of his visit.

“Founding Ancestor Vast Sea sent him back to our Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Xu Xin turned around, prepared to head to the Dao-Seeking Sect, but the Taciturn Daoist Priest pulled him back.

“Hey, wait, wait, wait. I worked so hard to capture Su Moran. That counts as a major meritorious service, right? Go through the procedures and get me released.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s original intention in staying in prison was to let Chieftain Jin experience life. After the incident in Ye City, this place was no longer suitable for them, so they might as well get out.

He pointed at Chieftain Jin beside him. “And my little brother here, you can just call him Jinzi. He captured a Fusion cultivator from the Heartless Creed. That’s also a major meritorious service.”

Xu Xin gave Chieftain Jin a meaningful look. In this day and age, there’s still someone eager to hang out with the Taciturn Daoist Priest? Is there something wrong with his brain?

“Fine. I’ll go look for the City Lord later to complete the procedures. Nothing else, right? If not, I’m leaving.” Xu Xin was in a hurry to get to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“And also, this person needs to be released too.”

“Could you say everything at once? Who is this person now?” Xu Xin looked in the direction the Taciturn Daoist Priest was pointing and saw the Innate Daoist Priest sitting in the corner.

“He’s a disciple of our Dao-Seeking Sect. His original intention was to infiltrate the Heartless Creed as a spy, but he didn’t expect the Heartless Creed base to be raided by the Ye City authorities. He was too embarrassed to say he was from the Dao-Seeking Sect, worried about tarnishing our sect’s reputation, so he got arrested.”

Xu Xin was flabbergasted. I didn’t expect the Dao-Seeking Sect to have such a pure-hearted and honest disciple. Judging by how he has just reached the Foundation Establishment Stage, he has probably been in the Dao-Seeking Sect for about a year.

To spend a year in the Dao-Seeking Sect yet still manage to grow out of the mud unsullied is truly remarkable.

“This can also be arranged.”

Xu Xin was about to leave but suddenly stopped. “There’s nothing else this time, right?”

“None, none. Go ahead.”

Soon, those from the imperial court left the prison. The Taciturn Daoist Priest, Chieftain Jin, and the Innate Daoist Priest also departed, leaving only Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou behind.

The two stared at each other. In the blink of an eye, the once lively cell had been reduced to just the two of them.

“Thinking about it carefully, there really doesn’t seem to be any reason for us to be released.”

They hadn’t contributed during the battle, and neither were they unjustly imprisoned like the Innate Daoist Priest.

“How many more days do we have to stay locked up here?”

“Ten days.”

The two brothers shook their heads and sighed. We’ll just have to stay here obediently and cultivate for ten days then.

“We don’t even have a roof over our heads anymore.” Lu Yang looked up. The starry sky was clear and boundless. The roof had been torn off at the very beginning by the Fusion cultivator from the Heartless Creed.

He was cultivating in his mental space, still cuffed with manacles, as he gazed helplessly at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy enjoying life on the other side of the cage. So envious.

“Good things didn’t happen to good people this time.”

~~~

After the Vast Sea Daoist Lord brought Su Moran’s soul back to the Dao-Seeking Sect, he immediately summoned the Grand-Shifu from Incarceration Peak and Elder Tao from the scripture library, and requested Yun Zhi’s presence.

Wu Lei’s corpse was handed over to Fifth Elder to be refined into a magical treasure.

On the other hand, Su Moran’s corpse wasn’t refined. After all, it was the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s spoils of war and could be used to strengthen his personal sword.

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s top-tier combatants convened here and directly performed soul searching, obtaining all of Su Moran’s memories.

Just then, personnel from the Ministry of Justice and the Luoshui Guard rushed over to liaise with the Dao-Seeking Sect regarding the matter on the Heartless Creed.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord shared the intelligence and frowned. “As I thought, it’s challenging to deal with the Heartless Creed. According to Su Moran’s memories, the Heartless Creed Leader’s appearance and age are unknown, suspected to be a half-immortal. Su Moran speculated that his purpose in founding the Heartless Creed was to gather all heartless individuals, observe their insights on the Heartless Dao, and use that to complete himself.”

“In other words, the Heartless Creed’s creed leader has been the same person since the founding of the Heartless Creed?” Luo Changhe of the Luoshui Guard was astonished.

“Extremely likely!”

“Alright, let’s not discuss that for now. According to Su Moran’s memories, the Heartless Creed headquarters holds his life tablet. Once his soul leaves his body, his life tablet will shatter. The Heartless Creed’s higher-ups will then immediately abandon the headquarters and relocate their base.”

“I’ll open a spatial gate to the headquarters. With luck, we might still be in time.”

Everyone stepped through the spatial gate and arrived at the Heartless Creed headquarters—the bottom of Blue Dragon Lake in Yun Province.

Unfortunately, by the time they arrived, the Heartless Creed had long since evacuated. The entire lakebed had been relocated through mighty abilities, causing the Blue Dragon Lake’s water level to drop by several dozen meters.

“Then let’s go to their respective bases!”

Su Moran’s memories contained the locations of all the branches. The Vast Sea Daoist Lord immediately opened numerous spatial passageways, heading toward those corresponding branches.

Each Heartless Creed branch had experts stationed, the weakest being at the Nascent Soul Stage. However, such levels of cultivation were insignificant before the combined forces of the Dao-Seeking Sect and the imperial court.

Some branches held a higher status and possessed the means to contact the creed’s higher-ups directly. Upon learning of the vice creed leader’s capture, they immediately fled. These branches were extremely few, comprising only one-tenth of the total branches. The other ninety percent of the branches were uprooted by the Dao-Seeking Sect and the imperial court, with interrogations conducted through the night.

The situation for the remaining one-tenth of the branches wasn’t much better. They could run, but their speed was limited by their cultivation. Many were captured by the Fusion cultivators who rushed over.

The Heartless Creed’s foundation was shaken, its vitality severely damaged.

1. “Changhe” literally translates to long river. ☜

Chapter 823: A Whale Falls, All Things Rise

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s joint operation with the imperial court to eradicate the Heartless Creed created such a massive commotion that anyone with even the slightest intelligence network was aware of it.

The mighty cultivation experts were rendered speechless for a long time upon hearing the news. Some even slumped into their chairs, their faces filled with disbelief.

“That old Taciturn scoundrel reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage? How is that possible?”

The steward wore a conflicted expression. “It’s unknown whether it’s true or false, but I heard this news was deliberately spread by the Taciturn Daoist Priest himself.”

“...That does seem quite in character for him.”

“Back then, he formed his golden core one day earlier than me and flaunted it in my face. If he has really reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, how insufferably pompous would he become?”

“If even this grandson can become a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, there’s no reason I can’t.”

“Heaven has no eyes!”

“Seclusion! Seclusion!”

Similar scenes played out across the cultivation world. For a time, major figures were cursing Heaven’s lack of eyes while deciding to enter seclusion.

Even the Fusion cultivators in the Demon Region and the East Sea were no exception; they were all attempting to break through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

When Zhu Tian presided over the court assembly, he noticed that more than half his ministers were absent. Upon asking, he learned that they had all entered seclusion.

With the Taciturn Daoist Priest's advancement to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, the once bustling cultivation fell into a temporary lull. Perceptive individuals suddenly had a feeling that the Great Era was approaching. They feared that many Transcendent Tribulation cultivators would emerge after this collective seclusion.

“I heard there’s an adage in the East Sea: A whale falls, all things rise. It perfectly describes the current situation.”

“Doesn’t ‘a whale falls’ refer to a dead whale? The Taciturn Daoist Priest isn’t dead, is he?”

“We can pretend he is.”

Of course, the lull was only applicable to the upper echelons of the cultivation world. The cultivators who hadn’t reached the Fusion Stage weren’t very familiar with the Taciturn Daoist Priest and were largely unaffected.

~~~

Buddhist Kingdom.

In the skies above the boundless desert, a figure swooshed past, disappearing before the travelers riding their camels could have a glimpse. Immediately after, several more figures flew through the air, closely pursuing the first figure.

“Ye Zijin, stop right there! If I don’t bring you to justice today, how could I face our predecessors?!” Several renowned eminent monks from the Buddhist Kingdom were chasing Lu Yang’s Second Senior Brother, Ye Zijin. The group’s leader bore the Dharma name Puxuan.

After all, they were eminent monks and had clashed with Ye Zijin multiple times. After a series of struggles, they finally surrounded him.

“Ye Zijin, what have you scribbled in our predecessors’ works?!” The eminent monks glared at Ye Zijin furiously.

Aware that he couldn’t possibly defeat this group of monks, Ye Zijin hurriedly waved his hands to dissuade them. “Hey, hey, hey, please don’t resort to violence, no violence please. We’re all people who have left secular life. There’s no need for fighting and killing.

“I simply wrote two sentences. Look how worked up you all are.

“Annotating beside scriptures is our Buddhist Kingdom’s tradition. I, Ye Zijin, by any measure, can be considered a saintly monk. If you all can annotate our predecessors’ works, then I also have the right to annotate scriptures. What’s wrong with that?

“You all often say that Buddhist teachings are vast and profound, that even a lifetime of comprehension can only allow one to grasp the surface. In that case, there’s no problem with me praising that ‘Buddhist teachings are boundless,’ right?

“We Buddhist sects also often say, ‘Only now do I know I am myself.’ Doesn’t this mean that after cultivating Buddhism and a pursuit for a lifetime, the final answer ultimately lies within oneself? In that case, it isn’t wrong for me to write ‘Buddhist teachings are boundless; turning back leads to the shore.’”

“Nonsense! Your words clearly advise others to return to secular life! One of our Buddhist disciples saw your writing, achieved great ‘enlightenment,’ and returned to secular life!”

Ye Zijin quickly responded, “You can’t put it that way. That was due to his poor comprehension ability. You shouldn’t blame it on me.

“I, Ye Zijin, am wholeheartedly devoted to Buddhism. Everyone in the Buddhist Kingdom wants to inscribe their praise for me on a stele. How could I possibly encourage people to return to secular life?”

The eminent monks grew incensed. Everyone wants to inscribe their praise for you on a stele? Everyone clearly wants to inscribe a eulogy for you on a tombstone![1]

“Then what did you mean by placing a copy of Longevity Art that can grow one’s hair next to the scriptures?”

Ye Zijin replied, “Oh, you’re talking about that? I lost that book. Since you found it, could you return it to me?

“No offense, but look at all of you, always getting angry. Your daily heart and mind cultivation doesn’t seem to be going well. On the other hand, look at my shifu—that’s true major success in cultivation of the heart and mind. He’s always cheerful, and now he has even broken through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.”

Hearing Ye Zijin bring up the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s achievement in reaching the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, Master Puxuan’s veins bulged. He belonged to the same generation as the Taciturn Daoist Priest and didn’t expect the latter to be faster than him in advancing to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. The more he thought about it, the angrier he became, and his aura fluctuated violently. Gnashing his teeth, he recited scriptures.

“This aura... He’s about to advance to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage!” The other masters were overjoyed to detect Master Puxuan’s aura fluctuations. They rapidly formed a protective circle around him to guard his cultivation.

Ye Zijin’s eyelid twitched.

“What in the world? Why is he breaking through after a few words? Is breaking through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage that easy?”

While Master Puxuan was undergoing his tribulation and the other eminent monks were protecting him, unable to pay Ye Zijin any mind, the latter seized this chance to accelerate his escape from the desert.

“I need to find a place that Master Puxuan won’t discover. Speaking of which, now that he’s breaking through to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he probably won’t come after a junior like me anymore. If he seeks someone out, it should be my shifu.”

Ye Zijin placed a palm on his chest, radiating a benevolent glow that made him resemble a saintly monk. “Shifu, I believe you have few rivals after your advancement to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Your disciple is worried that you might be too lonely, so I’ve found you an opponent, giving you a bit of pressure as well. Since we’re master and disciple, there’s no need for thanks.”

~~~

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were still oblivious to the changes occurring in the outside world, nor did they care. Their cultivation was low, and they were merely minor characters. There was no need for them to know so much.

The two lived quite comfortably during their ten days in prison. The drafty roof was swiftly repaired by Ye City’s bailiffs skilled in earth-type spells. The pillars that collapsed during the battle were also fixed by bailiffs adept at wood-type spells.

“I never realized such convenient spells existed.” Lu Yang witnessed the entire repair process of the prison. Truly, every discipline has its own specialists. Although my cultivation surpasses these bailiffs, I’m far inferior in the technique of building prisons.

I can only “Draw Underground Prison,” which doesn’t even have a door.

During cultivation, the arrays helped to enhance their control over their internal spirit energy.

Food was also not a problem. Although the Innate Daoist Priest was exonerated and released, he didn’t return to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Instead, he remained in Ye City, delivering meals to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou every day, all purchased from the Blessed Fortune Restaurant—the finest restaurant in Ye City.

“Founding Ancestor, you’ve spent too much on us.” Lu Yang felt somewhat embarrassed, though he knew these spirit stones were insignificant to the Innate Daoist Priest.

The Innate Daoist Priest was not short on money. On the contrary, he could be described as exceedingly wealthy. The Dao-Seeking Sect had a retirement system, where retired elders received an annual sum of spirit stones.

This meant that the Innate Daoist Priest had 120,000 years of unclaimed pension. One could only imagine the staggering sum of spirit stones that represented. Among Fusion cultivators, hardly any were richer than the Innate Daoist Priest.

Ten days passed. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s seclusion in prison concluded, and they escorted the Innate Daoist Priest back to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

1. I tried to translate the wordplay, but I’m afraid it might not be obvious. The original idiom, which means something like “praised by anyone who has a mouth,” includes a character that can mean “gravestone.” The same character is used in the second sentence, but this time, it means to “erect a tombstone” instead. ☜

Chapter 824: Either You Come Back, Or I Go Over

“Big Senior Sister, we’re back!” Upon returning to the sect, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou immediately reported their safe return to Yun Zhi—primarily, to report the Innate Daoist Priest’s safety and prove they had completed the task Yun Zhi assigned.

“You returned ten days later than I anticipated. Did something unexpected happen along the way?” Yun Zhi was slightly puzzled. I heard from Shifu that the matter with the Founding Ancestor had been clarified with the Ye City authorities, and that the Founding Ancestor had been released long ago.

Why has it taken Little Junior Brother and Junior Brother Meng another ten days to escort the Founding Ancestor safely back to the Dao-Seeking Sect?

Lu Yang was too embarrassed to say that while the Innate Daoist Priest had indeed been released, the two of them had not.

“Y-yes, something unexpected happened along the way.”

Yun Zhi nodded, not dwelling further on the matter. In any case, encountering something unexpected along the way is quite in line with Little Junior Brother’s luck.

“You came back just in time. Senior Immortal Fairy, could you please come out for a moment?”

“What’s up?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy popped her head out, resting on Lu Yang’s shoulder and making it appear as if he had two heads.

Yun Zhi opened a wooden box. Inside lay a green peach with a small branch still attached. It resembled a flawless piece of art more than a fruit. “Immortal Fairy, is this peach the fruit of the World Natural Spiritual Root you mentioned, the one that has the shape of a peach tree?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was astonished to see the peach. “You actually found it! I thought it would take at least eight hundred or a thousand years to locate it.”

“What is this thing?” Meng Jingzhou whispered. Judging by Lu Yang’s expression, he figured Lu Yang knew some inside information.

“It’s considered a top-tier natural treasure. You know His Majesty has only a few years left to live. Big Senior Sister asked the Immortal Fairy if there were any lifespan-extending methods. The Immortal Fairy mentioned that in ancient times, there was a peach tree that was a world spirit root. The peaches it bore were innate longevity-enhancing treasures that could save His Majesty’s life.”

“Such a thing exists?” Even Meng Jingzhou, who was backed by the Meng Family, had never heard of such a treasure existing in the world. “So, His Majesty can be saved?” Meng Jingzhou was delighted. Although the First Imperial Prince could make a qualified emperor, it’s best to avoid a succession if possible, lest the political situation become tumultuous.

“The item is correct, but it probably isn’t ripe yet, right?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recalled that ripe peaches were pink.

“This is what I believed as well.” Having received confirmation, Yun Zhi closed the box. The peach hadn’t been fully plucked; the nutrients in the branch were sufficient to let the peach ripen. They would wait for the peach to ripen before delivering it to the imperial city.

“Speaking of which, where did you find the World Natural Spiritual Root?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked curiously.

Hearing this question, Yun Zhi’s expression faltered momentarily, flickering with a hint of discomfort. She hadn’t expected the World Natural Spiritual Root to be in the peach grove in her hometown. No wonder the spirit energy there was abnormally abundant. It seems it wasn’t solely due to the Mother-Child River.

“I discovered it by chance. That peach tree had already run away.”

“Alright.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt somewhat regretful. The World Natural Spiritual Root growing legs and running off wasn’t a first-time occurrence.

“And one more thing, Junior Brother Meng. This is a family letter sent to you. They also requested me to relay that they hope you can make a trip home.”

“Asking me to go home again.” Meng Jingzhou rolled his eyes. Given all the trouble I’ve stirred up, I don’t believe Dad can forgive me.

As long as Dad doesn’t say he forgives me, I absolutely won’t return home!

Meng Jingzhou opened the envelope and scanned its contents. The more he read, the paler his face became, and his hands even trembled.

“What’s wrong?” Lu Yang asked.

“The letter says that if I still don’t return home, my dad will personally make a trip to the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Rather than getting beaten up at the Dao-Seeking Sect, I suggest you go home and get beaten up there.

“Big Senior Sister, can we prohibit my dad from entering the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

Yun Zhi shook her head. “Our Dao-Seeking Sect doesn’t prohibit family members from entering to visit disciples.”

Meng Jingzhou agonized over it, scratching his head guiltily. It looks like I have no choice but to go back.

“Old Lu, you come back with me. With an outsider present, my dad probably won’t beat me up too badly.”

“Will that work?”

“It definitely will. My dad admires you so much that he even wanted you to marry my younger sister. He’ll surely give you face.” Although I don’t know whether it’ll work out, I’ll just drag Old Lu along first.

“Really?” Lu Yang couldn’t help but feel that Meng Jingzhou’s words weren’t trustworthy.

“Why would I lie to you?”

Lu Yang said seriously, “Considering how I often trick you, it would be quite normal for you to trick me a couple of times.”

“How can you say that with such self-righteous confidence? Just say whether you’re going or not.”

“I’ll go.” Given the rare opportunity to visit the imperial city, Lu Yang naturally wanted to go.

The last time he went to the imperial city was when he served as the acting sect leader. He had directly headed to the imperial palace to meet the Xia Emperor and the other four immortal sect leaders, so he hadn’t seen what it looked like beyond the palace walls.

Calling the imperial city a “cultivation holy land” was no exaggeration. It was a vibrant scene with cultivators of all backgrounds gathered here—the most powerful cultivators in the world, the most skilled artifact-refiners, the most adept pill-concocters were all in the imperial... No, wait, they all seem to be in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Should the two of us disguise ourselves?”

“What for?”

“Look, you’re from the Meng Family, I’m the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple, and the two of us are going to the imperial city together. I’m worried that we’ll get intercepted before we even get through the city gates.”

The two exchanged a glance, silently taking out their masks and transforming their appearances.

The old horse had long since returned from visiting relatives in the East Sea and was back in the Dao-Seeking Sect. Upon hearing that Meng Jingzhou was returning to the imperial city, he was also elated.

But he soon realized something was amiss. Meng Jingzhou returning alone is fine, but why is Lu Yang tagging along?

Nothing will happen in the imperial city, right...?

The old horse chuckled at himself, thinking he was overreacting. How could that be? That’s the impregnable imperial city, teeming with formidable experts. How could anything happen there?

“Yay! Let’s go to the imperial city, overthrow the Xia Emperor, and establish the Great Dou Dynasty!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was also thrilled to hear they were going to the imperial city.

To celebrate the imminent founding of the Great Dou Dynasty, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had shed her prison garb, washed up, and changed her clothes, donning a bright yellow imperial robe and an imperial crown with tassel beads. Her small face was tense, striving to appear dignified and solemn.

With a sweep of her hand, she removed the prison cage from the mental space, replacing it with a palace hall constructed from immortal stones. She sat regally upon the throne, as if she were seated high above the nine heavens, gazing down upon her sole subject—Lu Yang.

Lu Yang felt that even Gou Jian, who slept on firewood and tasted bitter gall,[1] hadn’t risen as swiftly as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Your subject, Lu Yang, pays respects to Your Majesty.”

“Say ‘Exalted Majesty,’” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy commanded.

Lu Yang was very compliant, correcting himself. “Exalted Majesty Lu Yang pays respects to Your Majesty.”

“Somehow, I feel like something should be embroidered on the robe,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mumbled. But embroidering dragons, phoenixes, qilins, or whatnot won’t reflect my true status. Little Ling, Lianyi, and the Qilin Immortal combined aren’t a match for me. Embroidering them on the imperial robe would degrade its value.

“Second-in-Command, what do you think should be embroidered on this immortal’s imperial robe?” The founding Dou Emperor inquired of her Chief Eunuch, Lu Yang.

“Your Majesty, imperial robes have always been embroidered with images of the strongest,” Lu Yang reminded.

Realization dawned upon the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. She immediately began embroidering the imperial robe with her mind.

“Done.”

Lu Yang looked and saw that the imperial robe was embroidered with images of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy herself and Yun Zhi.

1. The story of King Gou Jian of Yue goes that he was captured by the enemy. To seek revenge, he endured countless hardships, including sleeping on firewood and tasting bitter gall to spur himself on. Eventually, the Yue state grew stronger and defeated the Wu state. The simple meaning of the idiom is “working hard and enduring hardship now to achieve success in the long term.” ☜

Chapter 825: Eldest Young Master Meng Returns Home

Lu Yang bit back his words, hesitating to say the imperial robe looked rather odd. “Immortal Fairy, are you sure what you embroidered on the imperial robe is you and Big Senior Sister?” He looked at the robe, genuinely unsure who the two figures on it were supposed to be.

“Of course. Aren’t the names written right here?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked down and pointed at two spots on the imperial robe.

Lu Yang thought, Thank goodness you wrote the names. Otherwise, even if you say that what you embroidered on the imperial robe is Old Meng and me, I would believe it.

“Xiao Yangzi, didn’t you say that imperial robes have always been embroidered with images of the strongest? If we talk about who’s the strongest in today’s cultivation world, it’s naturally Lass Yun and me!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy puffed out her chest, her expression and tone brimming with pride.

“...Why are you calling me ‘Xiao Yangzi?’”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked utterly perplexed. “What’s wrong with that? I heard that’s how emperors call the people (eunuchs) around them.”[1]

Lu Yang, “...”

Never mind. There’s no need to explain something so complicated to the Immortal Fairy.

“Then shall I make slight modifications to the embroidery of you and Big Senior Sister on the imperial robe?” Lu Yang couldn’t bear to look at the two figures on the imperial robe.

“Sure.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy immediately took off the imperial robe and tossed it to Lu Yang, then started running barefoot in circles around the great hall.

Lu Yang used his will to materialize golden and silver threads, threading a needle with them. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s exquisitely beautiful face soon appeared on the imperial robe.

“Hmm, it’s indeed a teeny bit better than this immortal’s skill.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rarely admitted that Lu Yang was superior at something.

Lu Yang was unperturbed despite the honor, continuing to embroider Yun Zhi. Soon, an image of her also appeared on the imperial robe.

Just as Lu Yang was about to praise the Everlasting Immortal Fairy a couple more times to solidify his position as Chief Eunuch, a rift appeared in the mental space.

It was Yun Zhi.

Her gaze fell upon Lu Yang, the needle and thread in his hands, and the imperial robe resting on his thighs. A rare twitch flickered at the corner of her eye.

“Little Junior Brother, you...”

Startled, Lu Yang hastily stood up to declare his innocence. “It has nothing to do with me! The Immortal Fairy made me do it!””

“Hey, wasn’t it you who suggested embroidering Lass Yun and me on the imperial robe?”

“Immortal Fairy, don’t speak nonsense. I didn’t say anything.”

Hearing Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy shifting blame back and forth, Yun Zhi roughly figured out the course of events.

“Immortal Fairy, have you considered changing the style of the imperial robe?” Yun Zhi kindly suggested, subtly hinting that this “thing” didn’t quite resemble an imperial robe.

“Change the style?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pondered briefly and suddenly saw the light. “You’re saying that since this immortal is the number one powerhouse in the world, only I should be embroidered on the imperial robe!”

Yun Zhi sighed softly. “Never mind. Let the imperial robe be as it is.” After all, there’s no one else in the mental space. The Immortal Fairy can wear whatever she pleases.

After Yun Zhi left, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy excitedly put on the robe and spun around happily, boasting to Xiao Yangzi. “Well? Well? Isn’t it beautiful?”

Xiao Yangzi bowed. “Your Exalted Majesty is innately beautiful. This imperial robe merely serves to highlight your appearance.”

~~~

In the past, when Lu Yang wanted to head to the Demon Region or the East Sea, he needed to find someone who had been there to ask about the local situation. This time, with Meng Jingzhou, a local, accompanying him, Lu Yang didn’t need to ask around.

“It’s a pity that Junior Sister Tao and the others have all gone to eradicate the Heartless Creed.”

Originally, Lu Yang had wanted to invite Tao Yaoye and Man Gu to the Buddhist Kingdom. Upon asking around, he learned that the situation with the Heartless Creed had changed so drastically that virtually no one in the Dao-Seeking Sect was idle. Every last person had been pulled in to handle the Heartless Creed’s aftermath.

On the other hand, Li Haoran hadn’t gone out. He was focused on comprehending artifact-refinement techniques and shouldn’t be disturbed.

With the old horse pulling the two along, they reached the imperial city in two days.

As the largest city in Great Xia and the entire cultivation world, the imperial city’s land mass was beyond imagination. From far away, Lu Yang could see several colossal dark shadows within the imperial city—mountains situated inside the city.

A river hundreds of zhang wide bisected the imperial city, dividing it into the southern city and the northern city.

This was Lu Yang’s second time visiting the imperial city, yet he was still awestruck.

At the city gates, Lu Yang saw many cultivators from the demon race, sea tribes, and the Buddhist Kingdom. Their attire and appearance greatly differed from those of the Central Continent and were instantly recognizable. Such cultivators were rare in other cities but were everywhere in the imperial city. To travel from other continents to Great Xia, these cultivators had to be at least at the Nascent Soul Stage.

When the soldiers at the city gates saw Meng Jingzhou’s proof of identity, their eyes contracted sharply.

THE Eldest Young Master Meng has actually returned to the imperial city?!

The soldiers watched the carriage enter the city. Out of professional integrity, they didn’t report Meng Jingzhou’s entry to their superiors.

Meng Jingzhou wasn’t a wanted criminal; there was no need to report it.

And the one who came to the imperial city with Eldest Young Master Meng is the legendary disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest?

The carriage stopped before a wooden plaque inscribed with the characters “Meng Estate.”

In the lower right corner of the plaque was a name—Jiang Ping’an. The first Xia Emperor had bestowed his calligraphy upon the Meng Estate, and this was no less significant than a golden death-exemption token.

“We’re here. This is my house.” Meng Jingzhou jumped off the carriage and gazed at the entrance gate he hadn’t seen for a long time, filled with myriad emotions.

Almost six years have passed since I ran away from home. Finally, I’ve returned.

“This is your house?!” Lu Yang disembarked and saw the Meng Estate gate, which towered like the legendary Southern Heavenly Gate on Mount Tai. The vermillion door panels were engraved with intricate, exquisite patterns. Two stone lions at the entrance held stone balls in their mouths, looking almost alive. The steps were carved from premium-grade spirit stones, their edges adorned with auspicious clouds and mythical beasts.

Even the imperial palace’s gates couldn’t be more imposing than this.

Even one of the imperial city’s mountains he had seen from afar was located within the Meng Estate.

“Is this wooden plaque written by the first Xia Emperor?” Lu Yang noticed the name of the calligrapher. The Meng Family was certainly qualified. After all, they were the other major contender for supremacy against the Xia Emperor.

“This is nothing. The imperial palace’s wooden plaque was written by my family’s old ancestor.”

When the two guards at the entrance saw Meng Jingzhou step down from the carriage, they were so flabbergasted that they stammered. One guard immediately ran inside to inform the head of the family. “Y-Young Master has returned!”

“Oh yo? It’s still the two of you guarding the gate.” Meng Jingzhou clearly recognized these two guards.

In the past, he couldn’t discern their cultivation levels. Now, he could tell they were both at the Advanced Divine Transfiguration Stage.

The remaining guard smiled sheepishly. “You jest, Young Master. It’s only been a few years. Not everyone can improve their cultivation as rapidly as you have.”

Meng Jingzhou was about to say more when his expression shifted. He sensed a terrifying oppressive aura spreading from within the Meng Estate.

“Young rascal, you’ve finally come back!”

A middle-aged man suddenly appeared before Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. Lu Yang hadn’t even seen how he arrived.

“D-Dad, I’m back.” Meng Jingzhou guiltily avoided his father’s eyes.

Seeing his son after so long, Meng Potian laughed heartily, patting Meng Jingzhou on the shoulder. “Good, it’s good that you’re back.”

Hearing his father’s normal tone, Meng Jingzhou surmised that his father had truly forgiven him. He finally dared to look up and meet his father’s gaze, sincerely calling out, “Dad.”

“Dirty laundry should not be aired in public. Your father is gratified to see that you’ve returned to receive your beating.”

1. If it’s not obvious, xiao (little) + character + zi is how eunuchs are often addressed. ☜

Chapter 826: A Good Brother Stabs Two Knives Into The Ribs

Upon hearing this, Meng Jingzhou’s face changed drastically, and he attempted to defuse the crisis with words.

“Dad, we’re still outside.”

“No big deal.”

With a sweep of his hand, Meng Potian brought both Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou inside the Meng Estate.

The old horse snorted and had the two guards unharness the carriage. He then leisurely strolled into the Meng Estate to catch up with his second brother, Xu You.

“I haven’t been back to the Meng Estate in ages. Where does Second Brother live again?”

~~~

Meng Potian took Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to the main courtyard. In Meng Jingzhou’s childhood, aside from climbing mountains, Meng Jingzhou had liked this place the most.

But now, he felt it wasn’t necessary to come here to reminisce about his childhood.

“Dad, there’s still an outsider present.” Meng Jingzhou once again tried to reason with his father.

I was insensible when I was a kid and deliberately made many mistakes, but so many years have passed. Even I, the involved party, have forgotten about it. Why can’t my father let it go?

“You must be Lu Yang. A handsome and talented man indeed.” Meng Potian’s tone softened slightly when facing Lu Yang. “I’ve long heard Little Zhou praise you for having the makings of the Taciturn Daoist Priest, capable of stirring up a string of incidents every time you go out.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Old Meng, so you’ve been spinning tales and talking bad about me behind my back, huh? Were you not right there beside me every time I went out?

Meng Potian continued, “The Battle of the Great Era precisely needs geniuses like you.

“I heard you don’t have a Dao partner yet. Your shifu is the Taciturn Daoist Priest, so there’s certainly no one who dares to become your Dao partner. Coincidentally, my daughter is sixteen, pure, and lovely—a perfect match for you. I think our two families can arrange a betrothal.”

Before Lu Yang could refute, he saw Meng Potian turn toward Meng Jingzhou with a stern face, his tone icy and eerie.

“Alright, there are no outsiders now.”

Seeing Meng Potian raise the iron ruler to discipline Meng Jingzhou, Lu Yang couldn’t bear to see his good brother get beaten and took a step forward. “Uncle Meng, please wait a moment.”

Meng Jingzhou was deeply moved. He’s my good brother after all; true friendship does show itself in times of adversity.

Meng Potian turned his head, not understanding why Lu Yang had stopped him.

“Old Meng must have committed deeds that angered Heaven and men, but he’s just one person. Punishing him alone might not be satisfying.

“It so happens that I know a move called ‘One Meng Into Ten Thousand Mengs.’ I can create ten thousand Meng Jingzhous, guaranteeing that you will have an utterly satisfying disciplining session, Uncle Meng.”

Executing One Meng Into Ten Thousand Mengs was far more difficult than One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords, for it placed extremely high demands on both spirit energy and spirit consciousness strength.

But that was not a problem. Lu Yang could temporarily boost his spirit energy by consuming pills. As for the strength of his spiritual consciousness, he could temporarily borrow some from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

Meng Potian was overjoyed to hear this. He hadn’t expected Lu Yang to know such a technique and outright told Lu Yang to go ahead and unleash it without restraint.

Lu Yang didn’t stand on ceremony. Dragging Meng Jingzhou by the ankle, he began performing the sword technique.

“Damn it, Old Lu, your grandfather—”

“One Meng Into Ten Thousand Mengs!” Lu Yang shouted, cutting off Meng Jingzhou’s last words

Meng Potian sensed something and looked up. Seeing the sky densely filled with his son, he grabbed his iron ruler and flew up to start beating them.

Meng Jingzhou’s blood-curdling screams reverberated through the skies above the Meng Estate, quite sweet-sounding to the ear. Lu Yang quickly captured this scene with a recording orb.

Not long after, Meng Jingzhou rubbed his backside as he fell down and began walking with a limp.

“Exhilarating!” Meng Potian found Lu Yang more pleasing to the eye the more he looked at him. He's the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple after all; he has learned some real skills.

Meng Jingzhou’s return caused a huge commotion. Soon, the direct branch of the Meng Family all came to the main courtyard to watch the spectacle.

“Jingzhou, you’re finally back! You have no idea how much your mom missed you. She stayed home all day, afraid she wouldn’t be here when you got back...” The first to arrive in the courtyard was a man who looked around thirty years old.

“Then where is my mom now?”

“She’s been at the imperial palace for several days.”

Meng Jingzhou sighed and introduced the man to Lu Yang. “This is my second uncle, Meng Poli.”

“Greetings, Second Uncle Meng.”

Meng Poli said, “Hey, this kid is way more polite than you, Jingzhou. You’ve never called me that.”

Meng Jingzhou rolled his eyes. “Second Uncle, have you forgotten that time you got drunk and insisted on swearing brotherhood with the stone lions at the entrance, saying you were the eldest brother and that the pair of stone lions were the second and third brothers? You even said that I should call the stone lions ‘Second Uncle’ and not you.”

Meng Poli’s face flushed red, and he coughed guiltily. “Ahem, words spoken while drunk don’t count.”

“Jingzhou is back?” A gentle, elegant voice sounded. The person looked identical to Meng Poli, but his demeanor was completely different. He clearly looked like a man devoted to scholarly pursuits.

“This is my third uncle, Meng Poci. He and my second uncle are twins. Do you remember me telling you I have an uncle stationed at the Demon Confinement Pass? That’s him.”

Lu Yang had a vague recollection. When he and Meng Jingzhou were thrown by Yun Zhi to the jungle at the border between Great Xia and the Demon Region, they had gone to the Demon Suppression Pass. At the time, Meng Jingzhou had regretfully said that he had an uncle at the Demon Confinement Pass, wishing the two of them had been thrown there instead.

“Third Uncle, why have you returned from the Demon Confinement Pass?”

Meng Poci showed none of the iron-blooded aura of a general guarding the border. He more closely resembled a great Confucian scholar from an academy. A faint smile tugged at the corner of his lips. “I guarded the Demon Confinement Pass for fifty years. Last year, the imperial court issued an order for me to be replaced.”

“That’s a good thing.” Meng Jingzhou smiled, surmising that after Great Xia established diplomatic relations with the Demon Region, they had recalled his particularly formidable third uncle to ease tensions.

“Elder Brother, you’re finally back?” A graceful figure suddenly ran out from somewhere, excitedly rushing up to Meng Jingzhou.

“Little Sister!” Meng Jingzhou beamed joyfully, ruffling his little sister’s hair and messing it up.

If anyone in the Meng Family has treated me best, it has to be my little sister. When I ran away from home without any money, it was my kind-hearted little sister who gave me a storage ring. I could freely squander the treasures inside, and they still haven't been used up yet.

“This is my younger sister, Meng Jingyu.”

“Greetings, Lu Yang-gege.” Meng Jingyu smiled sweetly. She was indeed as pure and lovely as Meng Potian had mentioned.

“Ah, what a good girl. Here, this is a gift from Lu Yang-gege.” It was the first time Lu Yang had encountered someone calling him “gege.” The people he had interacted with before were either peers or cultivators of surprisingly advanced age.

Lu Yang took out a wooden sword from his identity jade tablet. He had carved it while practicing the Sword Dao, modeling it after the Qingfeng Sword. It was capable of piercing through Divine Transfiguration cultivators.

“Thank you, Gege.” Meng Jingyu carefully received it, displaying excellent manners. Her politeness made Lu Yang sigh inwardly. She and Old Meng seem to be from entirely different species.

“My elder brother’s letters always mention the adventures he encountered with you when traveling. Lu Yang-gege, are all your training journeys outside so thrilling?” Meng Jingyu looked at Lu Yang with worshipful admiration. She had never left the imperial city and was especially fascinated by Lu Yang’s various experiences.

“What exactly did he say?”

“My elder brother said you often stir up trouble—like going astray and voluntarily joining the Everlasting Creed, forcing him to destroy the creed to save you; taking pleasure in challenging Foundation Establishment cultivators at the Golden Core Stage; and having endless peach blossom romantic luck, yet being unaffected by all spells and thus making it useless on you.”

Lu Yang’s expression remained unchanged. He simply chuckled dryly twice.

Chapter 827: The Origin of Meng Potian’s Name

“By the way, where’s Grandpa?” Meng Jingzhou waited half a day but didn’t see his grandfather. Grandpa dotes on me the most. If he were here, Dad definitely wouldn’t dare to beat me like this.

“He’s in seclusion. No telling when he’ll emerge.” Meng Potian added, “Alright, no matter what, Little Zhou returning home is a good thing. I’ve ordered people to prepare a meal. Let’s gather as a family.”

The “family” Meng Potian spoke of naturally included Lu Yang, who had joined at the last minute.

True to being the cultivation world’s number one ancestral clan, the Meng Family’s wealth was astounding. The table was laden with delicacies crafted from precious ingredients, many of which even Lu Yang couldn’t identify.

“Come on, help yourself. These are all beneficial for cultivation.” Meng Potian urged Lu Yang not to stand on ceremony and to treat this place as his own home.

“These are considered delicious? Let this immortal show the Meng Family some skills.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rolled up the sleeves of her imperial robe, ready to display her prowess, but Lu Yang hastily stopped her.

“Your Exalted Majesty’s body is worth a thousand pieces of gold. Since ancient times, there has never been a precedent for an emperor cooking.”

“There’s such a thing? How troublesome,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy grumbled, considering whether to simply abdicate and let Xiao Yangzi become the next Dou Emperor.

But upon second thought, she felt that Xiao Yangzi was too young and inexperienced. It isn’t time for him to succeed the throne yet.

“Consider the Meng Family unlucky for missing out on this immortal’s culinary skills.”

After placating the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Lu Yang could finally enjoy the meal in peace.

Lu Yang wondered what cultivation level the Meng Family’s spirit chef possessed. It was Lu Yang’s first time eating such sumptuous spirit cuisine. A single bite of venison warmed his whole body. Upon sensing it carefully, one could detect their cultivation slowly improving.

In fact, the effects of this spirit meal went far beyond that. Lu Yang’s cultivation talent was too high, and he had never encountered a bottleneck thus far. If a cultivator stuck at a bottleneck for a long time consumed this meal, their bottleneck would vanish without a trace, allowing them to advance to the next cultivation realm smoothly.

One could only wonder what other stories Meng Jingzhou had told his younger sister about Lu Yang. Meng Jingyu was especially curious about Lu Yang’s experiences, unable to resist constantly asking him questions even during the meal.

“Lu Yang-gege, can you tell me how you ended up joining the Everlasting Creed back then?

“Lu Yang-gege, I heard you formed your golden core faster than Elder Brother. What kind of golden core did you form?

“Can you really help people shave their heads?”

Lu Yang felt that he had been too lenient in assisting Meng Potian when he disciplined Meng Jingzhou earlier.

“Little Sister Jingyu, you have already drawn qi into your body?” Lu Yang noticed spirit energy fluctuations from Meng Jingyu. Although she wasn’t sixteen yet, starting cultivation a few months early was no issue.

“I’m already at the Qi Training Stage.” Meng Jingyu smiled proudly. Among her peers, she was the first to guide qi into her body. According to common parlance, she was at the Level Two Qi Training Stage.

After the welcome banquet concluded, Meng Potian ordered the servants to arrange a small courtyard for Lu Yang. Meng Jingzhou was next door, and beyond that was Meng Jingyu.

This clearly wasn’t the guest quarters but a place where only the Meng Family members had the right to reside.

“Your courtyard is quite clean.” Lu Yang smiled. Old Meng hasn’t been home for six years, yet the courtyard remains spotless, which goes to show the Meng Family’s care for him.

“Of course! After all, I am the Eldest Young Master. There must be someone cleaning here daily.” Meng Jingzhou grinned and walked into the courtyard, only to be deflected back by a force.

“What’s going on?” Lu Yang was surprised. Is the imperial city so dangerous? You can get attacked even within the Meng Estate?

“Damn it, who put a Spotless Incantation in my courtyard?” Meng Jingzhou was furious. This was clearly the effect of a Spotless Incantation, capable of repelling any foreign object from the courtyard.

Foreign objects included him, the owner of this very courtyard.

The fact that this Spotless Incantation could repel even me, a Double Infants old monster, indicates its high quality.

Meng Jingzhou tore off the Spotless Incantation posted at the entrance and successfully entered the courtyard.

The place Lu Yang stayed was likely cleaned daily. Not only was it clean, but it also didn’t have a Spotless Incantation.

Having settled their accommodations, Meng Jingzhou suggested giving Lu Yang a tour of the Meng Estate.

“This is the Martial Training Hall. Both direct and collateral branches of the Meng Family can cultivate here.”

On the arena stages, cultivators clashed with spells and mighty abilities. Although they couldn’t compare to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, they were considered quite remarkable among cultivators of the same cultivation realm.

“These people are the future of the Meng Family. Our family has invested tremendous effort to nurture them, ensuring their cultivation bears fruit. Once their cultivation yields success, they can begin handling various family affairs, like loan issuance and debt collection.

“I heard my father and uncles also cultivated in this martial Training Hall back in the day. The lecturers here are all at the Fusion Stage.

“This is the academy. I possessed a lot of cultivation knowledge before joining the Dao-Seeking Sect, right? I learned it all here.”

The sound of students reading aloud echoed from within the academy. Through the window, Lu Yang saw Meng Jingyu swaying her head as she read, studying assiduously.

There were also places like the Pill Concoction Chambers, Artifact Refinement Chambers, and the Accounting Office. All the hundred arts of cultivation could find expression within the Meng Family, whose comprehensiveness was not inferior to the Dao-Seeking Sect’s.

“I can’t take you into this mountain; even I can’t enter.” Meng Jingzhou brought Lu Yang to the foot of the mountain. Its peak soared into the clouds and was no less imposing than Heaven’s Gate Peak.

“It’s said that this mountain is inhabited by the mighty experts of our Meng Family. I just don’t know how many are at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.”

Before Meng Jingzhou began cultivating, he only knew that the Meng Family’s mighty experts stayed in the mountain, unsure of their cultivation realms. Now, with his broadened perspective and clear understanding of the Meng Family’s status as the number one ancestral clan, he believed the mountain housed Transcendent Tribulation experts, and more than one at that. Otherwise, given the Meng Family’s usual conduct, it would be difficult for them to establish a footing in the imperial city, let alone the cultivation world.

“Although I can’t take you in now, don’t worry. After I become the family head in the future, I promise to take you up the mountain for a tour.”

Lu Yang looked at Meng Jingzhou skeptically. “Someone with a Single’s Spirit Root can become the family head?”

A family head without a wife and children—how utterly selfless would that be?

Meng Jingzhou was extremely confident. “What are you saying? Once this young master becomes an immortal, why would a Single’s Spirit Root matter?”

“Single’s Spirit Immortal Root?”

“Get lost.”

“Speaking of which, your father’s name is quite domineering. Did your grandfather give it to him?” Lu Yang recalled that among the people he knew, no one had such an imposing name. They’re either called Huang Doudou or Bu Yaolian—names that clearly don’t sound like those of formidable powerhouses.

“It was indeed given by my grandpa, but the name’s meaning might be different from what you’re imagining.”

“How so?”

“My grandpa told me that on the day my father was born, the imperial city experienced a once-in-a-century downpour. My grandma also had a difficult labor and struggled to give birth to my dad.

“My grandpa couldn’t help out and could only pace around the courtyard. With the rain pouring then, his mood was particularly foul, and he cursed loudly, ‘Give me a break, Heaven! What kind of rotten weather is this?!”

“Coincidentally, right after my grandpa finished cursing, my dad was born.

“To commemorate that moment, my grandpa named my dad Meng Potian—break Heaven.”[1]

1. On the surface, the name Potian translates to “breaking the heavens.” The original Chinese sentence two paragraphs above is basically just “What kind of rotten weather is this?!” The character “po,” which means “to break,” can also mean “rotten/crappy.” The word for weather is “tianqi,” and “tian” means “sky” or “heaven.” In this particular sentence, the characters “po” and “tian” happened to end up side by side. Essentially, the reason for the name is completely different from what people would normally guess. ☜

Chapter 828: Battle of Riches

Though it was rather impolite, Lu Yang genuinely believed that Grandpa Meng’s education level might not be much higher than Man Gu’s.

They might even be on par.

“Then Meng Poci and Meng Poli... Never mind, I won’t ask.” Lu Yang felt that they were elders after all. It’d be discourteous of me to inquire about such matters. If Old Meng leaks too many secrets, the Meng Family might kick him out of the estate.

“What place is that over there?” Lu Yang pointed to a restricted room, guarded by a Meng Family elder at the entrance. It looked like a forbidden ground.

“Where the debt notes are stored. My dad told me that if all these could be cashed, they could buy half the imperial city.”

Lu Yang drew a sharp breath. No wonder it’s a forbidden ground. No amount of personnel guarding this place would be excessive.

“Not just debt notes are stored there. Our Meng Family has a mighty ability called ‘Borrowing Spell.’ When a cultivator at the Fusion Stage or above borrows money from us, they must not only leave a debt note but also lend us one of their techniques.

“Our family will then imprint that technique onto paper. In battle, we can replicate that person’s move.”

“So impressive.” Lu Yang hadn’t heard of anyone else knowing this mighty ability. It’s probably unique to the Meng Family.

Even the Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head, saying she hadn’t heard of it.

~~~

Meng Potian, the old horse, and Chief Steward Xu You gathered together. The three brothers hadn’t met for nearly six years and shared a casual drink in a side room.

The old horse lounged lazily on a wooden chair, using spells to bring the fresh grass from a plate to his mouth. His hoof held a wine cup, taking occasional sips.

“Old Horse, looking after little Zhou throughout the whole journey must have been tough.”

The old horse initially wanted to politely say it wasn’t tough, but recalling the six years of harrowing experiences, he simply couldn’t manage a carefree smile and utter the words “not tough.”

“Not tough—just a tough life.”

Meng Potian, “...”

I remember Old Horse used to be quite modest. Why has he become like this after acting as my son’s guardian?

“What do you think of the kid Lu Yang?” Meng Potian had a favorable impression of Lu Yang. He had seen many talented youths, but whether in terms of cultivation or character, none surpassed Lu Yang.

If Lu Yang and Little Yu take a fancy to each other, he can marry into the family.

The old horse’s eye twitched. Unpleasant memories flooded his mind as he suddenly recalled the scene where Lu Yang inadvertently resurrected the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Let me put it this way. Your Meng Family’s debt notes can buy half the imperial city, right?”

“Yes.”

“His luck can destroy half the imperial city.”

~~~

“Shall we eat something delicious?” Meng Jingzhou asked.

Lu Yang was puzzled. “Haven’t we eaten during the welcome banquet? I thought it was quite tasty.”

“Those aren’t the tastiest. Those spirit dishes try to balance taste and effect, but you can’t have the best of both worlds, so they fall short compared to true delicacies. I’m taking you to the most delicious place in the imperial city.” After all, the imperial city was Meng Jingzhou’s turf. He wanted to fulfil his duty as host.

“Let’s go then.” Lu Yang grinned. He remembered that Yun Zhi liked sampling local cuisine wherever she went. If it was truly as delicious as Meng Jingzhou claimed, he could pack some to take away when leaving the imperial city.

Considering Meng Jingzhou’s reputation in the imperial city, where everyone knew him, the two donned masks as they left the Meng Estate.

The place Meng Jingzhou proposed was called the Heavenly Fragrance Restaurant, the most luxurious restaurant in the imperial city. There were even rumors that it had a Transcendent Tribulation spirit chef, though that spirit chef hadn’t personally cooked in decades.

Heavenly Fragrance Restaurant was teeming with people. Fortunately, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou weren’t too late; there were still three empty tables remaining when they arrived. By the time they sat and ordered, the two remaining empty tables were also occupied.

“It really is delicious.” After the dishes were served, Lu Yang took a bite. Old Meng really didn’t lie. This is even better than what we ate at the Meng Estate.

“Of course. How could this young master have poor taste?” Meng Jingzhou was smug and eagerly dug in. He hadn’t eaten here in five or six years.

Perhaps those in the same profession were naturally at odds; the Everlasting Immortal Fairy turned her nose up at the dishes in Heavenly Fragrance Restaurant.

While Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou ate and discussed their next steps, they noticed some commotion at the restaurant entrance and couldn’t help but glance over.

A young man dressed in black, with an extraordinary bearing, walked in with his arm around a female companion, showing no regard for public decorum. Two guards followed behind him.

Lu Yang noticed the young man’s black robe was woven from dark gold silk spun by Ice-Mountain Silkworms, impervious to water and fire, and invulnerable to blades and spears; it was extremely rare. Even in the imperial city that was teeming with descendants of officials, few had the right to wear such clothing.

“No more seats?” The young man frowned. The restaurant was too crowded, with not even a single empty seat remaining.

He walked directly to one of the tables and stared down at the patrons sitting there. “This spot is taken by this young master now. Get lost.”

That table’s patrons seemed to realize the young man wasn’t to be trifled with. They hastily lowered their heads in affirmation and vacated the spot.

The young man glanced at the relatively simple dishes on Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s table and sneered. “Paupers shouldn’t come here.”

Then he beckoned. “Waiter, bring me a pot of Hundred-Year Divine Immortal Brew!”

Hearing the young man’s tone, the other diners were startled.

A regular pot of Divine Immortal Brew cost as much as a small family’s annual income in the imperial city. A century-old vintage’s value was unimaginably high. Even though the restaurant’s clientele was wealthy or noble, few could order the hundred-year version.

Seeing the young man’s extravagance, his female companion’s beautiful eyes sparkled. She pressed herself closer to him, deliberately rubbing her chest against his arm.

Meng Jingzhou snorted coldly. I’ve never seen anyone flaunting their wealth right in front of me.

As for flaunting a female companion, that’s going even more overboard.

He immediately beckoned the waiter. “Bring this young master a pot of Hundred-Year Divine Immortal Brew as well.”

The young man pretended as if he hadn’t heard Meng Jingzhou and continued ordering. “Cloud-Mist Steamed Spirit Fish, ten-year aged. One year less and I’ll tear your restaurant down!”

Meng Jingzhou ordered in a similar fashion, not even looking at the price. “Waiter, one Cloud-Mist Steamed Spirit Fish, ten-year aged.”

The young man glanced at Meng Jingzhou. An unfamiliar face—probably a foreign cultivator coming to the imperial city to seek connections. He sneered and deliberately ordered expensive dishes. “Blanched Five-Elements Spirit Vegetables, Red-Braised Sun-Crowing Chicken, Supreme Clarity Soul-Refining Porridge...”

“We’ll also have Blanched Five-Elements Spirit Vegetables, Red-Braised Sun-Crowing Chicken, Supreme Clarity Soul-Refining Porridge...”

Meng Jingzhou hadn’t originally wanted to order these. Although they were highly nutritious, their taste didn’t compare to what he initially ordered. But I don’t mind playing along with this young man.

Whatever dish the young man ordered, Meng Jingzhou ordered the same, without backing down an inch. The young man no longer felt the unique sense of superiority above the masses and instead felt that he had lost face in front of his female companion.

He slammed the table. “Waiter, let me ask you, what is the most expensive thing here?!”

The waiter hesitated, then cautiously said, “Honored guest, the most expensive thing here is our rent.”

Chapter 829: Meng Jingzhou’s Fearsome Reputation

“Who asked you about your rent?!” The young man raged. Why would I ask you about your rent? What use is renting this crappy place?

The waiter was likely intimidated by the young man’s demeanor and began to stammer. “H-honored guest, you didn’t ask clearly. I-I didn’t know you couldn’t afford the rent.”

“You!”

The young man was too ostentatious, quickly drawing the attention of other diners.

“Isn’t that Li Zhuo, the Left Chancellor’s youngest grandson?”

“He is Li Zhuo, one of the Imperial City’s Four Young Masters? I heard the Left Chancellor is particularly fond of this grandson.”

“Goodness, then the person competing with Li Zhuo in wealth is in for big trouble, isn’t he?”

“You don’t say! Who in the imperial city dares to vie with Li Zhuo for the spotlight?”

“And that waiter is probably going to suffer too.”

Lu Yang wasn’t clear about prices in the imperial city and curiously asked from the side, “Is Heavenly Fragrance Restaurant’s rent very expensive? Why does he look like he can’t afford it?”

Meng Jingzhou yawned in boredom beside him. “He’s a pauper after all; it’s understandable. He just likes to pretend to be a big shot and show off in front of his female companion. By tightening his belt a bit, he could scrounge up some money for a pot of wine and a few small dishes. But this rent? Even if he snaps his spine from tightening his belt, he wouldn’t be able to afford it. Waiter, I’ll pay one year’s rent for your Heavenly Fragrance Restaurant!”

The waiter was overjoyed and rushed to serve at Meng Jingzhou’s table, massaging his shoulders and legs. “Many thanks, dear guest!”

Li Zhuo’s face flushed red, then turned pale. He was extremely concerned with his pride and image. Despite being flamboyant in his actions, he had never been humbled—until now. He could even feel that the gazes of those who had recognized him and previously held him in reverence had begun to change.

He quickly calculated how many spirit stones he could muster. “Isn’t it just a year of rent? I’ll pay the Heavenly Fragrance Restaurant’s rent for two years!”

The waiter was ecstatic, running over to Li Zhuo’s side to massage his shoulders and legs with practiced movements.

“Three years,” Meng Jingzhou said lazily, not even lifting an eyelid. This was small change to him.

The waiter promptly switched sides again, hurrying back to Meng Jingzhou.

“Three and a half... Four years!” Li Zhuo truly didn’t dare to take out that many spirit stones, but he felt that saying “half a year” would make him lose face, so he added another half a year.

“Five years. In addition, put today’s entire tab for everyone on me,” Meng Jingzhou said offhandedly. He was in a good mood from eating and felt like spending however he pleased.

The waiter ran back and forth, wishing he could split into a clone to massage both bankrollers simultaneously.

Li Zhuo was so infuriated that he wanted to curse. Where did this parvenu come from? Once I find out his identity later, he can forget about clinching a single business deal in the imperial city!

“Six years!” He narrowed his eyes, staring at Meng Jingzhou's face, overcome with revulsion. “Wait. I can produce this many spirit stones. Can you? Since you just shouted ‘five years,’ you need to prove you have that many spirit stones!”

Meng Jingzhou scoffed. “Forget five years’ rent, I could even pay for six. I just can’t be bothered to compete with you.”
