“You said it yourself!” Li Zhuo refused to believe it. This person can produce that many spirit stones? Even for me, taking out that many spirit stones at once is a significant strain.

“Go summon a Meng Family member to collect the rent!” Li Zhuo ordered his guards. The Heavenly Fragrance Restaurant was a property of the Meng Family. I’ll also use this chance to send a guard to fetch more spirit stones from home; I don’t have that many on hand.

Not long after, Chief Steward Xu You arrived. He was usually the one who collected the rent from Heavenly Fragrance Restaurant.

With a pained expression, Li Zhuo pulled out a storage ring and handed it to Xu You. He had painstakingly scraped together this sum from various sources to cover the six years’ rent. If his father and grandfather learned of his actions today, they would likely fly into a rage.

But that doesn’t matter. Right now, all that matters is venting my anger.

Xu You inspected the storage ring with his spiritual consciousness. It was indeed six years’ rent.

“It’s your turn now!” Li Zhuo glared fixedly at Meng Jingzhou. “Let’s see how you come up with six years’ rent!”

Meng Jingzhou turned and extended a hand toward Xu You. “Uncle Xu, lend me some spirit stones.”

Xu You handed the storage ring he had just received to Meng Jingzhou. Although Meng Jingzhou was disguised, Xu You had seen him use this appearance when he arrived in the imperial city.

“See? Six years’ rent.”

“You’re from the Meng Family?!” Li Zhuo realized what was going on. He could no longer suppress his fury. He felt like a clown, played for a fool by the other party.

“So what if I’m playing you? You think you have the right to chase away other guests?” Meng Jingzhou stopped pretending and simply removed his mask.

Li Zhuo felt as if a bucket of cold water had been dumped over him. His ire that was about to erupt vanished completely as he stood rooted to the spot, dumbfounded. Then, he pointed a finger at Meng Jingzhou and stuttered. “You’re Meng Jingzhou?!”

Why has this guy come back?

Why didn’t anyone inform me?

Or am I the first to know that Meng Jingzhou has returned?!

“Oh yo? Li Zhuo, you’ve grown some nerve, daring to call this young master’s name directly?” Meng Jingzhou smirked menacingly, rolling his neck and loosening his wrists as he stepped closer to Li Zhuo. The latter was so terrified that he forgot about the beautiful companion in his arms and staggered backward.

The diners watching the spectacle hadn’t expected that the one who dared to contend with Li Zhuo in wealth would be Meng Jingzhou.

“Eldest Young Master Meng has returned!” Someone who understood the implications shuddered inwardly. The imperial city is probably going to be anything but peaceful in the coming days.

“Who is Eldest Young Master Meng?” The question came from someone unfamiliar with the imperial city.

“Eldest Young Master Meng, Meng Jingzhou—haven’t you heard of him? He’s the one who joined the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“Then who’s more formidable, him or the Imperial City’s Four Young Masters?”

“The Imperial City’s Four Young Masters are nothing! Back when Meng Jingzhou hadn’t left the imperial city, those four didn’t dare show their faces. This lord is a fearsome character who even dared to beat up the young imperial prince.”

“I heard someone taught Li Zhuo a lesson before. Was it Meng Jingzhou?”

“Yes, it was him!”

“Then who’s the person sitting beside Eldest Young Master Meng?”

“I don’t know him.”

Li Zhuo’s face was deathly pallid, thoroughly frightened by Meng Jingzhou. He forced a smile. “Young Master Meng, what are you saying? It’s just that we haven’t seen each other for so long; I was excited and momentarily forgot the rules.”

“Well, Old Lu, do you now know this young master’s status in the imperial city?” Meng Jingzhou flaunted triumphantly. This was a rule he had established back then—Li Zhuo and the others had to address him as “Young Master” when they saw him.

Lu Yang rolled his eyes, unwilling to engage. What’s the big deal? I was even the sect leader in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Old Lu... He’s Lu Yang!” Upon learning of Meng Jingzhou’s identity, those familiar with Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect easily guessed Lu Yang’s identity and cried out involuntarily.

In terms of fame alone, Lu Yang’s renown surpassed even the Left Chancellor’s.

Perhaps people didn’t know the Left Chancellor’s name or what he had done, but they certainly knew Lu Yang’s deeds.

“That’s Lu Yang—the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple and the next Dao-Seeking Sect Leader?”

“It’s him! Who else would dare to be called Lu Yang these days?!”

“Why have both of them come to the imperial city?!”

Chapter 830: The Popular Lu Yang

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were two prominent characters in Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect, and the Taciturn Daoist Priest even had entire chapters devoted to their stories. The two of them could truly be called world-famous. Whether it was foreign or local cultivators, all had heard of their names.

Local cultivators in the imperial city knew even more. For instance, they were aware of the fearsome reputation Meng Jingzhou once held in the imperial city. If he hadn’t run away from home, how could the “Imperial City’s Four Young Masters” have emerged?

Recently, Lu Yang’s reputation had become somewhat more resounding than Meng Jingzhou’s. The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s advancement to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage drew everyone’s attention, incidentally bringing Lu Yang into the spotlight as well.

Lu Yang facepalmed. I didn’t expect myself to be so famous. Old Meng simply shouted “Old Lu,” and people could already guess my identity.

In that case, there’s no point in being disguised.

Lu Yang also removed his mask, revealing the face that the world was familiar with.

“It’s really him!”

“You’re Lu Yang!” Li Zhuo’s focus shifted to Lu Yang.

There was some history between his grandfather and the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Hence, his grandfather had instructed him to give Lu Yang a proper lesson if he ever encountered him.

But now, I feel like just keeping myself safe would already be an achievement.

“Little Zhuo, you’ve grown quite arrogant, huh? Just because there’s no seat available, you snatched someone else’s spot? Why weren’t you like this when you followed me in the past?”

Li Zhuo offered an awkward, obsequious smile, not daring to speak.

“Uncle Xu, don’t worry about us. We’ll wander around the imperial city a bit more.”

“Alright.” Xu You smiled and left Heavenly Fragrance Restaurant.

“Young Master Meng, shall I leave too?” Li Zhuo cautiously asked, edging backward stealthily.

“Wait, what are you leaving for? When I placed my bid earlier, I said today’s tab was on me. Since you ended up with the highest bid, shouldn’t that promise be fulfilled by you?”

“Young Master Meng is right, absolutely right.” Li Zhuo didn’t dare say otherwise. All he wanted now was to get away from Meng Jingzhou quickly. What spirit stones? What female companion? I no longer want any of it.

“Alright, get lost.”

Lu Yang felt as though he was granted an amnesty and hastily left Heavenly Fragrance Restaurant.

~~~

The news of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s appearance rapidly spread throughout the imperial city.

“What? The old Taciturn scoundrel’s disciple has appeared?” The Minister of Personnel couldn’t sit still. His cultivation talent was limited, with no hope of reaching the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, so he hadn’t entered seclusion.

He thought he would never have a chance to triumph over the Taciturn Daoist Priest in this life. However, he didn’t expect Heaven to grant him a golden opportunity—the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s little disciple delivered right to his doorstep.

“Son, come here. How’s your cultivation been lately?” The Minister of Personnel summoned his youngest son, the most promising among all his sons and the one with the best cultivation talent.

The Minister of Personnel’s son was handsome and dignified, making young girls turn their heads on the street.

“Thanks to the pills you provided, I haven’t encountered many bottlenecks, Father. I’m now at the Apex Nascent Soul Stage.”

The Minister of Personnel nodded. “I hear people outside have started calling you a prodigy?”

His son flashed a confident smile. “I dare not claim to be a prodigy; it’s merely others flattering me. But when it comes to combat, I have indeed never lost.”

“That’s good then. The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s youngest disciple, Lu Yang, has arrived. Your father couldn’t defeat that old Taciturn scoundrel. Now, your father is counting on you. Go and spar with Lu Yang.”

“Ah?” His son was dumbfounded. I am talented, yes, but I can’t compare to a talent like Lu Yang, the champion at the Dao-Seeking Sect’s 120,000-year celebration.

That’s a monster who could fight Young Creed Leader Lu to a draw!

If I were that formidable in a fight, why would I still be hanging around in the imperial city? I could have just joined the Heavenly Court Creed.

~~~

“Grandpa, Meng Jingzhou and Lu Yang bullied me.” Li Zhuo cried injustice as soon as he returned to the Left Chancellor Estate. The more he thought about it on the way back, the angrier he became, but he was no match for Meng Jingzhou and could only seek his grandfather’s help.

Grandpa has grudges against both the Meng Family and the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Given the chance to get even, he will definitely take action!

The Left Chancellor was an old man with white hair. After listening to Li Zhuo’s embellished account, he pondered for a moment. “You’re saying that the old Taciturn scoundrel’s disciple is also here?”

“Meng Jingzhou is the main problem; he’s simply gone too far with the bullying!” Li Zhuo complained indignantly. He wasn’t too concerned about Lu Yang.

The Left Chancellor ignored him, continuing to mutter to himself. “Say, if you were to acknowledge Lu Yang as your big brother, you and Lu Yang would become peers, and the Taciturn Daoist Priest would be considered to belong to my son’s generation. That’s how the logic works, right?”

“Ah?”

“What ‘ah?’ Hurry up and go acknowledge Lu Yang as your big brother!”

~~~

When Lu Yang returned to the Meng Estate, invitations arrived like falling snow, covering an entire table.

“So many; quite popular, huh?” Meng Jingzhou teased. Although he had many enemies in the imperial city, he was the Meng Family’s eldest young master after all. Those who found him an eyesore didn’t dare act openly.

Lu Yang drew a line down the middle of the table and explained to Meng Jingzhou. “On the left are letters of challenge, and on the right are requests for sworn brotherhood.

“The challenge letters are from the sons of Shifu’s enemies. The brotherhood requests are from the grandsons of Shifu’s enemies.”

Meng Jingzhou egged him on. “What’s there to be afraid of with the challenge letters? Just fight them.”

Lu Yang sighed gloomily. “In a one-on-one fight, I naturally have no fear. The problem is, these are all joint challenge letters.”

In other words, they plan to gang up on me.

Meng Jingzhou scratched his head. This is indeed tricky. Lu Yang can’t foolishly walk into a group beating, nor can he accept a group of little brothers.

If we ignore these invitations and go out, we can’t eliminate the possibility of Lu Yang getting ambushed or having someone cling to his thigh and begging to acknowledge him as a big brother.

“I have an idea.” A spark of inspiration struck Meng Jingzhou.

“What idea?”

~~~

Luotian Forest was a small forest located within the imperial city. Cultivators came here all year round to comprehend the wood spirit qi.

Today, Luotian Forest was livelier than usual. Scions of officials and aristocratic families had gathered here.

“You also received Lu Yang’s response letter?” Li Zhuo got along well with the Minister of Personnel’s son. The two met and had a casual chat.

“Yes. It said to come to Luotian Forest to resolve the problem. It’s been half a day, but why isn’t he here yet?” The Minister of Personnel’s son was baffled.

While everyone was puzzled, Meng Jingzhou jumped down from the treetops.

“Everyone, quiet down. If anyone keeps talking, I’ll have my family raise your interest rates.”

Instantly, no one dared to discuss anything further.

“I believe you all know the reason we have gathered everyone here today—it’s for the sake of my brother, Lu Yang.

“Some of you carry the grudges of the old generation and wish to challenge Lu Yang, while some of you want to take advantage of our sect leader and acknowledge Lu Yang as your big brother. These are all understandable.

“But there is only one Lu Yang. If you all swarm him, he definitely can’t fight you all. If you all swarm him to be your big brother, he can’t accept that either.

“To resolve this problem, Lu Yang and I have discussed and decided to host a grand contest.”

“Grand contest?” The crowd furrowed their brows, not understanding Meng Jingzhou’s meaning.

“As the saying goes, the strong reign supreme; the strong possess special privileges.

“This grand contest shall be named the 'First Lu Yang Championship.' The tournament will adopt a team format, with two-person teams competing against each other. The winning team advances to the next round until a final champion is determined.”

Just as the crowd was still digesting Meng Jingzhou’s words, a large red box suddenly descended from the sky, landing in front of Meng Jingzhou. It was exquisitely packaged and as tall as a person.

Standing on a tree branch, Meng Jingyu caught her breath. She had been the one who threw the box.

Meng Jingzhou swiftly tore open the box, revealing Lu Yang, who was tied to a chair. He grandly announced, “And this...is the price for this tournament—Lu Yang.”

“As long as you win the tournament, you can either challenge Lu Yang or acknowledge him as your big brother.”

Chapter 831: Win-Win-Win-Win Situation

After Meng Jingzhou announced the rules of the tournament, a deathly silence fell over Luotian Forest. The crowd resembled a pack of wolves in the night, their gleaming green eyes fixed upon Lu Yang, who was bound to the chair.

Under their gazes, Lu Yang’s scalp tingled. Seeing a flurry of invitations pile up on a table in the Meng Estate was one thing; having those invitations replaced by a dense crowd of real people standing before him was entirely another matter.

Shifu, just how many people did you provoke in the imperial city? You’re at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage now. Why are you not rushing over to deal with these enemies?

In this perilous cultivation world, decisiveness and ruthlessness were necessary for self-preservation.

Meng Jingyu sat among the treetops. On her left was a plate of fruits transported from the East Sea and pastries from Heavenly Fragrance Restaurant. On her right was juice extracted from fruits shipped from the Demon Region. These were her compensation for her hard work in tying up Lu Yang, packaging him into an exquisite box, and tossing it at the opportune moment.

She watched the scene below with keen interest. This is much more interesting than cultivation or studying.

According to Elder Brother, letting me witness how cultivators fight will be greatly beneficial for my future cultivation.

Even if Father asks, I can say “true knowledge comes from real application.”

At the thought of this, she continued watching gleefully. Doing something like this for the first time was thrilling.

“Lu Yang is right here! Why bother with a tournament? Everyone, let’s rush at him together!” someone in the crowd shouted. He bore his family’s hopes and needed to wash away his past shame. He had no time for such drawn-out nonsense.

“Lu Yang is my future big brother. I’d like to see who dares lay a hand on him!” another person in the crowd yelled. He also bore his family’s hopes and wanted to acknowledge Lu Yang as his big brother to lower the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s seniority.

“Rushing at him together isn’t real skill; it’s an unfair victory. Defeating Lu Yang one-on-one is the proper way!”

“Nonsense! You’re at the Divine Transfiguration Stage; of course, you have the face to say you can fight him one-on-one. Lower yourself to the Nascent Soul Stage and try fighting Lu Yang!”

“Calm down, everyone, calm down.” Meng Jingzhou had anticipated such a situation. “If anyone dares to make a scene again, I, on behalf of the Meng Family, will announce that your family is our Meng Family’s best business partner!”

Meng Jingzhou stood with his hands behind his back, looking at the crowd below. Wherever his gaze swept across, people lowered their heads and didn’t dare to meet his eyes, fearful of becoming the Meng Family’s business partner.

“That’s more like it. No more objections, right? If there are no objections, let’s get ready for the tournament.”

In fact, the crowd was quite willing to have a tournament. The imperial city was huge, and they rarely had the chance to gather for one-on-one combat. Those who dared to challenge Lu Yang in teams had confidence in their own cultivation; they weren’t the type who purely relied on mountains of pills to forcefully raise their cultivation. If they left the imperial city and joined a sect, they would be accepted by first-class or even S-class sects.

“Come on, come on, let’s start drawing lots.” Meng Jingzhou brought out a large box containing pairs of number plates. Those who picked the same number would be opponents.

The box had been treated to block probing, preventing any cheating through spiritual consciousness.

The group of scions obediently lined up according to Meng Jingzhou’s instructions and drew lots, praying they would be matched up with weaker opponents.

Some were joyful, some were worried, and some had absolute confidence in their strength, believing they wouldn’t lose.

“Oh no, my opponent is Sun Chuanxian!” someone paled, aware that he couldn't defeat his opponent.

Sun Chuanxian,[1] son of the Minister of Works and one of the Imperial City’s Four Young Masters, was renowned for his martial prowess.

After Sun Chuanxian received his number plate, he didn’t even look to see who his opponent was.

My cultivation was achieved completely through diligent practice, without relying on pills. In terms of cultivation, few present are qualified to be my opponent. I believe I will definitely win in the end and become Lu Yang’s opponent!

“An Nan’er is here too?”

Yet another unfortunate soul was matched against one of the select few with the strongest cultivation among the imperial city’s younger generation.

An Nan’er was the granddaughter of the Nation-Stabilizing Duke. Legend had it that unnatural phenomena appeared at her birth, and had the Nation-Stabilizing Duke not intervened, the entire imperial city might have been engulfed by the unnatural phenomena.

Apart from her, there were also Luo Wushang[2]—son of the Minister of War, hailed as peerless in both civil and martial arts—and Zhong Yi—son of the Central Secretariat, meticulous in his thoughts, and said to be someone who could obtain anything he desired.

Sun Chuanxian’s match concluded swiftly. He condensed a frost dragon, which exhaled its icy breath, freezing his opponent into an ice block before tossing him out of the arena.

Ning Fan was the son of the Grand Imperial Censor. Watching Sun Chuanxian fight so cleanly and efficiently, he looked up at the sky. It seems unlikely that things will play out to the end.

Setting aside the final prize being Lu Yang, Sun Chuanxian had bullied Ning Fan several times in the past by relying on his fighting prowess. Ning Fan would have liked to defeat Sun Chuanxian, but unfortunately, his strength didn’t permit it.

“Ning Fan, do you want to win?” Meng Jingzhou quietly approached Ning Fan with a smile.

“Eldest Young Master Meng, what advice do you have?”

“Advice is too strong a word. I have a little item here that might be of help.”

“What little item?”

Meng Jingzhou whipped out a small wooden puppet from behind his back. It was three inches tall, neither sanded nor painted with a face, and looked extremely crudely made.

“This is a wooden puppet I just plucked from a tree. For your next match against Sun Chunxian, you don’t need to lift a finger. Just throw out this puppet, and it will fight for you. This puppet can exhibit a cultivation realm similar to yours, so it doesn’t violate the rules. Well, do you want it?”

“There’s such a good thing?” Ning Fan was overjoyed.

“Five hundred thousand spirit stones for a single rental.”

“So expensive?” Ning Fan was startled. Unlike Li Zhuo, he came from a family with an especially strict upbringing and didn’t have that many spirit stones.

“Perfect, it just so happens that we also offer lending services here.” This was the Meng Family’s main business. Meng Jingzhou deftly pulled out a pouch of storage rings containing high-grade spirit stones, along with a loan contract.

“Considering we’re acquainted, the annual interest is only ten percent. Not too much, right?”

“Umm...”

“Aiya, you’re on the verge of breaking through to the Divine Transfiguration Stage. Once you reach the Divine Transfiguration Stage, won’t you be able to come up with five hundred thousand spirit stones?” Meng Jingzhou wasn’t scamming Ning Fan. Upon reaching the Divine Transfiguration Stage, families would confer rewards, with the lowest being five hundred thousand spirit stones.

“I’ll buy it!” Ning Fan acquiesced through gritted teeth, borrowing five hundred thousand from Meng Jingzhou and handing over another five hundred thousand to rent the small wooden puppet.

“Can this thing really fight?” Ning Fan skeptically looked at the small puppet he was carrying, not feeling it was particularly powerful.

“What are you saying? I, Meng Jingzhou, may have a bad reputation, but I’ve never sold fake goods.”

Ning Fan rummaged through his memories. It’s true.

Soon, the first round ended, and it was time for Ning Fan’s match against Sun Chuanxian.

Everyone was aware of Sun Chuanxian’s prowess and had no confidence in Ning Fan.

To their surprise, once the match began, Ning Fan didn’t cast any offensive or defensive spells. Instead, he threw out a small wooden puppet.

The three-inch-tall puppet brandished a wooden sword, emitting “he-he, haha” sounds, as if it was trying to intimidate Sun Chuanxian.

Seeing this, Sun Chuanxian roared with laughter, utterly unimpressed.

Suddenly, the puppet slashed out with a terrifying sword qi, startling Sun Chuanxian into retreating a step backward while blocking with his ice dragon, narrowly avoiding injury.

Sun Chuanxian acted as though he was facing a formidable enemy and adopted a battle-ready stance, no longer daring to underestimate the little wooden puppet.

On the stage, Lu Yang focused intently on controlling the puppet to fight Sun Chuanxian.

This small wooden puppet was something he had created using a wooden clone and Shrinking Earth To Inches. As a prize of my stature, earning a little extra income isn’t going overboard, right? This was why he had discussed and arranged this with Meng Jingzhou.

Sun Chuanxian got to fight Lu Yang as he wished.

Ning Fan could defeat Sun Chuanxian.

Lu Yang earned five hundred thousand spirit stones by renting himself out.

Meng Jingzhou obtained a debt note of five hundred thousand spirit stones.

This was a win-win-win-win situation.

1. The name “Chuanxian” can somewhat be translated as “summoning immortals.” ☜

2. “Wushuang” literally means peerless in Chinese. ☜

Chapter 832: Unity is Strength

“Well, Little Sister, learned anything?” Meng Jingzhou leaped onto the treetops and downed the juice that Meng Jingyu was about to drink in one gulp.

Meng Jingyu looked at her brother gloomily, only speaking after a while. “Then why don’t we open an underground gambling ring and bet on Ning Fan to win?”

Meng Jingzhou waved his hand. “Our Meng family colludes with officials for business, but we still can’t do anything illegal.”

~~~

The little wooden puppet’s swordsmanship was extremely refined. Sun Chuanxian had seen many sword cultivators, but he had never encountered one with such skill.

“Ice Dragons Rise from the Sea!” Sun Chuanxian yelled, conjuring two ice dragons. The dragons exhaled their icy breaths, freezing the ground and coating the leaves overhead with a layer of frost.

The little wooden puppet continued to swing its tiny wooden sword, making “he-he, ha-ha” sounds, and created a crude Sword Dao field around itself. Neither the dragon breaths nor the extreme cold could harm it!

“Ning Fan, I didn’t expect you to be hiding such a skill!” Sun Chuanxian’s impression of Ning Fan shifted. We’ve fought so many times, yet Ning Fan has never revealed his identity as a puppeteer. Even when on the arena stage, he used the puppet’s cute appearance to deceive me. What a devious schemer!

Ning Fan was also astonished. He hadn’t expected the little wooden puppet to be such a formidable fighter. The five hundred thousand spirit stones were well spent.

“It looks like my biggest competitor in this tournament is you! With this skill, even Lu Yang would have a tough time if he fights you!”

The second round of matches proceeded simultaneously. Sun Chuanxian noticed that Lu Yang had been paying attention to their match while bound to the chair all this time. This means that he also thinks highly of Ning Fan’s puppet technique!

Lu Yang always believed in getting what you paid for. Since Ning Fan had coughed up five hundred thousand spirit stones, his service had to be worth the fee. Thus, he controlled the wooden puppet clone even more earnestly.

“Slash!”

The little wooden puppet gave a soft cry, beheading the two frost dragons. Like a tiny hammer, it then slammed into Sun Chuanxian, knocking him out of the arena.

“Ning Fan wins!”

“I really won?” Ning Fan’s face lit up with joy.

He was about to retrieve the puppet when he saw it scamper into the crowd, disappearing without a trace.

The service that was worth five hundred thousand spirit stones concluded right there.

~~~

The other match of the second round was equally eye-catching, featuring An Nan’er and Luo Wushuang.

“Fellow Daoist An, I never imagined we would meet here.” Luo Wushuang wore armor and wielded a long halberd, resembling an awe-inspiring young general who had cut through the battlefield.

“Unfortunately, I can’t yield to you this time. My father ordered me to defeat Lu Yang to wash away the shame of his previous defeat by the Taciturn Daoist Priest!”

An Nan’er’s expression was placid. The two jade bracelets on her wrists enlarged, transforming into two jade rings that hummed in the air. “What a coincidence. My grandfather also instructed me to acknowledge Lu Yang as my elder brother. I am determined to win this fight!”

Hearing this, prize Lu Yang wanted to shout, “If you want to acknowledge me as your elder brother, you don’t need to participate in the fight.” However, Meng Jingzhou seemed to have anticipated what he wished to say and stuffed a rag into his mouth.

You must be joking. How can all good things fall to you?

This was an unequal battle. Luo Wushuang was at the Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage, while Nan An’er was only at the Apex Nascent Soul Stage. One was a peerlessly talented combatant, while the other was a genius born with unusual celestial phenomena. If their cultivation realms were the same, they could have a proper back-and-forth fight. However, they were separated by a major realm, so there wasn’t much of a contest.

The two looked at each other, both seeming to have reached some sort of decision, and spoke at the same time.

“Fellow Daoist An, if I overwhelm you with my cultivation realm, even if I win, you likely won’t accept it. I’ll suppress my cultivation realm now. This way, if you lose, you will be wholeheartedly convinced.” As Luo Wushuang spoke, he formed hand seals, binding himself and suppressing his cultivation to the Apex Nascent Soul Stage.

“Fellow Daoist Luo, do not think that just because I am a cultivation realm lower, you are assured of victory. To be frank, I’ve broken through to the Divine Transfiguration Stage long ago. I had simply sealed my cultivation previously.” An Nan’er drew a line across her brow, and her aura surged violently. In the blink of an eye, she had risen to the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

Luo Wushuang, “...”

An Nan’er, “...”

Both sides fell into a prolonged silence.

An Nan’er spoke first, breaking the impasse. “Would you like to restore your cultivation to the Divine Transfiguration Stage?”

Luo Wushuang remained silent for a moment, then replied, “...That would take two hours. How about you reseal your cultivation?”

“After my cultivation is unsealed, I have to wait four hours before I can reseal it.”

Both sides fell into a prolonged silence again. They couldn’t possibly make everyone wait here idly for two hours.

“Fellow Daoist Luo, pardon my offense!” An Nan’er resolved herself. Although using a higher cultivation realm to overwhelm someone went against her principles, it was the only method now.

“Whoa, wait a moment...” Luo Wushuang hadn’t expected Nan An’er to act so decisively. Before he could react, two jade rings behind her shot forth and knocked him over, sending him flying.

“An Nan’er wins!”

~~~

Meanwhile, Zhong Yi, who was highly regarded by everyone, encountered a rather intractable opponent.

“Who is this? He fights so well. Looks like Zhong Yi is going to lose.”

“Probably some family’s illegitimate child who has been hidden away.”

Zhong Yi was struck and sent flying by his opponent, staggering several steps backward before regaining his footing. Gasping for breath, he stared at his opponent. “I didn’t imagine there to be an expert like you in the imperial city. You’ve hidden yourself so well! Who are you? Why have I never seen you before?”

His opponent appeared to be a youth around Zhong Yi’s age. Hearing Zhong Yi’s question, he looked somewhat abashed and slowly explained. “Actually, I’m not a cultivator from around here. I heard Luotian Forest in the imperial city was famous, so I came to take a look. After that, you all showed up and squeezed me into the crowd. It didn’t feel appropriate to leave then, so I stayed out of embarrassment. That guy surnamed Meng insisted I draw a lot, and before I knew it, I was fighting. And then I ended up running into you.

“By the way, I’m at the Fusion Stage.”

Zhong Yi, “...”

You’re a Fusion cultivator—how do you have the face to fight a bunch of youngsters like us? Do you have any sense of shame?

The Fusion Stage youth smacked the back of his head and laughed. “If I cared about face, I wouldn’t have cultivated to the Fusion Stage, right?”

Then he made a dashing exit, without even leaving his name.

“Zhong Yi wins!”

Zhong Yi was incredibly strong, overcoming all his opponents. He met An Nan’er in the finals and finally defeated her after three hundred exchanges.

“Congratulations on your victory, Fellow Daoist Zhong Yi.” Meng Jingzhou clapped with a smile, stepping aside to reveal the tightly bound Lu Yang behind him.

“Now, Fellow Daoist Zhong Yi, you may choose to challenge Lu Yang or swear brotherhood with him.”

In fact, this didn’t need to be asked. Meng Jingzhou saw the blazing fighting spirit in Zhong Yi’s eyes. He’s definitely going to challenge Lu Yang.

But can a mere Basic Divine Transfiguration cultivator defeat Lu Yang?

Zhong Yi didn’t answer directly. Instead, he said solemnly, “Our forebears forged a path through thorns and passed down their legacies generation after generation, creating the cultivation system for those who came after. At the end of the Great Yu era, the Jiang Family rose and led armies to establish the Great Xia Dynasty. This demonstrates that some things cannot be accomplished by a single person alone. Unity is strength.”

He pointed at Lu Yang, his words ringing with conviction. “I choose to gang up on Lu Yang!”

Chapter 833: Passing Off a Fake as Real

Lu Yang’s reputation preceded him, his renown spreading far and wide. Zhong Yi wasn’t a fool. If he went against Lu Yang by himself, he would certainly lose.

Hearing Zhong Yi’s wish, the crowd looked up, staring at Lu Yang. Even those who wanted to acknowledge him as their big brother were no exception.

After all, this was the champion’s wish—it had to be fulfilled.

Moreover, acknowledging him as big brother could be done after the fight too.

“Old Meng, what should we do?” Cold sweat poured down Lu Yang’s back. He felt like a fattened white hog tied to a chair, facing a pack of starving wolves.

Meng Jingzhou had anticipated this situation and signaled for Lu Yang not to worry. “Relax, I’ve already registered this with the authorities. Our event follows legal procedures; it doesn’t count as an unlawful gang brawl. Even if a mob fight breaks out, it’s fine.”

“...Then what about me?”

“You count as normal wear and tear.”

“Old Meng, your grandfather!” Lu Yang forcefully shattered the chair and ropes and took to his heels. If I don’t run now, there’ll be no chance later.

Meng Jingzhou smirked coldly at this scene. I still remember the “One Meng Into Ten Thousand Mengs” incident not long ago. Serves you right for helping my dad beat me!

If I don’t get back at you, my conscience won’t be at ease!

“Brothers, charge! Let’s take down Lu Yang together!” Someone below shouted.

Instantly, the scions swarmed forward, unleashing all sorts of techniques at Lu Yang without restraint.

Lu Yang suspected the person who yelled was arranged by Meng Jingzhou.

The first stage of the First Lu Yang Championship concluded. The second stage officially began, with all cultivators eliminated in the first stage revived to participate in the second stage.

“Shrinking Earth!” Lu Yang dove headfirst into the ground like he was swimming, evading the attacks. Luotian Forest had towering ancient trees with intertwined roots, and Lu Yang hid within these root systems, making him extremely difficult to locate.

“Where is he?!”

“Use spiritual consciousness to find him!”

“That won’t work. His spiritual consciousness is too strong; he’s shielding himself. We can’t find him!”

Lu Yang was like a deep-sea shark raising its head in the water to watch these ignorant tourists, who remained completely unaware that danger had quietly descended.

“Draw Underground Prison!”

Lu Yang drew a circle underground. A young master standing on the periphery suddenly fell into an underground cage.

This young master was about to call for help when he heard Lu Yang’s sinister threat. “Don’t shout. If you do, I’ll perform the Arhat Fist.”

Thanks to the Taciturn Daoist Priest, Lu Yang’s Arhat Fist’s reputation also spread far and wide.

That young master hastily shut his mouth and nodded, expressing his stance.

Satisfied, Lu Yang swam away, seeking his next target.

Two, three, four...more and more people were tricked into the underground prisons by Lu Yang.

Luo Wushuang was the first to notice something amiss. “Something’s wrong. Why are several people missing?!”

“I heard Lu Yang obtained the legacy of an ancient earthworm! Not only can he burrow underground, but he can also create underground cages!” Zhong Yi said seriously, spreading his spiritual consciousness. He stared nervously and vigilantly at his feet, a drop of cold sweat trickling down his cheek.

It’d be utterly humiliating to be dragged underground by Lu Yang.

Realizing that his plan was exposed, Lu Yang temporarily refrained from acting.

“Can’t be bothered that much now! Since he’s hiding underground and we can’t find him, let’s just flip the entire ground over!” a young master roared in anger, punching the ground, causing cracks to fissure the earth.

The others followed suit, using brute force or earth or wood elemental spells. Luotian Forest seemed to come alive as every inch of soil was churned upward.

Lu Yang shrank to a one-inch miniature figure, hiding behind a clump of overturned soil. Even so, the crowd spotted him with their sharp eyes.

“Over there!” Sun Chuanxian pointed at the tiny Lu Yang and hollered.

“Ice Dragon Mantra!”

“One Tree Reaches the Sky!”

“Flying Sand Whirling Stones!”

Unable to avoid the attacks, Lu Yang reverted to his original size. Simultaneously, he activated the Three Flavor True Fire and Golden Bird True Flame, merging the two into a wall of flame.

The ice dragon collided with the true fire, producing a hissing steam that obscured everyone’s view.

Lu Yang seized this opportunity to strike quickly, hitting as many opponents as he could.

“Arhat Fist!”

Sun Chuanxian was closest to Lu Yang and thus the first to enjoy the Arhat Fist treatment.

“Oh no!” Sun Chuanxian instinctively raised his hands to block, then suddenly remembered the terrifying effects of the Lu-Style Arhat Fist. He tried to switch from blocking to dodging, but it was too late. Struck by Lu Yang’s fist, he was sent flying backward.

Along with his body, his hair was also sent flying away.

“Quick, dodge! Don’t touch him!” others cried out. They didn’t dare to engage directly, scattering away. Lu Yang was like a wolf among sheep; wherever he went, the flock retreated.

At the critical moment, Zhong Yi stepped forward to take charge of the situation. “Everyone, don’t be afraid! I’ve learned the Buddhist forbidden technique, Longevity Art. I guarantee everyone’s hair will grow back!”

Hearing this, the crowd regained their courage and boldly continued fighting Lu Yang.

Lu Yang was trapped in a predicament. No matter how strong he was, he couldn’t defeat so many people at the same time. These people weren’t rootless rogue cultivators either; their combat power was outstanding for their cultivation realms.

Watching Lu Yang get beaten, Meng Jingzhou was delighted and cheered from the sidelines.

“Old Lu, left, left! Someone’s trying to hit you on the left... Hey, I even warned you. How did you still get hit?

“Put more force into it! Haven’t you all eaten?

“Old Lu, don’t just defend! Take the initiative!

“Look at you lot, can’t even fight properly. How did you achieve your current cultivation? Put your backs into it!”

“Old Meng, you forced my hand!” Lu Yang was enraged. You really think I have no way to deal with you?

Lu Yang’s moves changed. He stopped using both fists and spells simultaneously, focusing solely on fist techniques. His fist style also changed, becoming even more razor-sharp, unsettling everyone momentarily.

On the other hand, Meng Jingzhou found Lu Yang’s movements increasingly familiar.

Suddenly, Meng Jingzhou felt a portion of his power being drawn away, drifting toward Lu Yang, who was in an arduous battle with the crowd. Lu Yang’s form changed, transforming into Meng Jingzhou’s appearance.

Meng Jingzhou Animal Form Fist!

An ominous feeling immediately washed over Meng Jingzhou, and he turned to run. However, the Lu Yang who had turned into Meng Jingzhou wouldn’t give him that chance, breaking through the crowd and rapidly closing in on him.

Just as the crowd was about to attack, they halted their actions and looked at each other, unsure who they should strike.

“Old Lu, how dare you take on my appearance?!” One Meng Jingzhou grabbed the other Meng Jingzhou’s collar in fury.

“Bullshit! I’m the real Meng Jingzhou! It’s you trying to divert the calamity, you shameless dog!”

“I’m the real one!”

“I am the real one!”

“Little Sister, I’m your elder brother!” One Meng Jingzhou leaped into the treetops, seeking help from Meng Jingyu, who was watching the spectacle.

The other Meng Jingzhou also jumped onto the tree, speaking softly, “Little Sister, can’t you recognize your elder brother?”

Meng Jingzhou watched her two elder brothers jump up, her small mouth agape in shock for a long while.

She looked at one elder brother, then at the other. Seeing they were identical, she hesitated.

“Elder Brother mentioned in his letters that he often defeats Lu Yang-gege. How about you two fight, and whoever wins is my elder brother?”

Chapter 834: It Doesn’t Seem Like We’ll Lose Out Even if We Hit the Wrong One

Meng Jingzhou was momentarily stunned but quickly began to analyze. Lu Yang has transformed into me, but his various techniques are restricted, drastically reducing his combat power. However, this grandson Lu Yang had borrowed a portion of my power during his transformation. If we really fight, the outcome will be uncertain!

In that case, the answer is clear!

The real Meng Jingzhou attacked first, kicking the fake Meng Jingzhou down from the tree.

Seeing this, Zhong Yi was the first to come to a judgement, shouting, “Ambush? Someone who could do such a despicable thing must be Lu Yang!”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

What good deeds have I done in my daily life that made you all think so highly of my character?

He immediately jumped down from the tree, standing together with the fake version of himself, causing everyone to be unable to distinguish who was who again.

“What now?”

“Hit both! We won’t lose out even if we hit the wrong one!” Luo Wushuang yelled.

Everyone agreed it made sense. In fact, it was better to seize this opportunity to hit Meng Jingzhou.

Fighting Lu Yang or acknowledging him as big brother were orders from their elders. Hitting Meng Jingzhou came from their heartfelt desire.

“Old Lu, you bastard, dragging me down with you!”

“We’re both about to get beaten together, and you’re still acting?”

“Acting my ass! I’m asserting my identity!”

The two Meng Jingzhous bickered endlessly, but it didn’t matter. Everyone didn’t care which was real and which was fake.

Oh wait, it would be best if we could distinguish the real Meng Jingzhou. That way, we can hit him with even more force.

Meng Jingzhou realized this too. Lu Yang transforming into me is a blatant overt scheme. Even if they can distinguish who’s fake and who’s real, everyone will collectively turn a blind eye to it!

So vicious!

“Brothers, charge! Take Meng Jingzhou down... Ah no, take Lu Yang down and save Young Master Meng!”

“Kill!”

Seeing two Meng Jingzhous, everyone’s spirits were invigorated, and their attacks became sharper than before.

“Dang, Old Meng, you’re way too hated. After I turned into you, their attack methods have risen to a whole new level,” one of the Meng Jingzhous suddenly commented.

Everyone instantly realized this was the fake Meng Jingzhou.

They temporarily ignored the fake one and went to hit the real Meng Jingzhou. Their attacks originally aimed at this Meng Jingzhou were all directed toward the other Meng Jingzhou.

“Old Meng, do you have any damn shame? Why are you still pretending to be me?!” the other Meng Jingzhou cursed angrily, as if he was the real Lu Yang.

Everyone hesitated again, unsure who was real.

“Fellow Daoists, since we can’t distinguish them, let’s just follow the original plan—hit them both!”

~~~

Meanwhile, An Nan’er quietly withdrew from the battle and leaped into the treetops, sitting beside Meng Jingyu.

“Little Sister Jingyu, which one do you think is your elder brother?”

Meng Jingyu had her head lowered, eating fruits. Hearing An Nan’er’s question, she looked up and flashed an innocent smile.

“They’re both my gege.”

~~~

“Arhat Fist!”

“Arhat Fist!”

The two Meng Jingzhous were like carbon copies, their Arhat Fist movements perfectly synchronized.

Actually, this was normal. It was Meng Jingzhou who taught Lu Yang the Arhat Fist in the first place.

“Which side is losing hair?”

The scions who were struck hastily checked their hair and were surprised to find it intact—not a single strand had fallen off.

One Meng Jingzhou suddenly understood and pointed at the other Meng Jingzhou. “I’ve got it! You’re simultaneously using Arhat Fist and Longevity Art!”

“Nonsense! It’s clearly you using Arhat Fist and Longevity Art! Don’t pin it on this young master!”

Both Meng Jingzhous wanted to prove they were Lu Yang.

Lu Yang had considered reverting to his original appearance. But once he changed back, everyone might lack an excuse to target Meng Jingzhou, and he would still be the one to suffer.

“Heaven-Shaking Six Forms!” one Meng Jingzhou hollered. His entire aura elevated, and the soil beneath his feet shook and churned.

Although Lu Yang didn’t know the Heaven-Shaking Six Forms, that didn’t matter. No one else had seen the real technique either. Heaven-Shaking Six Forms is Third Elder’s unique art. How could juniors have the chance to witness it? Only the elders saw it when they were getting beaten.

Lu Yang used his fist as a sword. His aura also elevated to a higher level, and his fist technique was equally sharp. “Heaven-Shaking Six Forms!”

Despite dragging Meng Jingzhou in as a scapegoat, Lu Yang’s situation remained precarious. There were too many people. If not for his frequent sparring sessions with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, he would have been overwhelmed by the barrage of concentrated attacks long ago.

“Hmph, you’ve forced this young master’s hand!” Meng Jingzhou was enraged. He summoned his twin nascent souls, which merged and transformed him into an adept with three heads and six arms.

Three Heads Six Arms was Meng Jingzhou’s trump card, and he rarely used it. For safety’s sake, the Taciturn Daoist Priest hadn’t revealed all of Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s techniques during his storytelling. Hence, no one knew that only Meng Jingzhou could execute Three Heads Six Arms.

“Heaven-Shaking Six Forms!” Performing Heaven-Shaking Six Forms in the Three Heads Six Arms state amplified its power severalfold. No peer could possibly withstand this punch.

Zhong Yi quickly made a judgment. “So strong? Then he must be Lu Yang. Concentrate fire on the other one!”

The real Meng Jingzhou felt his pressure ease drastically, though he wasn’t sure whether he should be happy or not.

What do you mean the stronger one must be Lu Yang?

Seeing that this wouldn’t do, Lu Yang hurriedly drew his Qingfeng Sword to face his opponents.

Although Lu Yang seldom used swords, the world knew of his identity as a sword cultivator. Noticing the Qingfeng Sword drawn and witnessing exceptional swordsmanship, they were convinced it couldn’t be Meng Jingzhou impersonating him. They turned to deal with the real Meng Jingzhou.

Of course, they couldn’t be too obvious when targeting the real Meng Jingzhou. They still left about a third of their forces to besiege Lu Yang. Someone even shouted, “I didn’t expect Eldest Young Master Meng’s sword techniques to also be this superb! I am impressed!”

The real Meng Jingzhou cursed inwardly. When the heck did I learn sword techniques?

Meng Jingzhou was under focused fire, and part of his power was borrowed by Lu Yang. His stamina soon ran out, and he collapsed under the mob assault.

Seeing his scapegoat fallen, Lu Yang reverted to his original appearance, returning the borrowed power to Meng Jingzhou.

Everyone realized that the one who had fallen was Meng Jingzhou. Their expressions changed dramatically, and they hastily helped him up.

“Aiya, Eldest Young Master Meng, you should have said you were the real one earlier. Otherwise, we wouldn’t have hit so hard.”

Everyone chimed in agreement. “Exactly, exactly, we all thought you were Lu Yang. That’s why we went all out.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

I’ve only been away from the imperial city for over five years. How have you all become so shameless?

The second round of the First Lu Yang Championship continued. Prize Lu Yang was still putting up resistance obstinately, refusing to admit defeat.

Without Meng Jingzhou as a scapegoat, the full pressure returned to him.

In his mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy sat upright on her imperial throne, drawing out her words as she leisurely inquired, “Xiao Yangzi, do you need this immortal to help you?”

Lu Yang thought, Immortal Fairy, if you want to fight, just say so. You’re not even trying to hide that eager expression on your face.

Lu Yang bowed. “Your Exalted Majesty, please lend a hand.”

In the real world, Lu Yang was standing in the center of the crowd. He opened his eyes, his gaze containing the vicissitudes of life, as if it spanned countless millennia.

He swept his gaze across everyone and slowly said, “You ordinary mortals are but straw dogs. You have the fortune to behold this esteemed one, so why do you not bow?”

Chapter 835: Spirit Medium

“So haughty?!”

“He’s not taking us seriously at all!”

Originally, everyone was getting tired. Now, hearing Lu Yang’s brazen words, they instantly regained energy.

Facing the agitated crowd, “Lu Yang” showed no signs of retreating. His eyes were as calm as an ancient well. “Heh, not treating you all seriously? What qualifications do you have to be treated seriously by this esteemed one?”

In the mental space, Lu Yang facepalmed and sighed. Why was I so out of my mind to let the Immortal Fairy take over?

There’s no avoiding trouble now.

However, it was too late now. Lu Yang had already handed over his body to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Even if he regretted it, he couldn’t get it back until she had her fill of fun.

In the distance, Meng Jingzhou watched Lu Yang making bombastic statements in astonishment, and his heart sank. “Oh no, has he been beaten stupid?”

“Attack!” Luo Wushuang took the initiative, controlling the ancient trees in Luotian Forest. Their roots writhed like tentacles, emerging from the ground to ambush the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had anticipated this. The moment the roots shot out, she lightly tapped a toe on one and executed an aerial flip, easily evading the ambush.

Zhong Yi crouched on the ground like a lion with a flowing mane, emitting a roar that shook the heavens. This was the most orthodox Buddhist Lion Roar, its sound capable of shattering space.

The Lion Roar stirred spatial ripples, and the sound waves coalesced into a majestic lion that pounced at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

This was a sign of minor success in the Buddhist Lion Roar, where one could replicate three-tenths of the Buddhist Guardian Lion’s true essence.

“Iced Over a Thousand Li!” Sun Chuanxian also acted. A layer of ice coated his palms. Anything that his fists touched, whether human or demon, would turn into an ice sculpture.

At the same time, Luo Wushuang activated the ancient trees’ root system again to limit the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s movement space, ensuring the Lion Roar and ice dragon’s breath could strike her.

“Such bothersome roots. Paraquat Fist!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grumbled impatiently and threw an utterly terrifying punch. The moment the ancient roots touched her fist, they rapidly withered, losing all vitality.

Witnessing this, Luo Wushuang hurriedly severed his connection with the ancient trees, but he was a step too late. He felt completely drained, as if all his strength had been siphoned away, and couldn’t even stand. His legs gave way, and he slumped to the ground.

“What move is this?!”

Just as the Buddhist Guardian Lion manifested from sound waves was about to touch the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it trembled uncontrollably, as though it had encountered something terrifying. Unable to maintain its form, it dissipated with a boom.

Everyone was perplexed, not understanding what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had done.

Only Lu Yang, who was observing from the mental space, could roughly guess the reason. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy often consumed great demons in the ancient era, and those great demons imprinted that fear into their bloodlines. If the Lion Roar didn’t replicate three-tenths of the Buddhist Guardian Lion’s true essence, it might have been fine. But once it replicated the lion’s true essence, it possessed three-tenths of its spirit, so it had to face the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s suppression.

This suppression is more terrifying than the one on the Ancient Barbarian Tribe’s bloodline.

In the blink of an eye, only Sun Chuanxian remained to battle with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Others were worried about collateral damage from Iced Over a Thousand Li and didn’t dare to approach.

The temperature around Sun Chuanxian dropped to a frightening level. The air was dry, and the ground was frozen, yet this was merely due to the residual aura from his icy palms.

“You think holding two blocks of ice makes you impressive?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy derided him.

Suddenly, heat radiated from her, melting the ground’s ice. Her movements were elegant and light, like an ancient divine tree bearing ten suns. Layer upon layer of flames erupted from the ground, forming a sea of fire.

“Fusang Tree Fist!”

This was also one of the Immortal Fairy’s fist techniques. It envisioned the user as the Fusang Tree, emanating flames more terrifying than a Jinwu golden crow.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy danced amidst the flames with a graceful posture, resembling an immortal male fairy.

“What beautiful movements!”

“I heard the monarch of the Demon Kingdom, Supreme Lord Zhu Tian, entered the Dao through dance. Lu Yang’s dance might rival Supreme Lord Zhu Tian’s when he was at the Nascent Soul Stage.”

“It’s just that...the movements are so feminine?”

The spectators wore peculiar expressions. If Lu Yang’s earlier combat displayed masculine yang energy, the movements now were as feminine as could be.

“He probably learned it from the Taciturn Daoist Priest.”

“Makes sense.”

Everyone nodded, accepting this deduction.

Sun Chuanxian was engulfed in a sea of fire, unable to see the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s location. With just two punches, she broke his Iced Over a Thousand Li.

“Attack together!”

With Sun Chuanxian defeated, everyone finally stopped worrying about collateral damage and charged together.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s combat skills were exquisitely refined, a level even Lu Yang couldn’t reach. The power in every punch and kick was precisely measured. She could even leverage one opponent’s attack to strike another opponent, demonstrating her mastery of redirecting force.

Everyone was flabbergasted. Just moments ago, Lu Yang had been suppressed, but now, he seemed to be possessed by an immortal, becoming unbeatable and unrivalled. They could discern that Lu Yang’s combat power had risen to a new level, making him even harder to deal with.

In that case, we needn’t hold back.

“Nascent souls, come out!”

Everyone present was at the Nascent Soul Stage. Pick any one of them and place them in the outside world, and they would be considered a fearsome Nascent Soul old monster.

The scions all had family legacies. Every person’s nascent soul was different—metal, wood, water, fire, earth, ice, lightning, space, physique arts, artifact arts...akin to a hundred schools of thought contending, each with its strengths.

Lu Yang broke into a cold sweat on behalf of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

She’s the one fighting, but my body is the one getting hurt.

“Just a bunch of congenitally deficient nascent souls. No matter how many there are, it is futile.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke with indifference, still not taking everyone’s nascent souls seriously. “I shall let you witness this esteemed one’s Unbeatable Nascent Soul today!”

“Unbeatable Nascent Soul?”

Everyone was flummoxed. They had never heard of a nascent soul with such a name. No one could see the changes within Lu Yang’s body. Only Lu Yang, the person involved, knew best.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s consciousness entered his dantian. She had Lu Yang sever the connection, then personally took action to subdue the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

The moment the connection was cut, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul sensed grave danger and took to his heels. But how could the Everlasting Immortal Fairy give it a chance to escape?

She grabbed the Unbeatable Nascent Soul by the calf, pinned it in the dantian, and started pummeling it. Despite the Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s mastery of numerous techniques and being Lu Yang’s theoretical peak state, it couldn’t withstand the attacks of Lu Yang’s second nascent soul—the Everlasting Immortal Nascent Soul.

The first nascent soul was no match for the second nascent soul and bowed in submission at its feet.

“Appear!”

At the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s command, a plump and fair nascent soul flew out from the dantian, appearing above her head.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul bore nine parts resemblance to Lu Yang and one part resemblance to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. When Lu Yang was at the Golden Core Stage, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had cultivated in his stead for a period, thereby resulting in the nascent soul’s slight resemblance to her.

But those unfamiliar with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wouldn’t be able to tell.

“Unbeatable Nascent Soul, go! Eliminate their nascent souls!”

Chapter 836: Borrowing Without Returning

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had issued her command, and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul dared not disobey.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul conjured a hundred-zhang sword qi that swept across the assembly of heroes, stirring a sword gale. Leaves rustled incessantly, unsettling everyone’s hearts.

“A nascent soul can unleash such terrifying sword qi?” Everyone was astounded by Lu Yang’s cultivation in the Sword Dao and hastily controlled their own nascent souls.

With tacit understanding, they chose to have their nascent souls evade the attack.

Unlike the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, ordinary nascent souls couldn’t fight autonomously; cultivators needed to divert part of their attention to their nascent souls.

This gave the Everlasting Immortal Fairy an opening.

Seizing the moment while everyone controlled their nascent souls, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy struck boldly. If she were a starving wolf, these scions were a flock of lambs. Like a lamb among sheep, she struck whoever she saw.

“Take this fist!”

The Immortal Fairy Fist Technique appeared soft but was actually multifaceted and immensely powerful.

“So the Unbeatable Nascent Soul really can be used this way. This immortal didn’t guess it wrong back then,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy muttered softly.

“Immortal Fairy, what did you say?” Lu Yang didn’t catch her words.

“Ah, nothing. I said you need to cultivate diligently and defeat your Unbeatable Nascent Soul as soon as possible.”

“...Doesn’t this count as me defeating the Unbeatable Nascent Soul?” Lu Yang remembered the Everlasting Immortal Fairy saying she was his second nascent soul.

Since the second nascent soul defeated the first, doesn’t that mean I have also defeated it?

“It doesn’t work like that.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy displayed rare logical clarity as she explained the reason to Lu Yang. “You see, this immortal helped you defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, so it obeys my commands, not yours.

“And you have to obey my commands. So your relationship with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul is one of parity; there doesn’t exist a problem of who commands whom.”

Lu Yang understood. To control the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, I have two choices: either make the Everlasting Immortal Fairy obey me, or defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

Comparing the two, the second method has a higher probability of success.

In the real world, everyone was overwhelmed. The Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s attacks were too fierce. To prevent their nascent souls from being injured, they had to concentrate on controlling them.

But once they focused on dealing with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was left unattended.

“Half of the people deal with Lu Yang’s nascent soul, and the other half deal with Lu Yang himself!” someone yelled. To break the stalemate, they had to unite and act in concert.

This person was called Lin Zhongren, son of the Justice Court Grand Judge. Although he paled in comparison to Zhong Yi and the others, he was still considered fairly outstanding among his peers in the imperial city.

Now that Zhong Yi, Luo Wushuang, and Sun Chuanxian had fallen one after another, and An Nan’er remained seated beside Meng Jingyu with no intention to fight, someone had to step forward and take charge of the situation.

Lin Zhongren stepped forth to command the crowd, and everyone reluctantly acknowledged him.

“Wait, where is Lu Yang’s nascent soul?!”

To their astonishment, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul had vanished before their very eyes.

Suddenly, Lin Zhongren was struck by something. He was sent flying backward, slamming into an ancient tree.

“It’s Lu Yang’s nascent soul! Lu Yang’s nascent soul has turned invisible!” Someone reacted quickly, guessing what had happened.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul could use most of Lu Yang’s techniques. At the Foundation Establishment Stage, Lu Yang had attempted to learn a move called Invisibility Incantation, which hid only the body, but not clothes. Due to its overly niche and dubious utility, Lu Yang seldom used it.

But the Unbeatable Nascent Soul was different. It had no clothes, so it could employ it without reservation.

Lin Zhongren had wanted to step up and lead, but he was sent flying by the Unbeatable Nascent Soul. This threw the crowd into chaos again. Some dealt with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, while others searched for the Unbeatable Nascent Soul. Others even tried to step forward to take the lead, only to be defeated by the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

In the mental state, Lu Yang was pensive. To capture rebels, first capture their leader. Although the Unbeatable Nascent Soul seems to lack intelligence, it can rely on instinct to make the most reasonable responses.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul unleashed techniques without restraint while using “Swallowing Heaven” to devour the spirit energy in Luotian Forest. Everyone else’s rate of spirit energy absorption couldn’t compare. Soon, Luotian Forest’s spirit energy was depleted. Everyone’s spirit energy dwindled with each use and was no longer replenishable. Anyone who took out spirit stones to absorb the spirit energy within would have the spirit stones snatched away by the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

Watching from afar, Meng Jingzhou slapped his thigh. “Old Lu’s nascent soul is practically carved from the same mold as him!”

If I search my conscience and ask myself honestly, I know I definitely can’t do something so unscrupulous.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy applied both mental and physical pressure. Even if one ignored the Unbeatable Nascent Soul and focused on challenging the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it was pointless; she was too formidable.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy moved with tiger-like strides and dragon-like bearing, looking down upon the world and knocking down opponents with every punch. “This esteemed one told you long ago—you all are not up to it.

“Heaven and earth harbor great tribulations. This esteemed one was born in response, ordained by fate. How could you ordinary mortals be my match?

“However, considering you all possess some talent, you barely qualify to become subjects of the Great Dou Dynasty.”

Be it those who had already collapsed onto the ground or those about to collapse onto the ground, everyone was taken aback by the last sentence.

What in the world is the Great Dou Dynasty? Why haven’t we heard of it before?

“The Great Dou Dynasty is the dynasty this esteemed one intends to establish. It is the rightful orthodoxy of the world. You all may address this esteemed one as the Dou Emperor.”

It was the first time anyone had witnessed someone openly declare their intention to establish a new dynasty.

Completely disregarding Great Xia, huh?

This Lu Yang is too audacious; he’s even more lawless than the Taciturn Daoist Priest!

Lu Yang gazed helplessly at the mental space’s ceiling, feeling his reputation was tarnished.

“Is no one willing to join this esteemed one’s dynasty?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was somewhat disappointed. It seems only the Second-in-Command is willing to join the Great Dou Dynasty.

What a loyal subject.

No one had the will to fight further. Beaten by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, they discarded their armor and returned in defeat.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recalled the Unbeatable Nascent Soul and placed her hands on her hips, looking smugly at the fleeing scions. “Hmph, trying to fight this immortal? You’re far too early for that!”

In the mental space, Lu Yang wore an ingratiating expression as he negotiated with the almighty Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Your Exalted Majesty, the fight is over. Your subject’s body...”

To his surprise, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked like she wasn’t satisfied. “This imperial city seems quite fun, Xiao Yangzi. Let’s discuss—how about lending me this body to play a bit longer?”

“Ah? That...wouldn’t be so good, right?” Lu Yang hesitated. If I let the Immortal Fairy use my body again, how much worse would my reputation become?

Noticing that Lu Yang was reluctant to lend his body, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy changed tactics. “Lass Yun promised me that I can be acting sect leader for a year. This immortal has decided to use that chance now. In my capacity as acting sect leader, I now command you: hand over your body.”

After returning from the East Sea, Yun Zhi believed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s immense contributions allowed her to serve as the acting sect leader for a year. Back then, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had said she would save the opportunity for later.

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, you deliberately saved this chance to become acting sect leader just so that you can order me around, didn’t you?

“Your subject obeys the decree.”

Chapter 837: Lotus Blossom Brothel

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy called the Unbeatable Nascent Soul into the mental space once more.

After being defeated by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul no longer attacked Lu Yang on sight, appearing more subdued.

“Xiao Yingzi,[1] obey Xiao Yangzi for now. Do whatever he tells you to do.

“Xiao Yangzi, you need to spar more with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul. After all, it concerns your advancement to the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

“It’s best not to command the Unbeatable Nascent Soul to lose to you. When it comes to matters like cultivation, it’s better not to take shortcuts; be down-to-earth, lest some hidden side effects emerge at higher levels in the future.” The almighty founding emperor was concerned about a subject’s cultivation progress, testament to the subject’s standing in her heart.

Lu Yang nodded, indicating he understood.

Seeing Lu Yang so obedient gave the Everlasting Immortal Fairy a sense of satisfaction as a mentor and role model.

After instructing Lu Yang, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy prepared to experience life in the imperial city.

Meng Jingzhou was the first to reach Lu Yang. He looked at him with a strange expression and was somewhat hesitant, tentatively calling out, “Senior Everlasting?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was startled. “How did you tell?”

My disguise is practically flawless. How did this Meng boy see through it?

She quickly whispered, “Keep this to yourself. This immortal is currently the acting sect leader. I’m using that authority to temporarily possess Lu Yang and go out for some fun.”

Meng Jingzhou was filled with immense schadenfreude. Lu Yang, you brat, you were so imposing and all-powerful when you were the acting sect leader back then. Did you ever foresee this day?

“This junior understands. I won’t say a word.”

“Lu Yang-gege, are you alright?” Meng Jingyu hurried over, tugging at Lu Yang’s sleeve with concern. “Lu Yang-gege, you looked so handsome fighting everyone just now.”

“I didn’t expect you, little lass, to have such good eyesight and judgment.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was delighted to hear Meng Jingyu praise her.

“If you ever run into trouble in the future, this...I’ll have your back!” She originally intended to say “this immortal,” but then remembered she was currently using Lu Yang’s identity outwardly and needed to be cautious not to reveal herself.

If Lass Yun were to find out I’d exposed my identity, she’d definitely give me an earful.

After several rounds of battle, Luotian Forest’s ancient trees were left crooked, and the ground was churned up like earth dragons had flipped themselves and caused an earthquake. It was a messy sight. Upon returning to the Meng Estate, Meng Jingzhou asked his clan elders to restore the forest to its original state.

~~~

“Dad, I really can’t beat that Lu Yang.” An heir of a noble family returned home and reported the battle outcome to his father.

“I wasn’t the only one who acted; dozens of us besieged him, and we still couldn’t beat him. His nascent soul is ridiculously strong. Even an exceptionally gifted Divine Transfiguration cultivator couldn’t unleash that kind of sword qi!

“I wonder if Lu Yang can split his attention or if his nascent soul has some other special trait. It felt like a second Lu Yang, and its combat style was especially unscrupulous, often launching sneak attacks.”

“Such a nascent soul actually exists?”

“Exactly! I’ve never even heard of Lu Yang’s nascent soul. It’s probably self-created.”

Hearing this, the heir’s father stroked his beard pensively. “That old Taciturn brat’s little disciple really has some skill, even creating his own nascent soul.”

Although the heir hadn’t beaten Lu Yang, hitting Meng Jingzhou made him feel that the battle in Luotian Forest was still quite fulfilling.

But this sense of fulfilment is not something the older generations can experience, so there’s no need for me to mention it.

~~~

“What? Lu Yang beat all of you?” The Minister of Works was flabbergasted. My son is renowned for martial prowess; even if he’s not unbeatable among peers, he should be close. Why is the gap so large?

The Minister of Works prodded Sun Chuanxian’s forehead in frustration. “Look at you, always talking about how strong you are, so why did you fail at the critical moment?”

Sun Chuanxian wore a bitter expression. “Dad, you don’t know how strong Lu Yang is—exceptional swordsmanship, fist techniques stronger than sword techniques, mastery in various spells, and an especially powerful nascent soul. I fall short in every aspect.

“Dad, how about you suppress your cultivation realm and fight him?”

The Minister of Works rolled his eyes. I’m not stupid. Hearing Lu Yang’s battle achievements, I know I can’t win. Why would I suppress my cultivation realm to fight him?

~~~

After the Luotian Forest battle, the world once again witnessed Lu Yang’s strength. He showed the makings of an immortal, destined for a place in the upcoming Battle of the Great Era.

Of course, Lu Yang himself was completely oblivious to this. After all, he was currently being pummeled by the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, with no time to care about how the outside world evaluated him.

“Huff, huff—” Lu Yang panted heavily, watching the Unbeatable Nascent Soul warily.

He now indirectly controlled the Unbeatable Nascent Soul; otherwise, he would have been beaten even more badly.

“Nothing less from my theoretical peak state. It’s truly not easy to catch up to it.”

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul was Lu Yang’s theoretical strongest state at the Nascent Soul Stage. To defeat it, he could only hone his own skills to the pinnacle. Sparring with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul could help Lu Yang improve tremendously.

In the real world, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had temporarily taken over Lu Yang’s body, but she didn’t play nonstop. During her leisure time, she also assisted Lu Yang with his cultivation.

~~~

In the blink of an eye, the Shangyuan Festival had arrived.[2]

Meng Jingyu excitedly clamored to go out for some fun, wanting to drag Meng Jingzhou and Lu Yang along. “Lu Yang-gege, let’s go out and play!”

“Let’s go.” As soon as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy heard she could go out, she sprang up from the bed, halting her cultivation.

The Shangyuan Festival in the imperial city was especially lively. Every household was decorated with lanterns and banners, and pedestrians on the streets were jubilant, a sight that warmed the heart.

“What place is that?” “Lu Yang” suddenly pointed to a restaurant adorned with red lanterns, sensing strong worldly energy there.

Meng Jingyu shook her head, not knowing what place it was. She had never been to such a place.

Meng Jingzhou explained with an odd expression. “That’s Lotus Blossom Brothel, the Allure Sect’s base in the imperial city.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had some impression of the Allure Sect. She had even met their grand elder, Qianjiao Venerable Lord. I wonder if she has returned to the Allure Sect or is still pretending to be weak, like an old tiger disguised as a pig.

“And what does Lotus Blossom Brothel do?” “Lu Yang” pressed further.

“Lotus Blossom Brothel differs from other ordinary brothels. It’s staffed by Allure Sect disciples who sell their arts and not their bodies. These disciples are proficient in all refined arts—qin, chess, calligraphy, painting, poetry, and ballads. Brother Lu, are you interested in taking a look?”

It wasn’t Meng Jingzhou who had spoken, but someone else.

Meng Jingzhou turned and saw Zhong Yi standing beside them, elegantly fanning himself with a paper fan.

Meng Jingzhou’s expression turned unfriendly. “If I remember correctly, those who frequent Lotus Blossom Brothel are Confucian cultivators, right?”

Without some literary talent, one could easily embarrass oneself at Lotus Blossom Brothel.

Zhong Yi chuckled softly, looking at Meng Jingzhou and “Lu Yang” with a slightly provocative gaze. “What, the Taciturn Daoist Priest is proficient in poetry and ballads. As his disciple, haven’t you learned a thing?

“It sounds quite fun.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grew interested. This is a place that didn’t exist in ancient times. “Litter Sister Little Yu, shall we go in and look?”

Meng Jingyu never had the chance to visit such places and was also intrigued.

“I want to go in.”

“Then let’s go.” “Lu Yang” eagerly took Meng Jingyu’s small hand, making the latter blush.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t see anything wrong with her action. She often held Ao Ling’s and Jiang Lianyi’s hands like this in the past.

Zhong Yi’s smile froze on his face. Why am I being totally ignored?

“To completely ignore my provocation—what devious scheming.”

1. “Ying,” which means infant, is one of the characters in the term for “nascent soul.” ☜

2. The Shangyuan Festival is also known as the Yuanxiao Festival or the Lantern Festival. ☜

Chapter 838: Xiao Yangzi, Do You Know How to Write Poetry?

Lotus Blossom Brothel was extremely famous among the literati and scholars of the imperial city.

Firstly, it operated under the auspices of the Allure Sect, a legitimate S-class sect of the righteous path. Anyone who could join the Allure Sect was qualified to be called a “beauty.” The sect placed great importance on Lotus Blossom Brothel, viewing it as part of their disciples’ cultivation. One could easily imagine how incredibly stunning the beauties in Lotus Blossom Brothel were.

Secondly, those in Lotus Blossom Brothel were genuinely talented. Even members of the Imperial Hanlin Academy might not surpass them. If one’s literary works earned the Lotus Blossom Brothel’s recognition, their fame within the imperial city would swiftly follow.

Of course, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t care about such matters. She was merely there to watch the spectacle.

It was the Shangyuan Festival today, and Lotus Blossom Brothel was more bustling than usual.

Within Lotus Blossom Brothel, there was none of the heavy scent of rouge typical of common pleasure houses. On the contrary, the place resembled an elegant, chrysanthemum-like haven, frequented by refined gentlemen and graceful ladies.

There were also female cultivators clad in vibrant, long dresses gliding through the air, their sashes swaying with the breeze as they gently plucked pipa strings, evoking the beauty of a foreign land like the Buddhist Kingdom.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also spotted quite a few individuals she had hit in Luotian Forest.

Regardless of their cultivation levels, the scions of the imperial city were undoubtedly the most well-rounded in terms of their skills. From early childhood, they had studied cultivation knowledge and Confucian principles in private schools, becoming proficient in both literary and martial arts.

If one neglected to study Confucian classics and failed to master a few lines of classical poetry, it would be utterly embarrassing if they encountered a prominent figure in the future and were only capable of exclaiming “Holy shit, damn awesome!”

Lotus Blossom Brothel was a proper establishment, devoid of any bedroom affairs. It was not even strange for women to visit.

Meng Jingyu’s curiosity was no less than the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s. She gazed with wonder and envy at the beauties, who each possessed their own unique charm.

“These sisters are all so beautiful.”

“Are they?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t think much of them. She considered the Allure Sect disciples average in looks. They can’t even rank among the Top Ten Ancient Beauties, let alone compare to me, the almighty number one of that list.

“Little lass, you will definitely grow up to be more beautiful than all of them,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stated seriously. I’ve always been accurate in my judgment of people. I’m also rather fond of this young girl who had praised my combat style as dashing.

She affectionately booped Meng Jingyu’s little nose. The latter blushed and lowered her head, letting out a “mmm” that was as faint as the sound of a mosquito.

Meng Jingzhou, who had just entered, was at a loss for words.

Hold on, Senior Everlasting, could you please not use Lu Yang’s face to say such mushy things? I can’t get used to it.

In the mental space, Lu Yang paused his training session with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul and looked at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with a peculiar expression.

Immortal Fairy, do you know the concept of boundaries between men and women?

“Oh, Brother Lu is here as well?” Luo Wushuang noticed Lu Yang’s arrival at Lotus Blossom Brothel. The former’s cultivation had already been restored to the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

“Lu Yang is here?”

“That Lu Yang who demonstrated such mighty prowess in Luotian Forest?”

“Where, where?”

The battle of Luotian Forest had concluded not long ago, and memories of it remained fresh in everyone’s minds. Even those who hadn’t participated had heard about it.

“It’s quite lively upstairs.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked up at the top floor of the brothel, where Luo Wushuang stood leaning against the railing, greeting her.

“Brother Lu, why not go up and have a look? I heard the Allure Sect’s true lineage disciple, Yu Mengyin, has come here to cultivate. She’s on the top floor.” Zhong Yi once again instigated Lu Yang to go upstairs.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued ignoring Zhong Yi, taking Meng Jingyu’s hand as they went upstairs.

Meng Jingzhou raised an eyebrow, sensing ill intent from Zhong Yi. But if an immortal wishes to go upstairs, who am I to stop her?

“Brother Meng, you’re here too,” Luo Wushuang greeted with cupped fists, inviting Meng Jingzhou and the others to join him at his table.

Compared to his attire in Luotian Forest, his clothing here at Lotus Blossom Brothel was more refined and formal, lending him a more dignified bearing.

“What’s going on?” Meng Jingzhou noticed the top floor was filled with literati and scholars. At the far end was a layer of cyan gauze, behind which a female cultivator sat playing a qin. The melodious notes resembled ringing bells and were as refreshing as a spring breeze.

Luo Wushuang was taken aback. “Brother Meng, you don’t know? I thought you had also come for Ye Mengyin.”
