Meng Jingzhou knew Ye Mengyin. She’s a beauty on par with Junior Sister Tao. At the Dao-Seeking Sect’s celebration, Ye Mengyin had participated in the tournament as the Allure Sect’s representative in the Intermediate Golden Core category, and her opponent had been Meng Jingzhou.

Noticing that Meng Jingzhou was indeed unaware, Luo Wushuang explained, “Ye Mengyin has only been at Lotus Blossom Brothel for half a month, but she has already become the top courtesan. People are willing to spare no expense just to catch a glimpse of her.

“But she’s a true lineage disciple of the Allure Sect and purportedly has connections to Yejiao Venerable Lord. How could she lack spirit stones?

“Thus, Ye Mengyin established a rule: if someone can compose a poem that satisfies her, she will meet that person and perform a dance specifically for them.”

Ye Mengyin’s dance was not only peerlessly beautiful but also greatly beneficial to one’s cultivation.

Luo Wushuang gestured with his chin toward the seated crowd. “See? Five days have passed, yet no one has managed to produce a poem that pleases her.

“Today is the Shangyuan Festival. Ye Mengyin has stipulated that today’s poems must be related to the festival.”

Not everyone here came solely for Ye Mengyin’s dance; many sought to spread their reputation through the imperial city.

As they spoke, someone handed a written poem to a female attendant, who then passed it to Ye Mengyin behind the cyan gauze.

“Under the full moon, the lanterns glow as bright as day; during the Yuanxiao Festival, the festive mood fills the bustling streets. Cheerful chatter hides lantern riddles; tangyuan keeps the throat warm.”

Ye Mengyin recited the poem softly before continuing to play her qin.

The crowd erupted in laughter. It was merely an unremarkable doggerel, hardly worthy to be presented at Lotus Blossom Brothel.

The author of that poem fled in disgrace.

Swish!

Zhong Yi snapped his fan open with force. Turning to Lu Yang, he chuckled softly. “Brother Lu, as a disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest, you must be well-versed in poetry. Why not try your hand at a verse?

“Back then, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had left behind several renowned poems at the Lotus Blossom Brothel.”

He was convinced that while Lu Yang was brilliant in cultivation, he was utterly ignorant of Confucian studies. Otherwise, why has no one heard of his literary prowess before?

If Lu Yang failed to compose a poem, it would only add to the ridicule and make him a laughing stock.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was puzzled. “Since when have I been well-versed in poetry?”

Zhong Yi was dumbfounded. He hadn’t expected “Lu Yang” to admit it so bluntly, rendering his subsequent plans of provocation useless.

“Since Brother Lu is too timid to attempt it, perhaps I could have a try?” the person behind Zhong Yi said, casting a somewhat contemptuous glance at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

Only then did the Everlasting Immortal Fairy notice someone behind Zhong Yi. She pointed at the person, looking like realization had just dawned upon her. “Oh, I remember you! You were one of the people I hit in Luotian Forest!”

Just average in combat power and hardly left any impression.

In the mental space, Lu Yang felt helpless and provided the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with the person’s identity. “He’s called Yang Changbin. His father is an academician at the Imperial Hanlin Academy, while Yang Changbin himself is a Confucian cultivator. It’s said that he could write letters at the age of three, compose poems at five, and write essays at ten. His poetry and prose are quite famous in the imperial city.”

Zhong Yi had specifically brought Yang Changbin here, inviting him to compose poetry. Upon seeing Lu Yang also present at the Lotus Blossom Brothel, he had thought of making Lu Yang lose face through poetry, then have Yang Changbin step up to serve as a comparison.

Unfortunately, Lu Yang had seen through his scheme and hadn’t taken the bait.

“It’s Yang Changbin!”

“Damn it, why is he here too?!”

Yang Changbin’s reputation was greater than Lu Yang had imagined. Upon noticing Yang Changbin, the crowd wore expressions of chagrin, as though Yang Changbin’s mere attempt at poetry would guarantee him Ye Mengyin’s dance.

Yang Changbin flashed a confident smile. Before coming, he had heard of Ye Mengyin’s poetry theme and had already prepared his poem.

He instructed someone to bring ink, brush, paper, and inkstone. His brush moved like a soaring dragon and a slithering serpent as he wrote out his verse. He then had a female attendant deliver it.

Behind the cyan gauze, Ye Mengyin once again ceased her playing. She recited the poem softly and offered a rare critique. “A pity. The lines are good, but the diction is overly ornate, which instead diminishes the poem’s quality.”

The crowd burst into laughter again. Initially, when they heard Ye Mengyin recite the poem, they had all assumed it was a masterpiece worthy of her favor. Who could have guessed she could offer such a merciless critique?

Humiliated and enraged, Yang Changbin turned and glared fiercely at the crowd, his gaze particularly settling on “Lu Yang,” who was laughing the loudest.

“Brother Lu, with how loud you’re laughing, you must already have a composition in mind. Why not write it out for us all to see?!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scratched her head and hurriedly retreated into the mental space to seek help from her golden finger cheat.

“Xiao Yangzi, do you know how to write poetry?”

Lu Yang hesitated. “Writing poetry is difficult for me, but if you’re talking about reciting a few to keep up appearances, I do have some.”

Chapter 839: Transmigrating to a Cultivation World to Be a Plagiarist

“Well, Brother Lu? If you can’t compose anything, there’s no need to force it. Simply admitting it will do.” Seeing “Lu Yang” lost in thought, Yang Changbin gave a cold sneer, convinced that Lu Yang was incapable of producing a poem.

Meng Jingzhou wanted to compose a poem, but the problem was that he didn’t know how to do that. His creations would only reach the level of doggerels.

Meng Jingyu gazed pitifully at “Lu Yang”, tugging lightly on his sleeve with great concern. I can tell that Zhong Yi and Yang Changbin are deliberately targeting Lu Yang-gege.

Luo Wushuang frowned, feeling that Yang Changbin was going a bit overboard.

“Fine, I’ll write then,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said. She retrieved the four treasures of the study from her identity jade tablet, ground the ink, and began writing. In no time, she had completed a ci poem.

“So fast?” Yang Changbin furrowed his brow. This practically feels like you had prepared this in advance, writing it out without the slightest hesitation.

An inexplicable sense of foreboding arose within him. Could Lu Yang really be well-versed in the Confucian Dao?

The female attendant took the poem and passed it behind the cyan gauze to Ye Mengyin.

Ye Mengyin noticed the commotion in front of the cyan gauze. Hearing Yang Changbin demand a poem from Lu Yang, she had initially intended to help Lu Yang out of the predicament, but she never expected he could actually compose a poem on the spot.

With just a glance at those few lines, astonishment spread across her visage. Her hands trembled uncontrollably with excitement. Could this really be a ci poem composed on the spot by Fellow Daoist Lu Yang?

She had mentally prepared herself. If Lu Yang’s poetry proved lacking, she was ready to compose and recite a poem on his behalf.

Never did she imagine that Lu Yang possessed such outstanding literary talent.

“Young Miss?” the female attendant noticed something amiss with Ye Mengyin and whispered.

As if jerked out of a reverie, Ye Mengyin regained her composure and steadied her mind, preparing to recite the poem.

“Why hasn’t Fellow Daoist Ye recited the poem yet?” Zhong Yi raised an eyebrow. This was unprecedented, and everyone found it odd.

Right then, Ye Mengyin’s crisp voice came from behind the cyan gauze. “Green Jade Salver: Lantern Festival—”[1]

The crowd quieted down, all eager to hear what Lu Yang had written and find out whether it was a crude doggerel or a fine piece.

“The east wind tonight sets a thousand trees in bloom with flowers.

It also blows them down, like showers of stars.

Fine steeds and ornate carriages fill the streets with fragrance.

Xiao flutes sing like phoenixes, jade pots rotate and glow.

Fish and dragons dance through the night.”

Silence fell over the crowd.

Every person present was immersed in the scene depicted by the poem, unable to extricate themselves. “Fish and dragons dance through the night... In just a few short lines, it has painted such a vivid picture of the Shangyuan Festival.”

Many poems described the scenes of the Shangyuan Festival, but one that could immerse listeners in a dream of fantasy with just a few lines had not been seen for centuries.

Some stole glances at Yang Changbin. Regardless of how the lower stanza would turn out, just the exquisite descriptive technique of this upper stanza alone outstripped Yang Changbin’s overly flowery poem by several leagues.

Yang Changbin’s face turned ashen. He hadn’t expected the poem he had meticulously prepared to be eclipsed by Lu Yang’s impromptu creation.

He snorted coldly. So what if the upper stanza is good? If the lower stanza turns out to be nondescript, it will ruin the entire poem.

On the other hand, Meng Jingzhou wasn’t too surprised. After all, this is an omnipotent ancient immortal. Composing a few excellent poems shouldn’t be a problem.

Meng Jingyu gazed at “Lu Yang” with worshipful admiration, finding “him” more and more dashing. Is Lu Yang-gege not only highly talented in cultivation and combat, but also in poetry and prose?

Behind the cyan gauze, Ye Mengyin softly recited the lower stanza.

“Moth-shaped ornaments and snow-willow accessories adorn the ladies’ hair.

They pass by with smiles, leaving behind subtle fragrances.

I searched the crowd a thousand times.

Perchance I turned my head,

And there that person was—

In the dim glow of the lanterns.”

Upon reciting to the end, Ye Mengyin stared at the last line, lost in a trance. Earlier, she had only taken a brief glance, unable to grasp the meaning of the poem. But as she recited it before everyone, she gradually discerned Lu Yang’s intention.

“‘And there that person was—in the dim glow of the lanterns.’ Is this line written for me...?”

Utter silence.

After hearing the lower stanza, someone who was about to drink tea froze mid-motion, cup in hand, but unable to bring it to their lips.

More people turned their heads in shock to look at Lu Yang, their faces full of disbelief.

If the upper stanza was a rare, fine poem that depicted a beautiful scene, the lower stanza’s description elevated this poem to an even higher level.

A timeless masterpiece!

Once this poem emerged, it overshadowed the other poems through the ages. Any poem describing the Shangyuan Festival fell short; there was simply no comparison!

Yang Changbin had thought that even if the lower stanza was written well, he would nitpick to make Lu Yang lose face. However, when Ye Mengyin recited it, he opened his mouth and couldn’t find a single word, forced to close his mouth in defeat.

I don’t even have the qualification to critique this poem.

“Why is everyone looking at me?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy turned to look at Meng Jingyu beside her, meeting her gaze. She was baffled as to why everyone had such dramatic reactions.

Meng Jingyu was immersed in the depiction of “I searched the crowd a thousand times. Perchance I turned, and there that person was—In the dim glow of the lanterns.” Making eye contact with “Lu Yang,” her heart pounded uncontrollably.

Is this using poetry to express love? Could it be that the one Lu Yang-gege has been searching for all along...is me?

“Excellent, excellent! I didn’t expect Brother Lu to inherit the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s true legacy, capable of composing a timeless masterpiece!” Zhong Yi had intended to use this chance to humiliate Lu Yang. Never did I imagine Lu Yang to have concealed himself so well, presenting himself as a cultivation genius and never revealing his identity as a Confucian cultivator.

Zhong Yi considered himself quite scheming, but if he had such talent, he was certain he couldn’t hide it. He would have used it to gain fame long ago and wouldn’t have waited until today. Moreover, Lu Yang showed no sign of taking the bait despite Zhong Yi’s repeated provocations earlier.

Zhong Yi’s gaze toward Lu Yang held a trace of fear. Opposing someone whose heart is as deep as the abyss, I’m bound to be the unlucky one!

“You call this not well-versed in poetry?” Luo Wushuang recalled Lu Yang’s earlier words, looking at him with a mix of laughter and tears. If this counts as not proficient, no one in the world would dare call themselves a poet or bard.

“I just learned it.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rubbed the back of her head and chuckled.

I have seen such expressions from the crowd before—when I took Little Ling and Lianyi to pretend to be weak, like disguising ourselves as pigs to eat tigers.

I didn’t expect the Second-in-Command’s poem to have such an effect.

“Xiao Yangzi, you’re so amazing!” In the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Lu Yang excitedly. She hadn’t felt like this in a long time.

“Hmm? Xiao Yangzi, what’s with this expression of yours?”

Lu Yang wore a peculiar expression. He had anticipated the crowd’s reaction.

He sighed. “Nothing. I just didn’t expect my identity could be used this way.”

Lu Yang genuinely hadn’t expected that one day he could show off as a plagiarist, even though it was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy using his identity to do the showing off.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t quite understand what Lu Yang meant.

“Your identity?” She remembered Lu Yang often saying she should be a “golden finger cheat,” a “pocket grandpa,” or “pocket grandma.”

When she asked Lu Yang what that meant, he had said it referred to residing in a mental space and leveraging knowledge to help the body’s owner show off.

At the thought of this, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had a sudden realization. “Oh, I get it! By analogy with your naming, Xiao Yangzi, your current identity would be called a ‘portable old kid!’”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, I helped you show off, and this is how you repay me?

1. This is a famous poem written by Xin Qiji in the Song Dynasty. It depicts the scenes of the Yuanxiao or Shangyuan Festival, where the poet attempts to search for someone amidst the crowd, only to find her(?) in a dimly lit spot. ☜

Chapter 840: The Dance Isn't Up to Par

Pocket old kid Lu Yang was seriously pondering a question.

As a transmigrator possessing modern knowledge, I’ve not only become a disciple of the world’s number one sect, but also the junior brother of the world’s number one. I have an ancient immortal residing within my body, and the young master with the highest status is my friend. My cultivation talent is also among the top of my generation. Few throughout history can rival me.

So why is it that when it’s time to show off, it never seems to be my turn?

~~~

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, please come in for a chat.”

Once more, Ye Mengyin’s voice came from behind the cyan gauze.

No one was surprised. If a poem like Lu Yang’s couldn’t satisfy Ye Mengyin, then the problem wouldn’t be with them, but rather that Lotus Blossom Brothel was deliberately not welcoming them as guests.

Amidst the crowd’s gazes of envy and admiration, “Lu Yang” lifted the cyan gauze and laid eyes upon Ye Mengyin, who hadn’t shown her face for days.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had some recollection of Ye Mengyin. After all, I was the one who organized the Dao-Seeking Sect’s 120,000th-anniversary celebration back then.

Across the imperial city, word of Ye Mengyin’s captivating charm spread, speaking of how she was capable of making one fall for her at first sight. Indeed, Ye Mengyin was as peerlessly beautiful as the rumors claimed. Moreover, due to her innate allure bone, every movement exuded a unique grace. In terms of seductive appeal alone, she surpassed even Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting.

However, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt none of this. Ye Mengyin isn’t as good-looking as I am.

Ye Mengyin met “Lu Yang”’s clear gaze and was quite surprised. My allure bone affects even my fellow sect sisters. Meng Jingzhou’s victory over me back then had also relied on pure willpower.

Yet Lu Yang is now looking at me with such clear eyes—this is a first.

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, it’s been a long while since we last met. How about we move to a side chamber for a chat?” Ye Mengyin blushed. It was her first time inviting a male cultivator to her private boudoir.

They were only separated from the crowd by a single layer of gauze. Their voices and movements were clearly audible and visible, making it difficult to act freely.

“Sure.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t overthink it, agreeing readily.

Inside the boudoir, Ye Mengyin added a cinnabar dot to her brow. She wore a vibrant dress whose hem was embroidered with intricate, iridescent patterns of flying apsaras and auspicious clouds.

Watching this dance was greatly beneficial for cultivating one’s mental state.

“Your dance isn’t up to par.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t bear to continue watching. This dancing level is too poor, far inferior to Zhu Tian’s.

“When one dances, the body must move with the heart. Look at your movements—you are dancing completely by rote and lack spirit. Come, learn from me.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy personally took to the floor to demonstrate. Her movements were light and graceful, like a breathtakingly beautiful immortal fairy emerging from an ancient painting. Every smile and frown carried an inexplicable charm, far eclipsing dances like Ye Meng Yin’s that relied on enhancement from the allure bone.

Ye Mengyin was dumbfounded. Senior Brother Lu Yang knows how to dance too?

She had entered the Dao through dance and possessed the highest talent for the Dance Dao within the Allure Sect. Otherwise, she wouldn’t have been qualified to represent the sect at the Dao-Seeking Sect tournament.

Ye Mengyin had thought no one her age could outshine her in dancing.

Who would have thought? There’s indeed no one among female cultivators. But there is one among male cultivators.

“Could it be that the Taciturn Daoist Priest is also skilled at dancing?” Ye Mengyin recalled the rumors about the Taciturn Daoist Priest but hadn’t heard of such a thing.

Although the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s dance was elegant and moving, she was currently using Lu Yang’s body, which made it appear quite awkward to oblivious observers.

Fortunately, Ye Mengyin truly loved dance. She didn’t mind Lu Yang’s strange incongruity and earnestly followed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s instructions.

“Ah, that’s right. You must contemplate the meaning of the dance, not merely imitate it.”

In truth, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy danced better than Zhu Tian. Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi had both learned from her. However, she was mindful of her high status. During the gatherings of immortals in ancient times, she would let Zhu Tian perform on stage while she simply watched. Although Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi had learned from her, they still couldn’t compare to Zhu Tian in terms of talent in the Dance Dao.

In the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy adorned her hair with pearl and gold ornaments, her hair coiled high. Vermillion eyeshadow graced the corners of her eyes, and she wore a bright yellow robe as she danced elegantly within the grand hall. From her jet-black hair tips to her perfectly round toes, every inch of her skin radiated abundant vitality.

It had been a long time since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had danced. She needed to dance synchronously in both the mental space and the real world to recapture the feeling.

Lu Yang watched the Everlasting Immortal Fairy dance in a daze. He seriously pondered which minister in history had ever had the privilege of watching the emperor dance.

After the dance, Ye Mengyin was panting heavily from exhaustion, but her smile was especially bright. She could feel her progress in the Dance Dao, and it was significant progress.

“Many thanks for your guidance, Senior Brother Lu Yang!” She bowed seriously, not daring to slight him.

This round of guidance had saved her a decade of arduous cultivation. Calling him “benefactor-mentor” wouldn’t be an exaggeration.

However, one thing still eluded her understanding. That final line Lu Yang wrote—“and there that person was—in the dim glow of the lanterns”—what does it exactly mean? Was it really written for me? If it were for me, why do I feel like his behavior after entering my boudoir didn’t quite seem to match?

Could it be that Senior Brother Lu Yang found my talent in the Dance Dao too poor and was disappointed in me?

The more Ye Mengyin thought about it, the more she felt this was plausible.

~~~

News of “Lu Yang” composing poetry at Lotus Blossom Brothel spread rapidly throughout the imperial city, even shocking the great Confucian masters at the Imperial Hanlin Academy.

Good poems could not only be passed down through the ages, but more importantly, they could also serve as a cultivation method for Confucian cultivators.

“This is even better than the works of the old Taciturn scoundrel! I’m afraid Lu Yang’s achievements aren’t completely the credit of that old Taciturn scoundrel; his own innate talent for the Confucian Dao is astonishing!”

“Spells, mighty abilities, sword cultivation, Confucian cultivation... This talent of his outstrips even that old Taciturn scoundrel’s. The outside world says he has the makings of an immortal. The rumors are true!”

“Pay attention to this line from the lower stanza: I searched the crowd a thousand times. Perchance I turned my head, and there that person was—in the dim glow of the lanterns.” The outside world speculates that this was written for a little girl from the Allure Sect, but this old man holds a different opinion.”

“Brother Zeng, care to elaborate?”

“All of you should have heard many rumors about Lu Yang, right? Among those rumors, have you ever heard one about romantic affairs? Not once, right? This suggests that Lu Yang likely doesn’t care for such matters, and this poem isn’t as shallow as people claim.

“Look at this line under that premise. Who does ‘that person’ refer to? It’s very likely referring to himself!

“In that case, the meaning of this line is: After Lu Yang endured countless hardships in cultivation, he wished to seek something yet couldn’t find it. Finally, he had an epiphany and discovered that what he sought was his true heart!

“I have seen many too many cultivators who lost their true hearts after embarking on the path of cultivation. Although they achieved success in cultivation, they gave off a muddled feeling, causing them to falter in their subsequent advancements.

“To know others is wisdom, to know oneself is enlightenment. Lu Yang wrote this cultivation insight into his poem to remind and awaken many cultivators, making them introspect and break through their mental barriers!”

“Hiss, that does seem to be the case. This child possesses great talent.”

~~~

The Second Imperial Prince’s Official Residence.

The Second Imperial Prince examined the intelligence in his hand with a blazing gaze.

“If I want to seize the throne, Lu Yang’s assistance is indispensable. It is time to make contact with him.”

Chapter 841: Great Folly Appears as Wisdom

The Second Imperial Prince hadn’t found any lifespan-extending immortal grass in the Eastern Sea.

However, this did not affect his plans.

If I could find the immortal grass in the East Sea to prolong Emperor Father’s life, my standing in Emperor Father’s heart would rise, potentially even surpassing Big Brother, leading to my appointment as the crown prince.

If I couldn’t find the immortal herb, that’s also fine. Emperor Father would still witness my filial piety. Compared to Big Brother, who did nothing, this is still an advantage.

Moreover, this journey to the East Sea was genuinely perilous. A clash between two immortals at the Dragon Palace had broken out. If I had been slightly caught in the aftershocks, I would have met my demise. With all those dangers I’ve braved, Emperor Father can’t possibly remain unmoved.

Thus, it doesn’t matter whether I found the immortal grass. What matters is that I went to the East Sea.

Despite this, after he returned, he waited a year. The Xia Emperor had grown increasingly frail, yet there was still no sign of a crown prince being appointed. This inevitably made him somewhat anxious.

Coincidentally, Lu Yang arrived in the imperial city at this time. Drawing on the bond they had formed at the East Sea, he invited Lu Yang to his residence for a chat and to strengthen their rapport. Asking Lu Yang to help me ascend the throne will naturally follow.

Few knew that the Second Imperial Prince was a meticulous person.

~~~

“Hmm? The Jiang Family’s second son wants to invite this immortal over?” After receiving the invitation, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that the imperial city was truly bustling. She received invitations daily. Apart from the Jiang Family’s second son’s invitation, many invitations from scholars and literati arrived in quick succession, all inviting “Lu Yang” to compose and recite poetry. She had declined them all per Lu Yang’s wishes.

“Your Majesty, you must call him the Second Imperial Prince,” Lu Yang reminded. If she calls him the “Jiang Family’s second son” to his face, she can expect a foul expression in return.

“Oh, alright then.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was a qualified emperor who readily accepted advice. She would listen to whatever Lu Yang said.

“Then let’s go to the Jiang Family’s second son’s home.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy enjoyed lively places. The invitation states that the Jiang Family’s second son will host a banquet in Lu Yang’s honor.

“Let’s also bring Old Meng. He’s more familiar with matters in the imperial city. That way, when we arrive at the Jiang Family’s second son’s...the Second Imperial Prince’s home, we won’t be completely in the dark,” Lu Yang suggested, nearly following the way the Everlasting Immortal Fairy addressed him.

Upon learning that the Second Imperial Prince intended to host Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou frowned slightly. Based on my understanding of the Second Imperial Prince, I’m afraid this banquet won’t be merely a simple meal.

But since the immortal wishes to go, I dare not stop her. At worst, if any trouble arises, I will shield the immortal.

This time, Meng Jingzhou didn’t bring Meng Jingyu. It was unsuitable for Meng Jingyu to tag along for such an occasion.

The Second Imperial Prince’s banquet was set for three days later. When the time came, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, along with Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, headed to the banquet.

The Second Imperial Prince regarded Lu Yang highly. On the day of the banquet, he personally greeted “Lu Yang” and Meng Jingzhou at the entrance.

Spotting them approaching from afar, he jogged over. His face wore a warm smile that was just right, and he greeted them with cupped fists. “Gentlemen, it’s been a year since we parted in the East Sea. I have missed you greatly.”

Meng Jingzhou wore a similar smile, returning the salute. “Your Highness is too polite.”

“Please, come inside.”

“After you.”

The Second Imperial Prince’s purpose for hosting the banquet was to welcome Lu Yang. Now that the key figure had arrived, the banquet naturally commenced.

Perhaps fearing the banquet might lack liveliness, the Second Imperial Prince had also invited many scions. Lu Yang recognized a few, but he hadn’t seen most of them before, indicating that not all the scions invited were peers of the same age.

After the three took their seats, the Second Imperial Prince spoke first. “I have long heard of Fellow Daoist Lu Yang’s arrival in the imperial city. Unfortunately, I have been occupied with official duties and haven’t had time to receive you. Today, I have finally found the time to welcome you properly. I hope you will not take offense.

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang has certainly made a grand splash in the imperial city. Not only did you beat all the geniuses of your generation here, but you also composed a poem at Lotus Blossom Brothel, earning resounding applause from the crowd. Even the great Confucian masters of the Hanlin Imperial Academy have praised your poem effusively, lauding its ability to illuminate one’s clear heart and true nature.

“Come, let me introduce these individuals to you.

This is Hong Guanshan, grandson of the Minister of the Treasury.

“This is Kong De, son of the Grand Governor’s Office Chief Secretary.

“This is...”

The Second Imperial Prince introduced them one by one. Hong Guanshan and the others wore proud smiles; their identities were their pride.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy simply nodded politely. She was uninterested in these people’s identities. Besides, I have no idea what a “Minister of the Treasury” or the like actually does.

Listening by the side, Meng Jingzhou’s expression shifted slightly. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy might not understand what these individuals represented, but he certainly did.

These people were involved in every aspect of Great Xia—the military, finance, security of the imperial city, and more. If they could all be rallied to the Second Imperial Prince’s cause, they would form an immensely powerful force.

This was the Second Imperial Prince displaying to Lu Yang the number of backers he had.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grew somewhat impatient listening and finally couldn’t help but ask, “Why do you keep mentioning who their fathers and grandfathers are when you introduce them? Aren’t they famous themselves?

“Look, when I introduce myself, I just say I’m Lu Yang, and everyone knows me. There’s no need to say anything else.”

Once those words left her mouth, the smiles on the faces of Hong Guanshan and the others stiffened. This had struck a sore point of theirs.

With just a single encounter, she has made us feel utterly ashamed. This ability to perceive the subtlest details is truly terrifying! No wonder His Highness the Second Imperial Prince is so desperate to win Lu Yang over!

“Moreover, what does their status have to do with me?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked, perplexed. I don’t care what their names are, so why bother about who their fathers and grandfathers are?

Better to finish the introductions quickly and start the banquet.

The Second Imperial Prince’s heart skipped a beat. I refuse to believe that Lu Yang doesn’t understand my underlying intentions. But he said he doesn’t care about their identities and status. Is he trying to hint that he’s unwilling to participate in this struggle for the throne?

The Second Imperial Prince decided not to continue showcasing his backing and instead proceeded with the banquet as Lu Yang had wished.

The banquet proceeded smoothly, with female dancers providing entertainment, cups clinking, and everyone drinking and making merry.

The dancers moved gracefully, but compared to Ye Mengyin, they were like minor magicians in the presence of a great magician. Compared to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, they weren’t even fit to hold her shoes. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had little interest in watching them dance.

“Having Zhu Tian instead would be more like it.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy wasn’t fond of alcohol. She remembered that the Epoch Immortal once used his body to brew a jar of immortal wine. Its aroma was so potent that even a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator would become dizzy and feel like they had been transported to an immortal land with just a sniff. Back then, the Qilin Immortal and the Nine-Layers Immortal had drunk straight from the jar. They got drunk and caused a ruckus, which was rather unbecoming.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that as the head of the Ten Ancient Beauties, she must be mindful of her status and not engage in such déclassé behavior. Hence, she had always harbored some resistance toward wine.

“By the way, Xiao Yangzi, would you like to see the scene of the Qilin Immortal and the Epoch Immortal throwing a drunken tantrum? I still have a recording here.”

Lu Yang hurriedly shook his head. Anyone who sees this will die. I still want to live a few more years.

The Second Imperial Prince drank until he was thoroughly intoxicated. Riding the alcohol’s influence, he leaned close to Lu Yang and began pouring out his woes.

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, my heart is filled with bitterness. Emperor Father is reaching the limit of his lifespan, yet the matter of succession remains undecided. Big Brother claims to have no interest in the throne, but there is no kinship in imperial families. Who can say for sure?

“And there’s also Old Four and Old Five. They also claim to have no interest in the throne, yet they all have preparations in secret.”

The Second Imperial Prince shook his head and sighed, his genuine feelings slipping through. “The winds and clouds in the imperial city are unpredictable. Fellow Daoist, you are an outsider and see things most clearly. Tell me, who will ultimately seize the throne?”

Upon hearing the Second Imperial Prince’s words, the crowd, who had been drinking and enjoying themselves, pretended to converse while secretly observing Lu Yang’s reaction.

His Highness is using the alcohol as an excuse to lay his cards on the table, hoping to know whether Lu Yang will join our faction.

Meng Jingzhou’s expression changed slightly as realization dawned upon him. If the answer contains any flaw, it may drag both the Meng Family and the Dao-Seeking Sect into the struggle for the throne!

But both the Meng Family and the Dao-Seeking Sect have always maintained a neutral stance and don’t participate in the contention for the throne!

Such a precedent must not be set!

Realization also dawned upon Lu Yang. This is the Second Imperial Prince’s true objective in inviting me here.

He’s forcing me to choose a side!

I must answer cautiously and not give the Second Imperial Prince an opening to exploit.

Just as Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were pondering how they should respond, they saw the Everlasting Immortal Fairy reveal a surprised expression.

She asked, “So it’s actually up to me who gets to be emperor?”

Chapter 842: Should Learn More from the Immortal Fairy

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had initially thought that establishing the Great Dou Dynasty would require some effort. For instance, Yun Zhi and her might need to personally take action, overthrow the Great Xia Dynasty, and set up a new imperial court.

Considering that overthrowing Great Xia couldn’t be solved by force alone and would likely encounter numerous obstacles in practice, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been too lazy to establish the Great Dou Dynasty in the outside world.

Who would have thought? Great Xia’s imperial family is so amenable. Whoever I want to be emperor gets to be emperor.

I'm currently the Acting Sect Leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Ruler of the Heavenly Court, and soon to be the founding emperor of the Great Bean Dynasty. The leaders of the three largest factions in the world are all me. This is a level of treatment I hadn’t even enjoyed in ancient times.

That’s why I said there isn’t so much scheming in the world. See? Everyone is a good person.

Lu Yang stared at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy in shock and suspicion. Immortal Fairy, your previous intelligence was all an act, right?”

“Xiao Yangzi, why are you staring at me?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked Lu Yang in bewilderment. It’s my first time seeing the Second-in-Command show such an astonished expression.

“N-nothing. I just think you’re quite clever, Immortal Fairy.”

“Of course, this immortal is clever.” Although I don’t understand why the Second-in-Command suddenly said this, hearing him praise my intelligence still makes me happy.

In the real world, Meng Jingzhou was filled with reverence toward the Everlasting Immortal Fairy due to her response. Truly an immortal! Not only has her cultivation been supreme since ancient times, but her emotional intelligence is also so high, leaving others in the dust.

In contrast, it’s such a waste to have the immortal accompany Lu Yang. So many years have passed, yet he hasn’t learned a thing, spending all day just to scheme against me.

He should study properly in his mental space!

Upon hearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s response, the expressions of those present changed.

What astuteness! Not only did she skillfully avoid answering, but she also trapped the Second Imperial Prince!

Whether the Second Imperial Prince answers “Lu Yang gets to decide” or “Lu Yang doesn’t get to decide” will be wrong.

If he says the former, it will be treason, a capital offense. If he says the latter, it will imply that Lu Yang is useless, and the Second Imperial Prince will not have the face to befriend him again.

Such scheming, such calculation, combined with such stunning cultivation—no wonder he’s called the number one of the younger generation!

Even the Taciturn Daoist Priest couldn’t achieve this level in this youth!

Fortunately, the Second Imperial Prince was meticulous. Although he was startled by “Lu Yang”’s answer, he continued feigning drunkenness. This way, even if trouble arises in the future, I’ll have an excuse.

To his surprise, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued speaking. “If you don’t know who should be emperor, then I shall do it. Would you like to seek a position under me?”

The Second Imperial Prince broke into a cold sweat on the spot and didn’t dare to continue his drunken act.

If I continue pretending, who knows what other treasonous words Lu Yang may utter?

He had heard that back in Luotian Forest, Lu Yang had once boasted conceitedly about wanting to establish a Great Dou Dynasty. Now he’s bringing up this topic again.

Could it be that he had already anticipated my actions back in Luotian Forest?!

What terrifying calculation.

Some jokes Lu Yang can make, but I can’t.

Who is Lu Yang? He’s the next Sect Leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect, highly valued by the half-immortal Yun Zhi. During his disappearance in the East Sea, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord had personally gone to the East Sea to search for him, demonstrating how much importance he places on Lu Yang. Not to mention that Lu Yang had saved the Dragon Ancient Ancestor.

A future immortal sect leader with extremely close ties to three half-immortals—be it in status or background, no one can match him.

As long as Lu Yang only speaks about it, it doesn’t count as real rebellion. Who would dare lay a finger on him?

Not even Emperor Father would dare.

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, you jest.” The Second Imperial Prince dared not continue the conversation. If I keep going along with him, I should forget about inheriting the throne; whether I can retain my title as prince will be uncertain.

The Second Imperial Prince’s gaze toward “Lu Yang” held a trace of awe. It’s the first time I’ve encountered a genius whose scheming is even more meticulous than mine.

There are always people beyond people, just like there are skies beyond skies.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t understand why everyone looked at her with awe. Is it because I’m going to be emperor?

That does make sense.

The Second Imperial Prince changed the subject, pointing at the female dancers again. “Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, are you interested in these dancers? If so, you may take them all back. Dual cultivation with them can also boost your cultivation.”

“What would I want them for?”

Seeing Lu Yang decline, the Second Imperial Prince wasn’t surprised. With a bright pearl like Ye Mengyin setting the standard, these dancers are indeed unlikely to catch his eye.

He clapped his hands. A procession of attendants carrying trays filed out from a side chamber. On the trays were various rare treasures and cultivation secret manuals, all greatly beneficial for cultivation. Any single item would qualify as the highlight of an auction. Even the other invited guests felt a surge of envy at the sight of these treasures.

His Highness really spared no expense, huh?

“I felt an instant connection with Fellow Daoist Lu Yang and have prepared some humble gifts. I hope you will accept them without disdain.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy indeed disdained the gifts. With just a glance, she recognized the origins of these items. They’re of no use to me; even the stones at the entrance of my cave abode are more valuable than these things.

Then again, these things aren’t for my use, but for Lu Yang’s.

In that case, they’re somewhat helpful.

The Second Imperial Prince had conscientiously prepared these treasures for Lu Yang, aiming to secure a potential ally. If Lu Yang accepts these items, it would indicate he leans toward my side.

The Second Imperial Prince secretly observed Lu Yang’s reaction, feeling extremely nervous.

“Given for free?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that the imperial city truly had many good people.

“Naturally.” The Second Imperial Prince nodded with a smile.

“Then I won’t stand on ceremony. Thank you.”

The lead attendant produced a storage ring, stowed away the items from the trays into it, and respectfully presented it with both hands.

Seeing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy accept the storage ring, the Second Imperial Prince’s smile broadened.

It seems everything he said previously was because he didn’t want to be probed. At the very least, he has accepted these treasures. Even if he doesn’t support me in the future, he won’t oppose me either.

Given for free? One should not accept rewards without merit. How could there truly be free things in this world? Everything comes with a price.

“Immortal Fairy, you shouldn’t have taken those things.” In the mental space, pocket old kid Lu Yang remarked with slight concern. If it were me, I wouldn’t have accepted anything from the Second Imperial Prince.

“Hmm? Why can’t this immortal accept them?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was puzzled as to why her golden cheat finger was so anxious

“Accepting the gifts is equivalent to you choosing a side.”

“Choosing a side? What side?”

“Eat someone’s food, and the mouth grows quiet; accept someone’s gifts, and the hand grows tame.” Lu Yang tried to explain it as simply as possible.

“Didn’t this immortal confirm before taking them? They were given for free,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stated. She acted with caution and left no loopholes.

“Then in the future, if you become enemies, would you attack the Second Imperial Prince?”

“Of course, I would.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy found the Second-in-Command’s question baffling.

“Besides, this immortal didn’t take them for free. I said thank you.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Is my skin too thin? Should I learn more from the Immortal Fairy?

Chapter 843: So the Xia Emperor’s Status Is Actually This High

Upon returning to the Meng Estate, Meng Jingzhou sought out his father and recounted in detail the events that had transpired at the Second Imperial Prince’s Official Residence.

Meng Potian was not surprised by the Second Imperial Prince’s actions to win Lu Yang over. He looked at Lu Yang with a smile. “Among the nine imperial princes, the Second Imperial Prince isn’t the only one who wants to make contact with Little Lu. It seems that he was the first one who couldn’t restrain himself. That’s normal; his usual behavior shows that he is poor at keeping his composure.”

“He’s not the only one?” Meng Jingzhou was stunned. Old Lu is so popular?

“Since the First Imperial Prince demonstrates little interest in inheriting the throne, it’s inevitable that other imperial princes develop ambitions. According to the intelligence that we have gathered, the Fourth Imperial Prince and the Fifth Imperial Prince have intentions to contend for the throne.”

“Is the throne that attractive?” Meng Jingzhou thought the throne was utterly useless. I wouldn’t take it even if it’s offered to me.

Meng Potian glanced at his son and Lu Yang. They’re all family; nothing is off-limits. “That is the throne. It bears the nation’s fortune and carries the will of the people. It’s a position above all but one. If that person within the imperial palace’s forbidden ground doesn’t act, the Xia Emperor is the most exalted person under heaven. No one can defy his wishes.”

In the mental space, Lu Yang pondered upon hearing Meng Potian’s words. It does seem true. The Xia Emperor does appear to be a considerably exalted person.

“But why didn’t I feel this way before?” Lu Yang was puzzled, recalling his previous impression of the Xia Emperor.

His initial contact with the Xia Emperor was when the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wanted the Xia Emperor to be the Fourth-in-Command. Subsequently, when the Everlasting Immortal Fairy became the acting sect leader, she went to the imperial palace and challenged the four sect leaders of the Great Immortal Sects, even wanting to challenge the Xia Emperor. This frightened the Xia Emperor into granting Lu Yang the privileges of attending court without hastening, being announced with only his title, and wearing his sword and shoes into the palace hall.

After those experiences, coupled with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy constantly chattering about the embarrassing antics of the ancient immortals, it was difficult for Lu Yang to feel any sense of reverence toward the Xia Emperor.

“You have also had contact with Great Yu cultivators, especially the Great Yu Alliance’s Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, whom the Dao-Seeking Sect captured, the missing Sixth Yu Emperor Wu Youdao, and Great Yu’s Second Imperial Preceptor. Why have they all chosen to awaken at this time? Was it merely to become immortals? No—they also intend to replace Great Xia and rebuild Great Yu.”

Meng Potian wasn’t aware that Wu Youdao and the Second Imperial Preceptor had also been captured by the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“It is said that the person in the imperial palace’s forbidden ground will not act unless the survival of Great Xia is at stake. Therefore, whoever ascends the throne is effectively the ruler of the Central Continent.”

“What cultivation realm is that person in the forbidden ground at?” Meng Jingzhou had long heard there was an ancestor of the Jiang Family in the imperial palace’s forbidden ground.

Meng Potian’s expression turned grave, as if he was discussing a taboo.

He slowly uttered, “Immortal.”

“Oh, I figured as much.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Meng Jingzhou calmly accepted this fact, displaying none of the dramatic change in expression that Meng Jingzhou had anticipated.

The founding emperors of Great Qian and Great Yu were immortals, so it was logical that Great Xia also had an immortal.

Meng Potian’s face twitched slightly. What have you two brats been exposed to outside? How can you have no reaction to an immortal?

“No wonder our family’s ancestor couldn’t defeat the Jiang Family’s ancestor.” Meng Jingzhou now understood why his ancestor had lost. Since Jiang Ping’an was an immortal, how could Meng Junzi possibly have won?

“Our ancestor wasn’t competitive enough. If he had won, I would be the First Imperial Prince now.”

Meng Jingzhou felt the weight on his shoulders grow a little heavier. It seems the task of producing an immortal for the Meng Family has fallen to me.

“So you now understand why the throne is so important. It’s equivalent to being the immortal’s spokesperson.”

Just then, a knock sounded at the door. Steward Xu pushed it open and entered.

“Patriarch, someone has come to repay a debt.”

Steward Xu rarely addressed Meng Potian as “Big Brother.” Calling him that gave the impression that they were some kind of underworld organization, especially with a line like “Big Brother, someone has come to repay a debt.” It makes our Meng Family feel like some illegal operation.

Our Meng Family has always operated within the law, unlike diabolic creeds, which are unregistered illegal organizations.

“Who is it?” Meng Potian asked. Typically, routine lending and repayment can be handled by Xu You. As the family head, he shouldn’t need to get involved.

For Xu You to notify me suggests that the other party has a high status, or that the repayment amount is substantial.

“That person calls himself Shi Huagu and wishes to repay a debt of one billion spirit stones.”

Meng Potian nodded. “One billion spirit stones. That is indeed a significant sum.

“Shi Huagu... I recall the ‘One More Time Barbeque’ chain is his venture, right?” Meng Potian had some recollection of this new, rising business genius.

“But I don’t recall us lending him money.” Especially a loan of one billion spirit stones—I’d definitely remember.

“That promissory note has been examined. It was indeed issued by our Meng Family. However, there are traces of karmic abilities modifying the ‘debtor’ field. It appears he voluntarily assumed the debt of the previous debtor.”

Meng Potian was deeply moved. I never imagined there’d be such a loyal and righteous person in the world. “Let’s go, take me to see him.”

With one foot already out of the door, Meng Potian turned his head and called to Meng Jingzhou and Lu Yang. “You two probably haven’t seen the debt repayment process before. Come and have a look too; consider it broadening your horizons.”

Even if Meng Potian had proposed that, Meng Jingzhou would have gone to watch the spectacle.

He was too familiar with the name Shi Huagu.

~~~

The Meng Estate’s reception area.

The reception area had many private rooms. Their quality varied depending on the value of the business conducted.

In a high-class private room, Shi Huagu nervously awaited the arrival of someone from the Meng Family with decision-making authority.

“Don’t be nervous. Haven’t you saved up the one billion spirit stones?” The creed leader Mu Baiyi had also come. Shi Huagu’s debt was considered a legacy issue from the previous creed leader, making it half an official business. Thus, he came along to avoid any mishaps along the way.

“Finally, no more being struck by lightning.” Shi Huagu was quite emotional. He had waited a full four years for this day, enduring one lightning tribulation every month. That was fifty lightning tribulations in total. It’s a miracle that I’m still alive.

I shouldn’t have been so grabby back then. Why did I have to snatch Qin Haoran’s treasure?

Treasure my ass!

If not for the Heavenly Court Creed appearing and showing me the way, who knows how many lifetimes it would take for me to earn this many spirit stones?

“You must be Shi Huagu?”

Meng Potian turned up with Meng Jingzhou and “Lu Yang,” his face beaming with a warm and genuine smile.

“Yes.”

Noticing Meng Jingzhou and “Lu Yang,” Shi Huagu was momentarily taken aback, not expecting them to be present. He had met Lu Yang once when he was seeking Tao Yaoye’s help for advertising. As for Meng Jingzhou, he had only seen his portraits.

Mu Baiyi had met them both at the corpse-driving inn in the Wilderness Province.

Just two talented juniors. Shi Huagu didn’t dwell on it. He handed over Qin Haoran’s promissory note and the storage ring containing one billion spirit stones to Meng Jinggzhou, nervously awaiting the outcome.

Meng Potian first examined the promissory note meticulously. Our Meng Family always follows the rules; we won’t accept money that isn’t rightfully ours.

Then, he inspected the storage ring three times. Our Meng Family always follows the rules; we can’t lose out on any money that is rightfully ours.

“Mmm, the promissory note is real. The storage ring indeed contains one billion spirit stones.”

Hearing this, Shi Huagu heaved a sigh of relief. He stood up to take his leave, only to be stopped by Meng Potian.

“Wait a moment. You haven’t repaid the interest yet.”

Chapter 844: This Is Much Faster Than Robbery

“Interest?” Shi Huagu’s body gave a shudder.

It was hard to imagine a Fusion Stage expert being unable to control his own body.

“Of course. Loans naturally have interest. Otherwise, why would we lend you the money?” Meng Potian said matter-of-factly. He couldn’t understand why Shi Huagu was reacting so strongly.

The Meng Family isn’t running a charity. We can’t just lend money to anyone as long as they pay it back. If that were the case, the Meng Family would have gone bankrupt long ago.

Shi Huagu’s smiling face looked even worse than if he were crying.

Damn it, how could I have completely overlooked the existence of interest?

Beside him, Mu Baiyi also lost his composure, even though he was supposedly here to support his subordinate. He had forgotten about the interest too.

Not only does Shi Huagu owe money, but I do as well.

However, he had borrowed the money from the Luodi Merchant Guild after changing into the appearances of all the creed members. He had thought that once the barbeque shops were profitable enough, he could repay the debt as soon as possible to avoid the matter coming to light.

If this gets exposed, I won’t survive even if I’m at the Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

“H-how much is the interest?” Shi Huagu was so frightened that he stumbled over his words, wishing he could dig up Qin Haoran’s corpse and whip it.

Meng Potian was quite enthusiastic about a major client like Shi Huagu. Moreover, he admired Shi Huagu’s loyalty and righteousness for daring to assume such a debt.

However, admiration aside, accounts have to be settled clearly.

“You see, it was clearly stated at the time of the loan—this is a ‘Tribulation Safety Insurance.’ As long as you successfully advance to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, the interest stops accruing, and you only need to repay the principal. If you fail the tribulation, the interest is calculated at twelve percent per annum.”

Meng Potian wrote the calculation process in the air to help Shi Huagu understand.

“Forty years have passed since the original loan. At the time of the loan, it was stipulated that repayment would adopt the ‘equal principal and interest’ method. For a loan of one billion, the average monthly repayment would be about...one thousand one hundred...subtracting the one billion you’ve already paid, forty-five billion remains.

The air was filled with dense calculations, causing Shi Huagu’s heart to tremble with fear.

As a Fusion cultivator, he did not lack such simple computational ability. He just couldn’t accept this reality.

Beside him, Mu Baiyi’s eye twitched. If we had this many spirit stones, Fengdu Ghost City would have been built long ago.

And this is only what Shi Huagu owes. I myself owe even more.

I had originally thought I could repay the debt early and accelerate Fengdu Ghost City’s construction. But now, I suppose I should forget about it. Fengdu Ghost City can be built slowly; there’s no need to rush.

Currently, the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and the Radiant Sun Creed are thriving under the Heavenly Court Creed’s leadership. With Young Creed Leader Lu’s guidance, the Radiant Sun Creed quickly shifted their research direction. Items such as solar candles are about to enter the market, likely capable of earning spirit stones even faster than opening barbeque shops.

Mu Baiyi tried his best to think positively.

In the mental space, Lu Yang thought, No wonder your Meng Family follows the laws so strictly. This legal money-making method is faster than illegal activities.

Even if you make Shi Huagu go around robbing people, he still can’t get this much.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt deep regret. “What a pity! This immortal lost out big time! I should have found a bank to deposit some spirit stones. After three hundred thousand—no, four hundred thousand years—how many spirit stones could this immortal have earned?!”

“...Uh, let me ask something. Your Majesty, are you certain any bank could have operated from ancient times until now?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy contemplated. Xiao Yangzi has a point.

Hence, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy returned to her usual cheerful self.

~~~

Shi Huagu and Mu Baiyi left the Meng estate, both crestfallen.

“Creed Leader, what now? Do we return to the headquarters?”

Mu Baiyi shook his head. “Haven’t you noticed? The standard of living for the imperial city’s populace is higher than in other cities. This implies that their ability to embrace new things is greater. Previously, when we opened barbeque shops, we started from small places and gradually spread to surrounding cities.

“Barbeque shops are common. Our advantage is the good flavor, something universally accepted. It’s not exactly a novel concept.

“But the things invented by the Radiant Sun Creed aren’t necessarily something anyone can accept immediately. To open up the solar energy market, I think we should start from the imperial city.

“How about this? You go contact the people from the Radiant Sun Creed. Let’s all come to the imperial city for a site inspection.”

Shi Huagu thought, No wonder he’s the creed leader. His observational and thinking skills are stronger than mine.

......

~~~

“Emperor Father, your son has returned.”

Within the imperial palace, the dignified First Imperial Prince paid respects to the Xia Emperor.

Three months ago, someone reported officials in Ji province for corruption, deception, and covering up. Jiang Qun traveled to Ji Province to investigate corrupt officials, traveling incognito and visiting the commoners to search for clues. When he encountered obstacles from officials, he revealed his identity to intimidate them. Incidentally, he also met a beautiful companion and gained a promising romance. Now, he had just returned to the imperial city.

Who would have thought that Emperor Father has aged so much in just three months?

That high-spirited Xia Emperor was nowhere to be seen. The current Xia Emperor resembled an old man on the verge of decay. His face was wreathed in wrinkles, and his eyelids drooped, covering his eyes.

Wasn’t it originally said that he has ten years of lifespan left? Less than half that time has passed, and he already seems to be on the verge of collapse!

The Xia Emperor favored his eldest son the most. Seeing Jiang Qun return, he smiled and put down the memorial booklet in his hand, beckoning him over.

“Emperor Father, your health...” A wave of sorrow rose in Jiang Qun’s heart.

He knelt before the throne, allowing his father to pat his head. In a daze, it felt like he had returned to his childhood, when his father sat on the throne and he sat on his father’s lap.

“Cough, cough... It’s fine. This emperor knows his own body. I can still live for a while longer.” The Xia Emperor’s eyes were cloudy, his vision severely declined. His speech was slurred and flecked with spittle.

“Even if Heaven wants to take this emperor’s life away, it’s still not time.

“This emperor knows you seek a life of freedom and have no intention to inherit the throne. As a parent, I won’t force you.

“However, if the crown prince is not decided early, and one day I can no longer hold on and pass away, the national fortune attached to me will lose its master and may become restless. That will inevitably lead to turmoil, requiring the Old Ancestor to step in.

“This national fortune is the foundation of our Great Qia. No mishap can be allowed.

“Old Two is too scheming, prone to outsmarting himself. Old Three knows he lacks talent for governance, devoting himself solely to literature... Your eight younger brothers all have various flaws and are unfit for the great responsibility. I can’t be at ease if I entrust this kingdom to them. As for your seven younger sisters, you also know...”

“Emperor Father, say no more. I will be the emperor!” Jiang Qun was heartbroken, sobbing uncontrollably as he nodded in agreement.

I know Emperor Father has always held me in high regard. Otherwise, he wouldn’t have entrusted the matter of handling the Ji Province officials to me. This was for me to establish my authority.

“Ah, that’s what you said! No backing out!” The Xia Emperor suddenly straightened his back, his eyes clear and bright, shining with vigor as he looked at Jiang Qun. There was no trace of the man on death’s door from moments ago.

Jiang Qun, “...”

Dad, if you’re fine, could you please stop acting?

Second Younger Brother says there’s no honesty in imperial families, with schemes everywhere. He is absolutely right.

Chapter 845: The Icy Throne

“I've changed my mind,” the First Imperial Prince Jiang Qun said calmly, not finding his words the least bit shameless.

Who said I want to be emperor? Who heard it? Is there proof?

“Hey! This emperor taught you since childhood that a promise is worth a thousand gold; you must be honest and keep your promises. Have you forgotten all that?!” The Xia Emperor grew anxious. It wasn’t easy to trick him into relenting. How could he change his mind just like that?

Jiang Qun looked at his father with disbelief. Why didn’t I see you being honest and keeping your promises when you were feigning illness earlier?

“It’s no use even if you change your mind. This emperor has captured it all with a recording orb.” The Xia Emperor understood what kind of person his eldest son was and had made thorough preparations.

Just obediently become emperor.

“I have no shame!” Jiang Qun yelled, sticking his neck out like a dead pig unfazed by scalding water, a stark contrast to his elegant public image.

Father and son glared at each other like two fighting cocks, neither yielding.

In the end, the Xia Emperor couldn’t hold out and conceded first.

He let out a long sigh. “Just look at you. Everyone is fighting to inherit the throne. Why is it that when it comes to you, you absolutely refuse?

“Inheriting the throne makes you not only the ruler of the Central Continent but also the vessel of the national fortune. You know the wonders of the national fortune; it greatly aids cultivation.”

Jiang Qun also bared his heart. “Dad, you should know best as the person on the throne. The throne seems comfortable, but in reality, it’s restrictive in every way. Putting aside other things, can you travel incognito among the people like I do all day?

“Cultivators seek a carefree life, one of freedom and ease. If I ascend the throne, I’ll lose my freedom. Even with the aid of the national fortune, my mental state will deteriorate. How could I cultivate in the future?

“Huh? Dad, what’s with your expression? As a cultivator, haven’t you even comprehended such a simple principle?”

The Xia Emperor, “...”

Don’t think you’re all that impressive just because your cultivation talent is higher than your dad’s.

“Let’s also talk about that ancestor in the forbidden ground. Although I don’t know his identity, I assume he also once sat on the throne. Why did he step down from the throne? Surely it’s also because he found it stifling?

“How about this? You pick a successor you like. I think Second Younger Brother, Fourth Younger Brother, and Fifth Younger Brother all have the ambition. Let them inherit the throne, and I’ll assist him to ensure he doesn’t make mistakes.”

The Xia Emperor’s beard bristled with anger. “Nonsense! Our family has never had such a precedent in a hundred thousand years!”

“Dad, if there’s nothing else, I’ll be leaving then. You should just rest and recuperate in peace.” Jiang Qun prepared to take his leave.

“Wait.” A sudden thought struck the Xia Emperor, and he called Jiang Qun back.

Jiang Qun had no choice but to walk back, hands tucked in his sleeves. “What?”

“Didn’t you say that when you travel incognito among the people and encounter injustice, it feels particularly satisfying when you reveal your identity?”

Jiang Qun hesitated for a moment and told the truth. “...Yes.”

“Then, how about this? You know all my habits. Transform into my appearance and handle official duties for a few days. I’ll go out and have some fun.”

Jiang Qun looked at his father in shock. Dad, do you hear what you’re saying?

The Xia Emperor felt his son was right. For cultivators, the most important thing is freedom and ease. “I don’t have many days left to live. Can’t I enjoy life a little? As my eldest son, what’s wrong with sharing your father’s burdens?”

“As you command.” Since his father had already said so much, Jiang Qun could only comply.

“Come, come, sit here.” The Xia Emperor hurriedly vacated his seat, pressing his son onto the throne, while he went to the national treasury to find treasures that could conceal his identity.

The Xia Emperor’s cultivation was mediocre, only at the Divine Transfiguration Stage. If he relied on his own methods for disguise, he could easily be recognized. But that was fine; the national treasury was full of means to conceal one’s identity.

Jiang Qun watched his father’s retreating figure. Even from behind, he could see his father’s joy, as if he was finally liberated from the throne.

He breathed out a sigh, feeling that the throne was not comfortable at all. It was icy, the cold seeping into one’s heart.

“Why doesn’t this chair even have a cushion?

“And my dad sat here for so long, yet it’s still not warmed up?”

~~~

Perhaps someone had intentionally spread the news of the Second Imperial Prince hosting Lu Yang, or perhaps the other imperial princes could no longer restrain themselves. Ever since “Lu Yang” left the Second Imperial Prince’s residence, “he” received gifts daily from both the Fourth Imperial Prince and the Fifth Imperial Prince.

Although Lu Yang’s inclination didn’t have a decisive effect, it could still play a massive role in the succession to the throne. Everyone wanted to win over this heavyweight chip.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was completely oblivious to how important she was, and neither did she care why people were sending her gifts. She generously accepted them all. With these gifts, she helped Lu Yang cultivate, causing his sleep quality to improve considerably.

Meanwhile, Lu Yang was sparring with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul in the mental space.

“One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords!” Lu Yang yelled.

High up in the mental space, densely packed swords materialized, a sight that made one’s heart shudder with fear.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul also performed One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords. Streaks of sword qi transformed into tangible swords that darted out from the ground.

Human and nascent soul attacked simultaneously. Tens of thousands of blades collided, sparks flying everywhere, killing intent soaring to the sky.

Next, both Lu Yang and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul executed Village in Palm. Their palms clashed with a thunderous boom.

Lu Yang had unleashed two major killing moves successively, depleting his spirit energy. Just as he was catching his breath, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul charged over and slammed into him, sending him flying.

“Stop, stop, stop. I’m not fighting anymore.” Seeing the Unbeatable Nascent Soul about to continue, Lu Yang hastily called a halt.

He and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul had the same total amount of spirit energy. However, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul still had strength left after consecutively using two moves. This implied that the Unbeatable Nascent Soul used its spirit energy more meticulously when unleashing these moves, ensuring no wastage. This is what I need to learn.

“Perform it once more for me to see.”

With the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s verbal decree, Lu Yang could command the Unbeatable Nascent Soul as he pleased. He could not only have the Unbeatable Nascent Soul spar with him but also make it repeatedly perform a specific move for him to observe and analyze.

Thus, Lu Yang’s cultivation speed increased significantly.

“Hmm? The Jiang Family’s fourth son wants to invite this immortal over.” This day, while routinely receiving gifts, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy discovered an invitation among them.

The Fourth Imperial Prince’s tone in the letter was exceedingly magnanimous, expressing his hope that Lu Yang would visit his home and allow him to extend the courtesies of a host.

Lu Yang had heard that this Fourth Imperial Prince had a strong jianghu air about him. He loved making friends and didn’t mind their status, having friends from all walks of life.

Previously, Lu Yang hadn’t paid much attention to this. But after hearing from Meng Jingzhou’s father that the Fourth Imperial Prince also had ambitions for the throne, he began contemplating the purpose behind the Fourth Imperial Prince’s actions.

From another perspective, having friends from all walks of life indicated that the Fourth Imperial Prince’s eyes and ears were everywhere—a terrifying intelligence network. I’m afraid even Senior Brother Dai’s intelligence isn’t as detailed as the Fourth Imperial Prince’s.

Lu Yang pondered. It appears that this Fourth Imperial Prince feels that he has sent enough gifts and established some rapport, which is why he sent the invitation.

“Immortal Fairy, are you going?”

“Sure, why not?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had enjoyed herself the last time she visited the Second Imperial Prince’s residence.

Chapter 846: The Fourth Imperial Prince’s Scheme

The Fourth Imperial Prince had planted an informant among the Second Imperial Prince’s retainers. He knew every detail of what transpired on the day the Second Imperial Prince hosted Lu Yang.

“Lu Yang managed to turn the tables, changing his identity from guest to host in an extremely short time. Such scheming is truly admirable. Even my Second Elder Brother, who’s always known for his meticulous scheming, fell for it.”

Aware that Lu Yang was not easy to deal with, the Fourth Imperial Prince had spent consecutive days sending gifts to the Meng Estate to demonstrate his goodwill.

Now, he felt that the goodwill had been sufficiently demonstrated and that he could proceed to the next phase of his plan.

~~~

“Brother Lu Yang! Your reputation precedes you. Meeting you today, your bearing is truly extraordinary!” Like the Second Imperial Prince, the Fourth Imperial Prince stood at the entrance to welcome Lu Yang. He even followed the jianghu etiquette, making him seem less like a noble prince and more like a chivalrous hero from the greenwood.

The world spread tales of his forthrightness and his willingness to befriend anyone regardless of status. In reality, every person he befriended was useful to him. To conceal his true intentions, he had even sworn brotherhood with many ordinary, unremarkable cultivators.

Meng Jingzhou had temporarily entered seclusion, so the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t bring him along. Moreover, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that Meng Jingzhou’s presence made little difference.

I have the Second-in-Command in the mental space to strategize for me.

Even if the Second-in-Command’s wisdom is inferior to my own, he can still provide some ideas for reference.

The Fourth Imperial Prince secretly observed “Lu Yang”’s attitude. Noticing “he” was unmoved by the praise, the Fourth Imperial Prince couldn’t help but find it a bit strange.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also found the Fourth Imperial Prince strange. Why are you telling me all these obvious truths? Isn’t this common knowledge? Why are you being long-winded?

The Fourth Imperial Prince felt that “Lu Yang” was indeed inscrutable and had no choice but to continue speaking. “Brother Lu, please, come inside quickly.”

The Fourth Imperial Prince’s official residence featured winding streams and picturesque gardens, with musicians playing melodies that complemented the environment, creating quite an ambiance.

Many cultivators had gathered at the Fourth Imperial Prince’s official residence. Scions from ancestral clans constituted a small portion; the majority comprised brothel proprietors, teahouse owners, painters, physicians, and even matchmakers.

These friends had gone through life and death with the Fourth Imperial Prince and were absolutely trustworthy.

In contrast to the atmosphere from the music, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could sense that upon her arrival, everyone was looking at her with very tense expressions.

The Fourth Imperial Prince invited Lu Yang to the secondary seat, while he took the main seat.

Once the Fourth Prince was seated, the atmosphere relaxed considerably. Fine wine and delicacies were served as if they were complimentary, even more sumptuous than the feast at the Old Dragon Emperor’s birthday banquet at the East Sea.

Of course, this was partly because the Fourth Imperial Prince had far fewer guests than at the Old Dragon Emperor’s birthday banquet.

Although the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was quite disdainful of these spirit dishes, which she found average, considering that eating them could help Lu Yang’s cultivation, she had no choice but to consume them.

Cups clinked, and from time to time, performers used spells and magical abilities to liven the atmosphere. For a while, laughter and cheerful chatter filled the air.

Suddenly, the Fourth Imperial Prince was moved by the scene and set down his bronze wine cup, letting out a long sigh.

“What a pity. I fear we may find it difficult to have such gatherings in the future.”

These words immediately cast a heavy pall over the venue. The guests also set down their chopsticks, their gazes turning to the Fourth Imperial Prince. Before coming, they had roughly guessed the reason the Fourth Imperial Prince had gathered them here—to conspire for a great undertaking.

“Your Highness, why do you say that?” someone asked loudly.

The Fourth Imperial Prince looked at everyone with a complicated expression, then glanced at “Lu Yang,” who had been eating with “his” head down the whole time. He grabbed his wine cup and drained it in one gulp. Perhaps the words to come were too treasonous, and he required alcohol to pluck up his courage.

“Emperor Father’s lifespan is nearing its end. I am his son, yet I can’t offer any help. Watching Emperor Father age day by day, I can hardly eat or sleep.

“In my sleep, I often dream that Emperor Father has passed away. Big Brother, Second Elder Brother, and Third Elder Brother fight for the throne, plunging the people into abject misery. I wake up in the middle of the night, covered in cold sweat.

“I often think about how Emperor Father loves the people like his own children and would absolutely not wish to see such a scene. I want to change all this. Unfortunately, my power is weak and limited. How could I possibly interfere in the struggle for the throne?

“By then, Great Xia would be in turmoil. We are all people who care for the world in our hearts. How could we drink and make merry here?”

Everyone envisioned the scene the Fourth Imperial Prince described and lowered their heads one after another. Some even shed tears of sorrow, their emotions genuine.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked up, not understanding why they had suddenly started acting. Forget it, it’s got nothing to do with me. She continued lowering her head to eat for Lu Yang.

The Fourth Imperial Prince naturally had no idea of what was going through “Lu Yang”’s mind. Noticing “Lu Yang” look up, he believed “Lu Yang” was beginning to take an interest in them.

Below, a middle-aged scholarly man spoke up. “Actually, there is a method. But this method is treasonous and cannot be implemented.”

The Fourth Imperial Prince said urgently, “Teacher Lu, please say it.”

“It cannot be said.” Teacher Lu continued shaking his head.

“No matter how treasonous it is, how can it compare to the peace and well-being of the people in the world?” Under the Fourth Imperial Prince’s persistent questioning, Teacher Lu finally revealed the plan.

“If we desire peace under heaven, we need an undisputed ruler of the world to inherit the throne. Rightfully, that should be the First Imperial Prince. However, the Second Imperial Prince and Third Imperial Prince would not stand idly by. This is what gave rise to the struggle for the throne.

“As long as the three imperial princes lose the qualification to contend for the throne, the throne will naturally be yours.”

The Fourth Imperial Prince wanted to speak up to stop him, but Teacher Lu seemed to already know what the Fourth Imperial Prince wanted to say and didn’t give him a chance to speak. “Your Highness, I know you have no intention of contending for the throne. But for the sake of the world’s populace, there is no other way.”

The Fourth Imperial Prince opened his mouth, wanting to say something in rebuttal, but the words seemed so feeble on his lips. In addition, his sworn friends were gazing at him with earnest eyes. How could he utter words of refusal?

“Never mind, never mind.” The Fourth Imperial Prince lowered his head, as if he was resigned to fate. He then asked, “But how are we supposed to make my three elder brothers give up on the throne?”

Everyone fell silent. This was the most difficult part.

The Fourth Imperial Prince turned his head to consult “Lu Yang.” “Brother Lu Yang, do you have any idea?”

Hearing the question directed at her, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy slurped a mouthful of noodles and looked up at the Fourth Imperial Prince. “Simple. Can’t you just rebel?”

Lu Yang had expected the Fourth Imperial Prince to show a shocked expression. To his surprise, the Fourth Imperial Prince seemed to have anticipated the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s question and continued asking.

“Then, would you be willing to help me?”

The Fourth Imperial Prince had been waiting precisely for this answer from Lu Yang. Based on the intelligence gathered from the Second Imperial Prince’s side, Lu Yang often used rebellion and establishing new dynasties as a topic for idle boasting, cleverly sidestepping the issue of contending for the throne, which made the Second Imperial Prince afraid to engage in deep conversation with him.

But the thing is, I indeed have thoughts of rebellion!

If I don’t rebel, I have no chance of inheriting the throne.

If Lu Yang answers that he’s unwilling, it’ll mean that he’s admitting to idle boasting, and I will have other methods to force him to choose a side.

If Lu Yang insists on saving face and says he’s willing, that will be even better. I can directly drag Lu Yang down into the water and make him stand on my side.

“Sure,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy agreed readily. This suits me perfectly.

Chapter 847: Rebellion

“Since you intend to rebel, have you made preparations?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked. Looking at the Fourth Imperial Prince and his group, they didn’t seem to be acting on an impulse.

“Of course, we have.” The Fourth Imperial Prince laughed heartily. With Lu Yang’s help—or rather, once Lu Yang joins us, the Dao-Seeking Sect can’t possibly stand idly by. If we drag the Dao-Seeking Sect in, our odds of successfully usurping the throne will rise to ninety percent!

“Brother Lu Yang, please take a look. This is my brother, Gongsun Jiu. He possesses a top-tier divine speed cultivation technique, capable of unleashing speed rivalling the Transcendent Tribulation Stage in a short burst. He can approach Big Brother under the pretext of presenting a treasure and strike in an instant. Big Brother wouldn’t even have the time to react!”

Gongsun Jiu grinned broadly. “Your Highness recognized my worth and offered me opportunities. This is my chance to repay your kindness.”

Killing the First Imperial Prince meant certain death. Gongsun Jiu was already prepared to sacrifice his life for the Fourth Imperial Prince.
