The Fourth Imperial Prince introduced another person. “This is my brother, Tang Feng. His assassination skills are superb. If Brother Gongsun fails in the first strike, he will execute the second assassination. No one would expect the interval between the two assassinations to be so short.”

Tang Feng’s appearance was ordinary, allowing him to blend into a crowd.

“Your Highness rescued me from dire straits. My life is yours!”

The Fourth Imperial Prince continued with his introductions. “And this brother is skilled in making poison. He can cause someone to die silently, where they go to sleep and never wake up again!

“This brother is in charge of intelligence. Nothing major or minor in the imperial city escapes his network.

“As for him, he is actually a follower of Second Elder Brother and has long since ascertained his dietary habits and daily routine.

“There’s also...”

Assassins, intelligence agents, informants, excellent actors, failed scholars...

The Fourth Imperial Prince introduced them one by one. Those who could attend this banquet were all his trusted confidants, absolutely loyal to him. Moreover, each possessed unique skills and was hidden among all walks of life. If they revealed their true abilities, they could carve out a reputation for themselves in the jianghu.

The Fourth Imperial Prince’s plans targeting his three elder brothers had long been in the making. However, he still couldn’t figure out their trump cards. With Lu Yang’s addition, everything will be solved.

No matter how great their trump cards are, how can they be compared to the Dao-Seeking Sect?

“Originally, I also planned to make a move against Emperor Father. After all, every additional day he lives allows my younger brothers’ influence to grow, potentially undermining my position. Unfortunately, he has the national fortune protecting him, making it difficult to harm him. That said, I can approach it from other angles, such as destroying everything that may extend Emperor Father’s lifespan!”

“Oh, your preparations are quite thorough.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded, giving a lukewarm comment.

“Brother Lu Yang, it’s still not enough. We need your help!” The Fourth Imperial Prince gazed intently at “Lu Yang,” his eyes filled with sincerity.

“Are you unable to steel yourself and make up your mind? The Everlasting Immortal Fairy thought about it. If that’s the case, I’ll just help the Jiang Family’s fourth son once.

“Alright then, I’ll help.”

A triumphant smirk spread across the Fourth Imperial Prince’s visage. He had used recording orbs to capture everything from his initial contact with Lu Yang until now to prevent Lu Yang from simply walking away.

Now, Lu Yang is a locust on the same boat as me!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stood up. She was the type to act on whatever came to mind. “Then let’s make a trip. Relying solely on you people to deal with your three elders will be somewhat challenging. We need to enlist external forces.”

The Fourth Imperial Prince was elated. He’s taking me to the Dao-Seeking Sect to find helpers.

“Wait a moment, I’ll prepare some meeting gifts.”

“No need.”

~~~

After the Xia Emperor left the imperial palace, he disguised himself and transformed into a naive-looking youth, vastly different from his usual image.

His eldest son had told him, “If you want people to look down on you, you have to disguise yourself as a greenhorn cultivator and give others the impression that you’re inexperienced. This way, it’s less likely for conflicts to arise.”

These were all based on Jiang Qun’s experience.

Suddenly, the Xia Emperor spotted two familiar figures: Yun Zhi’s little junior brother and his fourth son.

Why are these two here?

What puzzled the Xia Emperor even more was that “Lu Yang” was arguing with officials at the entrance of the Ministry of Justice, and it seemed quite heated.

“Why won’t it do? Can you be reasonable?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was somewhat angry. Why is my perfect plan meeting setbacks from the very beginning?

“Get lost, get lost. This isn’t a place for your nonsense.” The officers impatiently shooed “Lu Yang” away.

The Xia emperor strode forward and sternly reprimanded the officers. “Silence! As officials of the Ministry of Justice, how can you treat people so unreasonably?”

The officers glanced at the Xia Emperor and ignored him outright.

The Xia Emperor’s heart leaped with joy. My chance to show off has arrived!

Judging by the situation, Lu Yang must have encountered some injustice and came to the Ministry of Justice to file a complaint, but the Ministry of Justice practiced favoritism and was unwilling to handle the case, leading to this argument.

In moments like this, it is my turn to step forward and uphold justice! After the Ministry of Justice officials belittle and ignore me, I will ideally discover some shady dealings and dirt within the Ministry. When the Ministry tries to cover it up, I can then reveal my identity as the Xoa Emperor before their stunned gazes!

He turned to “Lu Yang,” pretending not to know him, and asked with cupped fists, “Fellow Daoist, what brings you to the Ministry of Justice, and why have you faced such unreasonable treatment?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sized up the Xia Emperor.

For some reason, the Xia Emperor felt guilty. Could Lu Yang have seen through my identity?

That shouldn’t be the case though. The jade pendant I’m wearing is a national treasure-level artifact; how could a Nascent Soul cultivator see through it?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stamped her foot furiously and pointed at the Fourth Imperial Prince, indignantly saying, “I came to report him for plotting a rebellion! The Ministry of Justice won’t accept it and thinks I’m lying! How unreasonable!”

The Xia Emperor, “...”

Wait, what did you just say?

The Fourth Imperial Prince’s reaction was even more dramatic than the Xia Emperor’s. His eyes widened in disbelief as he stared blankly at “Lu Yang,” involuntarily crying out, “This is what you meant by saying you’d help me?”

Never could the Fourth Imperial Prince have imagined this change of events. Moments ago, Lu Yang had verbally agreed to help me rebel and promised to take me to find helpers. But the next moment, he brought me to the Ministry of Justice to report me for plotting a rebellion.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at the Fourth Imperial Prince with a baffled expression, not understanding his extreme reaction. “Yes, what’s the problem? Didn’t you say you wanted to eliminate your three elder brothers to ascend the throne? I thought everything would be solved as long as you rebelled.

“I heard that in Great Xia, those who rebel face the nine familial exterminations. That way, your three elder brothers will definitely die.

“So, here I am, helping you to enlist external forces.”

“Then what about me?!” The Fourth Imperial Prince glared fixedly at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. I don’t know whether my three elder brothers will die, but I know I’m definitely doomed!

“But at the time, you only said to eliminate your three elder brothers. You didn’t say you also wanted to stay alive.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had thought that if the Fourth Imperial Prince’s nine clans were exterminated, the Jiang Family would be left with no one, and it would be her turn to ascend the throne. This is a gift delivered right to my doorstep.

Chapter 848: Terrifying Calculations

Initially, the Xia Emperor had intended to reveal his identity and berate the Ministry of Justice officers. But when the words reached his lips, he couldn’t bring himself to shout them out.

It was his first time hearing that a prince rebelling warranted the nine familial exterminations. No wonder the Ministry of Justice officers were trying to chase Lu Yang away.

He deserves it.

The Fourth Imperial Prince glared fixedly at “Lu Yang,” searching for any hint of jest on his countenance.

However, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy showed no reaction. Her words just now were her genuine thoughts.

The Fourth Imperial Prince was so angry that he laughed. “Lu Yang, let me tell you, don’t try to be clever and play petty tricks. During the discussion in the courtyard earlier, you were the first to suggest rebellion. If you report me, you can’t escape either!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was perplexed, unable to understand the Fourth Imperial Prince’s mind. “How was I the first to suggest rebellion? Didn’t you gather all the people for rebellion? That proves that you were preparing to rebel. I simply followed your line of thinking and voiced your inner thoughts.”

The Fourth Imperial Prince carefully recalled the events in the courtyard, and realization dawned upon him. Lu Yang had never substantively participated in the rebellion plan from start to finish!

This neither counts as complicity nor incitement—this is innocence!

No, there is still a chance to turn things around.

“This is just your side of the story! There’s no evidence!”

That’s right, for a major matter like rebellion, verbal evidence alone can’t secure a conviction. Furthermore, Lu Yang is the only one who has accused me of treason.

The brothers in the courtyard who conspired for the great undertaking all shared life-and-death bonds with the Fourth Imperial Prince and were highly principled. They would absolutely never betray me!

“Ah, but don’t you have recording orbs? I saw you start recording the moment I entered your house. Wasn’t that meant to serve as evidence now?”

In the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes, the Fourth Imperial Prince’s thoughts aligned with her own. To eliminate his three elder brothers, he intended to rebel, leading to the nine familial exterminations, where he takes everyone down with him.

The Fourth Imperial Prince probably couldn’t steel himself and make up his mind to report himself, so he sought my help and invited me to his house, discussing rebellion in my presence and using a recording orb to preserve evidence.

As the Fourth Imperial Prince wished, I came to the Ministry of Justice to report him.

The only two problems are that the Ministry of Justice seems unwilling to interfere in this matter and that the Fourth Imperial Prince wants to back out at the last moment.

How vexing.

The Fourth Imperial Prince’s gaze toward Lu Yang changed once more—fearful, dreadful, and trembling.

In just the span of a visit as a guest, Lu Yang had completely outmaneuvered me! From the moment he stepped through the door, he had been acting, pretending to bare his heart in cooperation and coaxing me into revealing my trump cards. He had even calculated that I would use recording orbs for leverage and threaten him, so he turned the tables, flipping them into evidence of rebellion!

This scheming is even more terrifying than what he’d displayed at Second Elder Brother’s residence!

How laughable that I wanted to tie Lu Yang to my ship. Am I even worthy of scheming against Lu Yang? First, I need to survive this immediate crisis!

Seeing the situation turning dire, the Fourth Imperial Prince turned and fled. However, how could the Everlasting Immortal Fairy let him escape?

The Fourth Imperial Prince’s cultivation at the Divine Transfiguration Stage was no different from a mortal before the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Controlling Lu Yang’s body, she grabbed the Fourth Imperial Prince’s wrist and slammed him to the ground, leaving him utterly disoriented and causing him to see stars. The impact even created a crater in the ground.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also seized the opportunity to snatch the Fourth Imperial Prince’s storage ring, which contained the recording orbs.

The commotion from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s one-sided exchange with the Fourth Imperial Prince was huge, drawing the attention of the Vice Minister of Justice, who hurried over to check on what had happened.

Who dared to start a fight right at the Ministry of Justice’s entrance? Do they think our Ministry of Justice is a pushover?

“Hmm? Has someone in charge arrived?”

Lu Yang informed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy that, based on the person’s attire, this was the Vice Minister of Justice, a fourth-rank senior official.

A fourth-rank senior official was considered a high position. The Minister of Justice was a third-rank senior official.

“You came at the right time. I just caught someone plotting a rebellion and came to report the case.”

The officers didn’t recognize the Fourth Imperial Prince, but how could the Vice Minister of Justice not? Noticing the Fourth Imperial Prince pinned to the ground by “Lu Yang,” he involuntarily shuddered.

Who? The Fourth Imperial Prince is rebelling?

I have worked in the Ministry of Justice for several hundred years, yet it is the first time I’ve heard of someone coming here to report a prince for treason.

Is this something our Ministry of Justice can handle?

“Ah, you don’t handle rebellions?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked, frightening the Vice Minister of Justice into cold sweat.

“Don’t speak nonsense! What do you mean we don’t handle rebellions? If word of that spreads, people might think that our Ministry of Justice is also planning to rebel.”

“If you can’t make a decision, then have someone who can come out.” Seeing the Vice Minister of Justice still hesitating, the Xia Emperor reminded him from the side.

I know my son’s character all too well. My “good” son likely genuinely wanted to rebel. This matter must have a resolution!

The Vice Minister of Justice was in a dilemma. Hearing the Xia Emperor’s reminder, he seemed to see the light. That’s right! Why am I distressed over this? It’s not like I don’t have superiors above me.

At that thought, he immediately went inside to find the Minister of Justice, Xu Xin.

Currently, Xu Xin had just concluded a brief seclusion and came out to change his mood.

Before he could relax, he heard his subordinate reporting to him.

“Lu Yang has come here to report the Fourth Imperial Prince for rebellion?!”

Even during his heart devil tribulation, he hadn’t dared to envision such absurd events.

But the problem was that this wasn’t a heart devil tribulation—it was happening right before his eyes!

Xu Xin clutched his head in pain. After the old Taciturn scoundrel finished tormenting me, is it his little disciple’s turn now?

This little disciple’s troublemaking skills far surpass the old Taciturn scoundrel’s back in the day.

“Just accept it. He’s already run all the way here to file a complaint. It’s inappropriate not to accept it.”

Based on my understanding of Lu Yang, although this kid can stir up trouble, he doesn’t seem to tell lies.

The Ministry of Justice prepared to hold a formal court session to handle the case—a rare occurrence.

The Vice Minister of Justice came to the Ministry of Justice’s entrance and deferentially invited “Lu Yang” inside, fearing this little ancestor might cause some other trouble, like reporting the Second Imperial Prince for rebellion too.

“And you, come in too. You heard the conversation between the Jiang Family’s fourth son and me just now, right? You count as a witness.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also pulled the Xia Emperor inside. “By the way, what’s your name again?”

Before leaving the palace, the Xia Emperor had already thought of a name. The Jiang Family traditionally favored “Xia” as a surname when assuming false identities outside. Since I’m the exalted Son of Heaven, my choice of name should be obvious.

“Xia Tian.”[1]

He had fabricated an entire set of false identities and wasn’t afraid of the Ministry of Justice verifying them.

The Ministry of Justice held court.

Out of trust for Lu Yang, Xu Xin personally broke the restrictions on the Fourth Imperial Prince’s storage ring and retrieved the recording orb inside.

In the recording orb, the Fourth Imperial Prince was in high spirits, fervently introducing his brothers’ extraordinary skills and detailing how to eliminate his three elder brothers one by one. The testimony infuriated the Xia Emperor beside him, his face turning livid.

The evidence was conclusive.

Xu Xin exhaled a sigh. It is exactly as Lu Yang described. The Fourth Imperial Prince indeed has intentions of rebellion. This is a major crime.

“Guards! Escort the Fourth Imperial Prince to the prison!”

“Xu Xin, how dare you!” The Fourth Imperial Prince panicked. If I get imprisoned, I’ll lose any chance of turning things around!

Xu Xin couldn’t care less about the Fourth Imperial Prince’s bluster. I was an official before your father was even born. Who do you think you are? He waved impatiently, ordering the guards to take the Fourth Imperial Prince away.

“Lu Yang, rest assured. A prince who breaks the law is equally guilty as a commoner. This matter will definitely receive a fair trial,” Xu Xin said to “Lu Yang” with a pleasant expression, trying to hint to the latter to stop stirring up trouble. Our Ministry of Justice is small and can’t withstand any upheaval.

“Then can his nine clans be exterminated?” This was what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy cared about most.

Xu Xin, “...”

Receiving no answers from Xu Xin, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy turned to the Xia Emperor. “Do you think his nine clans can be exterminated? Otherwise, exterminating three clans would also do.”

The Xia Emperor, “...”

Back in the palace, you wanted to hit me but didn’t succeed. Now you want to kill me directly, is that it?

1. “Xiatian” also means summer. Alone, “tian” means sky or heaven. ☜

Chapter 849: The Fox Borrowing the Tiger’s Might

After seeing off the great deity that was Lu Yang, Xu Xin finally heaved a sigh of relief. Otherwise, this kid would have insisted that the Ministry of Justice exterminate the Fourth Imperial Prince’s nine clans, making it tricky to handle the situation afterward.

But another problem immediately presented itself. The evidence for the Fourth Imperial Prince’s rebellion is conclusive, but I can’t directly try the Fourth Imperial Prince either. Such a major matter is beyond my capabilities.

“Your Excellency, you still have people above you,” the Vice Ministry of Justice kindly reminded his superior upon seeing his predicament.

Xu Xin saw the light.

That’s right! I’m just the Minister of Justice, a third-rank senior official. Matters of treason should be handled by His Majesty.

~~~

After Jiang Qun sat on the throne, he displayed extraordinary political acumen, managing state affairs no less competently than the Xia Emperor. Otherwise, the Xia Emperor wouldn’t have felt secure temporarily entrusting him with the position.

“Back then, Emperor Father always talked about how troublesome handling state affairs was, having to navigate between various factions and balance interests. It seems it’s not that difficult after all.”

Jiang Qun placed a reviewed court document onto the pile of documents that was half a person high. The only issue was that he remembered the pile of court documents hadn’t been this high before.

“After the Taciturn Daoist Priest succeeded in advancing to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, a large number of people have entered seclusion, huh?” Jiang Qun understood the reason and sighed inwardly.

The numbers are just a little larger than I’d expected, but it’s still within my capabilities.

“Let me take a look at this court document. Lord Xu temporarily emerged from seclusion... What matter has he encountered? Fourth Younger Brother plotted a rebellion... Lu Yang reported him and even demanded the nine familial exterminations?!”

After skimming through it, Jiang Qun’s hand trembled slightly.

I take back my words. Dad, is this the kind of thing you usually handle?

As he read the court document carefully, his anger grew. Finally, he snorted coldly and slammed the table.

“You have quite the nerve, Fourth Younger Brother! You even dared to think of killing me!”

He wrote his response on the court document, instructing the Ministry of Justice to summon several Transcendent Tribulation experts of the imperial court to round up the Fourth Imperial Prince’s sworn brothers in one fell swoop.

As for the matter of the nine familial exterminations, that’s simple.

“I can just pardon myself, can’t I?”

~~~

The large-scale purge targeting the Fourth Imperial Prince’s faction began swiftly. People from the Fourth Imperial Prince’s side were captured, many still bewildered about what had happened.

Wasn’t Lu Yang supposed to help the Fourth Imperial Prince enlist external forces and eliminate the first three imperial princes? How did it become our side getting arrested?

What exactly happened?

The Fourth Imperial Prince’s faction was not small. During the arrests, attempts at resistance led to multiple clashes. But with several Transcendent Tribulation old ministers backing the operation, their resistance couldn’t make waves.

The Fourth Imperial Prince’s downfall shocked all factions in the imperial city. Initially, with the Xia Emperor’s limited lifespan, the various factions had their own calculations, hoping to benefit from the situation. However, the imperial court’s swift and thunderous actions temporarily intimidated them.

The Second Imperial Prince stared at the intelligence in disbelief. Only a few days have passed, and Lu Yang has gotten rid of Fourth Younger Brother.

“Could he be using this matter to warn everyone not to try winning him over to seize the throne?”

The Second Imperial Prince shuddered. I must absolutely not become this person’s enemy!

Originally, the Fifth Imperial Prince had wanted to win Lu Yang over, but he quieted down, not daring to entertain any further ideas about Lu Yang. The subsequent series of plans was also scrapped.

~~~

Upon hearing the Fourth Imperial Prince’s Official Residence had been sealed, the mastermind, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, happily waited for the Ministry of Justice to lead their personnel to raid the imperial palace and confiscate the possessions.

“To my knowledge, according to Great Xia’s laws, the emperor possesses the authority to grant amnesty. It’s probably impossible to implicate the Fourth Imperial Prince’s nine clans through guilt by association.” Noticing “Lu Yang” grumbling the entire way about when the Ministry of Justice would raid the palace, the Xia Emperor’s eye twitched. The Xia Emperor had no choice but to explain, hoping Lu Yang would stop harping on it.

“There’s such a rule?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was truly unaware. Even with my intelligence, I can’t devise a perfect usurpation plan.

She furrowed her brows. “It seems the Jiang Family had foresight; they anticipated today’s events when they stipulated the authority to grant pardons back then!” The Jiang Family managed to formulate such comprehensive laws. Their thoroughness is no less inferior than the Second-in-Command’s, only a bit below my own.

The Xia Emperor, “...”

I think that when they stipulated the authority to grant pardon, no one envisioned today’s events.

“I see that you’re also a talent. Do you want to follow me?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy found Xia Tian quick-witted. After the Great Dou Dynasty is established, he can be appointed as prime minister.

The Xia Emperor didn’t know he had been demoted to a future prime minister. He had merely heard that Lu Yang was a prodigy of the current era, often displaying abnormal actions, with strange things constantly happening around him.

My days are numbered. I might as well personally witness the growth of a future prodigy and reveal my identity at a critical moment. That would make my trip worthwhile.

“Sure,” the Xia Emperor readily agreed.

~~~

“That’s Lu Yang!” In the shadows, several pairs of greenish eyes were fixed intently on Lu Yang.

They were none other than the Fourth Imperial Prince’s sworn brothers. Breaking through multiple encirclements, they had escaped and temporarily avoided imprisonment.

But this was only temporary. With the imperial city sealed, they couldn’t escape no matter what; their arrest was only a matter of time.

We’re not scared of getting captured, but this traitor Lu Yang must die!

Gongsun Jiu, who possessed a divine speed cultivation technique; Tang Feng, whose assassination skills had reached unfathomable heights; the one with mastery in poison arts—these were the brothers the Fourth Imperial prince prided himself on. They had the ability to kill the first three imperial princes. With them making a move, a mere Nascent Soul cultivator like Lu Yang stood no chance of resisting!

“Act now!” Gongsun Jiu commanded through auditory messages.

His brothers moved like soul-reaping envoys from the Nine Netherworlds. When they struck, it meant certain death.

The moment they left the ground, they sensed several terrifying oppressive auras appear, pinning them firmly in place.

Thud. Unable to withstand such pressure, they knelt on the ground, their faces filled with panic.

Transcendent Tribulation Stage! And it’s not just one Transcendent Tribulation cultivator targeting us!

Even when the Ministry of Justice raided the Fourth Imperial Prince’s Official Residence and confiscated his possessions, there hadn’t been that many Transcendent Tribulation cultivators involved.

What’s going on? Why are there so many Transcendent Tribulation experts protecting Lu Yang?!

Could it be that Lu Yang has calculated even this detail?

An old man carrying a shoulder pole walked out from an alley, occasionally calling out “scissors sharpening.”

The old man stood before Gongsun Jiu, a look of contempt on his face.

“How dare you make a move against His Majesty? You must be tired of living.”

Gongsun Jiu and the others were flummoxed. His Majesty? What Majesty?

The Xia Emperor’s safety was of utmost importance. He naturally couldn’t have left the palace alone; palace experts had long been tailing him, providing covert protection.

Even if Gongsun Jiu and the others’ target was Lu Yang, there was a possibility of accidentally harming the Xia Emperor. Hence, they absolutely could not be allowed to act.

~~~

In the mental space, Lu Yang analyzed the current situation for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Your Exalted Majesty, since you reported the Fourth Imperial Prince, you will likely face retaliation from the remnants of his faction in the future. Be careful.”

Lu Yang wasn’t worried about the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s safety; he was worried about his own body.

My scrawny arms and legs can’t withstand the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s antics.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was touched. I didn’t expect Xiao Yangzi to care so much about me.

She comforted him. “Relax, relax. This immortal’s luck has always been great. There won’t be any danger.”

Chapter 850: Mountain-Splitting Axe

Though the Everlasting Immortal Fairy herself was completely unaware, she had practically become a prominent figure in the imperial city long ago. Various factions closely watched Lu Yang’s every move.

The Second Imperial Prince and the Fifth Imperial Prince paid special attention to Lu Yang’s activities. They knew the Fourth Imperial Prince’s remnants would definitely make a move against Lu Yang. This was the price for opposing an imperial prince.

Although they were competitors with the Fourth Imperial Prince, this was still an internal matter of the imperial family. There is no place for an outsider like Lu Yang to interfere.

Moreover, he resorted to such a dirty method as reporting!

He must pay the price in blood!

However, despite waiting for a long time, what arrived was the silent disappearance of the Fourth Imperial Prince’s remnants, with not even a single corpse left behind. There were only several large craters formed by people kneeling on the ground.

“Transcendent Tribulation Stage! There are more than one Transcendent Tribulation cultivators by Lu Yang’s side!” They simultaneously concluded. If only one Transcendent Tribulation cultivator had acted, the matter couldn’t have been handled so cleanly!

“No wonder Lu Yang has always been so fearless. We thought he relied on the Dao-Seeking Sect as his backing, but never imagined he had Transcendent Tribulation cultivators by his side!”

The two princes reeled from the shock. The more they interacted with Lu Yang, the more terrifying he seemed—his strength appeared bottomless!

Yet no one knew that the limelight figure Lu Yang had long had his body taken over by an ancient immortal. The current immortal was merely a puppet manipulated at will by that ancient immortal. How pitiful, how lamentable.

~~~

As the Meng Estate was surrounded by enemies, outsiders couldn’t enter. However, Meng Potian had high hopes for Lu Yang’s future and granted him privileges that were equivalent to those of Meng Jingzhou in the Meng Family.

Apart from inheritance, this included all rights, such as bringing outsiders in.

After hearing that Lu Yang had used the Ministry of Justice to eliminate the Fourth Imperial Prince, Meng Potian increasingly felt that Lu Yang had an affinity with the Meng Family.

“Lu Yang-gege, you’re back?” Seeing “Lu Yang” return, Meng Jingyu excitedly ran over.

“Who is this gege?” Meng Jingyu curiously looked at Xia Tian behind Lu Yang.

Hearing Meng Jingyu call him “gege,” the Xia Emperor’s face twitched slightly. He knew Meng Jingyu. He had even personally attended her hundredth-day celebration.

Meng Jingzhou and his sister’s mother was the Xia Emperor’s elder sister, the Eldest Imperial Princess. In terms of seniority, Meng Jingzhou and his sister were his nephews and niece.

“His name is Xia Tian. Although his cultivation is lacking, his mind is sharp. He works for me now.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke with the tone of a bandit king, which Meng Jingyu inexplicably found impressive.

Meng Jingyu blinked and sweetly greeted, “Hello, Xia-gege.”

The Xia Emperor was beginning to regret his decision. How could I have forgotten? Following this kid Lu Yang may broaden my horizons, but Lu Yang is so close with Meng Jingzhou; I will have to interact with the Meng Family frequently.

What am I supposed to do then?

I have just stepped through the Meng Family’s door, and I’m already a seniority lower.

Meng Jingyu had little interest in Xia Tian, grabbing “Lu Yang”’s hand as she ran toward the study.

“Lu Yang-gege, the teacher assigned homework about ancient history. Can you teach me? My elder brother often praises your exceptional knowledge of ancient history.”

The Meng Family emphasized their children’s holistic development, which included learning history.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy immediately agreed. “A trivial matter.”

When it comes to ancient history, who could be more familiar with it than I am?

~~~

Meng Jingyu was a diligent and studious child. The study displayed neatly arranged books with their covers somewhat soiled, clearly the result of frequent reading. It was completely unlike the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who let books gather dust in her study.

“How do you answer this question? ’An ancient immortal once forged the Mountain-Splitting Axe. What was the reason for its creation?’”

If the real Lu Yang were here, he would tactfully tell Meng Jingyu that ancient history wasn’t worth studying and that learning modern history was good enough.

But the current Lu Yang had his body taken over. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy would only speak the unvarnished truth.

“If you’re asking about that, then there’s quite a story to tell...”

~~~

The next day, the private teacher coldly swept his gaze across the fidgeting juniors of the Meng Family. He was notoriously ill-tempered, obstinate, and feared no one.

“Yesterday’s assigned homework was indeed somewhat difficult, especially regarding the origin of the Mountain-Splitting Axe.

“As everyone knows, the Mountain-Splitting Axe is an ancient magical treasure. Although its power is far inferior to the immortal artifact, the Heaven-Splitting Axe, its fame is in no way lesser.”

Both the Mountain-Splitting Axe and Heaven-Splitting Axe were extremely famous. Back during the Dao-Seeking Sect’s entrance trials, the River Spirit had produced an ordinary axe, the Mountain-Splitting Axe, and the Heaven-Splitting Axe from the river.

“Regarding the Mountain-Splitting Axe’s origin, no ancient text clearly records it. However, by conscientiously studying the extracurricular reading I assigned, you can deduce the answer.

“The Mountain-Splitting Axe was forged by the ancient immortal, the Heaven Mandate Immortal, before he became an immortal.

“According to records, the ancient forebears were trapped in ten thousand massive mountains, and it was hard to establish contact with the outside world. The Heaven Mandate Immortal forged an axe, split the mountains, and carved out a path. Hence, the ancient forebears named this axe the Mountain-Splitting Axe.”

The teacher's voice grew increasingly icy. “But look at all of you! Blank submissions! Of course, not everyone did that. Meng Jingyu, come, tell us what you wrote!”

Meng Jingyu spoke up confidently, recounting the story the Everlasting Immortal Fairy told her yesterday. “In ancient times, the Heaven Mandate Immortal was impoverished. To eke out a living, he excavated mountains and charged tolls. He would place the axe across the road and say to passers-by, ‘This mountain was split open by me, and these trees were planted by me. If you wish to pass, leave the toll behind.’[1] Only after receiving payment would the Heaven Mandate Immortal lift the axe and let them pass.

“Hence, the ancient forebears named this axe the Mountain-Splitting Axe.”[2]

“You learned this from a book?” The teacher’s expression was peculiar. Which pirated book is misleading students?

“This is what Lu Yang-gege told me. It can’t be wrong.” Meng Jingyu had complete trust in Lu Yang.

“Lu Yang? Call him over! I'll debate this with him!” The teacher naturally knew of Lu Yang’s reputation, but that was as a cultivation genius, not a history genius. I have painstakingly studied ancient history for so many years; how could I possibly fear Lu Yang in this field?

Meng Jingyu hurriedly brought “Lu Yang” over.

“Lu Yang-gege, Teacher said what you told me yesterday was wrong.”

“Ah, which part is wrong?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was puzzled. Had I misremembered? That shouldn’t be. I was the one who came up with the catchphrase for the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

The teacher stated the standard answer, which was also the widely accepted answer in academic circles.

“Isn’t that roughly the same as what I said?”

The teacher was so furious that his beard bristled. “It’s completely different! The Heaven Mandate Immortal in your version is a bandit who blocked the roads!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy retorted with conviction, “How is that a bandit? The Heaven Mandate Immortal toiled hard to chisel through mountains with his axe, creating a passage, and cultivated the Tree-Planting Mantra to plant trees. Isn’t it reasonable to charge a fee?”

“Then the Heaven Mandate Immortal couldn’t possibly have said things like ‘this mountain was split open by me!’” The teacher felt that this was slandering the image of an ancient immortal.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was even more perplexed. “If you don’t say that, how would others know you were the one who split open the mountain? How would they willingly pay the fee?”

1. This is a bandit-style catchphrase in Chinese novels. ☜

2. The name could be interpreted as splitting/cleaving mountains or opening mountains. ☜

Chapter 851: An Unexpected Acquaintance

The teacher opened his mouth, intending to refute, but the words seemed to get stuck on his tongue.

It seems that Lu Yang has a point.

“Then how do you explain the Heaven-Splitting Axe? It can’t be that the Heaven Mandate Immortal used the axe to split a path through the sky, shout ‘this sky was split open by me,’ and charged a toll, thus naming the axe the Heaven-Splitting Axe, right?!’

The teacher recalled the origin of the Heaven-Splitting Axe. No ancient text recorded why the Heaven Mandate Immortal named his immortal axe thus. It was a mystery that plagued historians, with various theories abounding.

Some speculated that the Heaven Mandate Immortal once split the heavens open, separating hundun primal chaos and dividing yin and yang. Others theorized that when the immortal axe was forged, an unusual phenomenon occurred, where the sky was split open, and all living beings paid homage. Some also surmised that with this axe, the Heaven Mandate Immortal could refine heaven and earth anew, evolving earth, fire, wind, and lightning... Antiquity historians debated endlessly, with no consensus in sight; all were conjectures without evidence.

“It’s because the Heaven Mandate Immortal found the name cool! Does there need to be another reason?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at the teacher, baffled.

She always felt that techniques and artifacts didn’t need flashy names and that simple ones were fine, like the Play-Dead Technique and Immortal Fairy Fist Technique. On the other hand, the Heaven Mandate Immortal always believed that the names of techniques and artifacts had to be cool, such as the Heaven-Splitting Axe, the Hundun Primal Chaos Furnace, and the Universe Bell.

“How risible! What kind of figure was the Heaven Mandate Immortal? There must be profound meaning behind those naming choices!” The teacher evidently didn’t believe the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s explanation. This is simply absurd.

He continued, “For example, the legendary Hundun Primal Chaos Furnace! Ancient texts clearly record that the Heaven Mandate Immortal used this furnace to refine hundun primal chaos, thus naming it the Hundun Primal Chaos Furnace!”

“Ah, you’re talking about the Hundun Primal Chaos Furnace? That’s because this immortal...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy almost revealed her identity out of habit but stopped halfway. Finding it inappropriate, she quickly changed course. “That’s because the Heaven Mandate Immortal used the furnace to cook a faceless hundun beast, so he named it the Hundun Primal Chaos Furnace.”

The Hundun beast was one of the Four Perils of the Ancient Era, equally famous at the Qiongqi.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy quite missed the Hundun Primal Chaos Furnace. Cooking without it feels like something is missing.

The teacher hesitated but didn’t retort. He suddenly recalled that the Heaven Mandate Immortal had seemingly written the Comprehensive Culinary Compendium, which mentioned how to cook a hundun beast. It does seem plausible.

Could the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s naming sense truly be this poor?

“Lu Yang, since you presume to have some understanding of ancient history, do you dare come to our Imperial Taixue Academy for an academic discussion?”

The teacher’s name was Ye Gu. He wasn’t a member of the Meng Family but a historian from the Imperial Taixue Academy. He taught at the Meng Family as a private teacher simply because they offered a high salary.

“Now?”

“Now!” After suffering successive blows from “Lu Yang,” Ye Gu wanted to seek help at the Imperial Taixue Academy.

The Meng Family disciples below instantly erupted into cheers. With the teacher returning to the Imperial Taixue Academy, there would be no classes today.

Ye Gu glared fiercely at them and had someone distribute the test papers prepared beforehand, immediately triggering a wave of groans.

~~~

The Xia Emperor hadn’t entered the private school. He was waiting outside when he saw Lu Yang walk out.

“Where are we going?”

“To the Imperial Taixue Academy. This person thinks my knowledge of ancient history is pretty good, so he’s inviting me to give a lecture,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied happily.

The Xia Emperor’s expression turned off. The Imperial Taixue Academy is full of obstinate, curmudgeonly old scholars. Could they really invite Lu Yang to give a lecture?

“I’m telling you to come to the Imperial Taixue Academy for an academic discussion!” Ye Gu corrected.

“Taunting me with reverse psychology; I get it.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy saw through Ye Gu’s non-existent subtle intentions at a glance.

As Lu Yang’s follower, the Xia Emperor naturally followed them to the Imperial Taixue Academy.

~~~

The Imperial Taixue Academy was a prestigious educational institution in Great Xia. However, its research focused not on cultivation but on history. Most historical information about Great Qian and Great Yu were results of the Imperial Taixue Academy’s research.

And the most mysterious of all—ancient history, the subject of many legends—also fell within the scope of the Imperial Taixue Academy’s research.

Along the way, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy saw many disheveled scholars arguing with each other, each holding their own view and not yielding an inch.

“This Comprehensive Culinary Compendium clearly states that cooking times should be measured in seconds! How can that be wrong?!”

“Loan characters! They must be loan characters!”

“What loan characters? The Heaven Mandate Immortal must have loved salt! Have you not seen how he would always look down and say, ‘This lord has eaten more salt than the roads you have walked?’ after defeating formidable foes? That’s ironclad proof!”

The three scholars argued, looking as if they might come to blows at any disagreement.

In the mental space, Lu Yang watched all this silently, feeling that the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s reputation was probably beyond salvage.

Lu Yang saw another group of scholars discussing.

“According to my analysis, the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s Dao Fruit is likely related to heavenly tribulations.”

“That’s indeed possible... Wait, what did you just say?”

“I was saying that the Heaven Mandate Immortal... Right, what was I saying?”

The two scholars looked at each other, neither able to recall what had just been discussed.

Ye Gu led Lu Yang and the Xia Emperor deep into the Imperial Taixue Academy, to a simple and crude thatched cottage.

Inside, an elder with a weathered face was discussing something with someone. When the conversation grew exciting, his eyebrows would dance in delight.

The elder was none other than the Dean of the Imperial Taixue Academy, Qi Xiuya. Long renowned, he was a master of both ancient and modern history, with his attainments in the field of history unmatched. The outside world respectfully called him “Dean Qi” or “Elder Qi.” He rarely appeared in public, living a reclusive life. Even Lu Yang, who was currently in the limelight, had never heard of him.

One could even say he held no grudge against the Taciturn Daoist Priest, which showed just how isolated he was.

The person sitting opposite him had his back to the door.

Seeing Ye Qu enter, Qi Xiuya was somewhat surprised and asked with a smile, “Little Gu, shouldn’t you be teaching at the Meng Family at this hour? What brings you here?”

“Teacher, while lecturing at the Meng Family, we discussed the origin of the Mountain-Splitting Axe. This fellow Daoist Lu Yang proposed an alternative theory for its origin.”

Ye Gu recounted “Lu Yang”’s words. Qi Xiuya stroked his long white beard, remaining silent.

“That is an interesting viewpoint. But there’s no evidence, right?” Qi Xiuya also didn’t know whether “Lu Yang” was right or wrong, so he sought help from the person sitting opposite him.

“Fellow Daoist Jin, what do you think?”

Qi Xiuya formally introduced the person sitting across from him. “Let me introduce this fellow Daoist I’ve recently befriended. This fellow Daoist appears young but possesses unique insights into ancient history. Just half a day of conversation has greatly expanded my knowledge.

The person addressed as Fellow Daoist Jin looked down pensively. “I have indeed heard that in the early years, the Heaven Mandate Immortal had yet to rise to prominence. Cultivation resources were insufficient, and he charged tolls. The axe he used back then was indeed the Mountain-Splitting Axe, and he would mutter things like ‘this mountain was split open by me...’

“Strange. People nowadays shouldn’t know about such things.”

Fellow Daoist Jin stood up and faced Lu Yang with a slightly surprised gaze.

Only then did Lu Yang see Fellow Daoist Jin’s appearance—a petite, cute-looking young girl with a cold, unsmiling visage.

Lu Yang didn’t recognize Fellow Daoist Jin, but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy did.

She was Jin Caiwei, the Qiongqi Tribe’s Little Ancestor.

Chapter 852: Jin Caiwei

As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy recognized Jin Caiwei, Jin Caiwei in turn recognized Lu Yang.

~~~

Ever since Chieftain Jin returned to the tribe the last time and proposed to Jin Caiwei that the Qiongqi Tribe ally with the Dao-Seeking Sect, she had been ruminating over the issue.

The Dao-Seeking Sect has the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, a half-immortal who wields the Space Incipient Dao Fruit. They’re indeed qualified to cooperate with our Qiongqi Tribe.

However, she was accustomed to acting alone and didn’t like cooperating with others.

Subsequently, she enumerated the current factions that surpassed the Qiongqi Tribe and concluded that it would be difficult to gain a firm footing in the upcoming Battle of the Great Era.

Zhu Tian governs the Demon Region with over ten Transcendent Tribulation cultivators as his subordinates. Jiang Lianyi has awakened. Ao Ling has awakened. The forces of these three ancient acquaintances are far beyond what I can handle.

The Buddhist Kingdom is suspected of having half-immortals. If it really comes down to a battle, I myself am not afraid, but the Qiongqi Tribe as a whole can’t defeat the Buddhist Kingdom.

The Great Xia Dynasty’s power is unfathomable, and they likely have an immortal with them; we can’t defeat them.

The ancient Heavenly Court is even harder to fight; they have two immortals.

Great Yu’s forces include the First Yu Emperor and the two Imperial Preceptors, experts beyond my capabilities.

And there’s Great Qian’s forces, which have never shown themselves.

An unknown immortal has also appeared in the East Sea; we can’t defeat them either.

The Meng Family can provoke so many formidable enemies and still thrive, indicating they also have a half-immortal behind them.

And this isn’t even counting the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the other two ancient immortals.

Jin Caiwei grew more alarmed the more she counted. If the Qilin Immortal doesn’t appear, staying within the top eleven will be impossible.

These factions are either too large, unsuitable for collaboration with our Qiongqi Tribe, or house immortals, which prevents me from taking the initiative.

By these calculations, only the Dao-Seeking Sect meets the criteria for cooperation—both of us have half-immortals, and both of us are of similar scale.

“Little Jin Que has a point. We can consider cooperating with the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

With this in mind, she decided to set out to observe and investigate the Dao-Seeking Sect.

However, she didn’t go directly to the Dao-Seeking Sect; that would be too direct. Therefore, she went to the imperial city—Great Xia’s cultivation center—to understand local cultivators’ opinions of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

During this time, she heard the Imperial Taixue Academy did some research on ancient history and wanted to see what they had discovered, and that was how she coincidentally met Dean Qi Xiuya.

But she hadn’t expected to run into Lu Yang here.

~~~

As the next sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect and a cultivation seed highly regarded by the Vast Sea Daoist Lord, Lu Yang was one of Jin Caiwei’s key observation targets.

Judging by Lu Yang’s knowledge of the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s secret stories, it seems Lu Yang also has secrets.

“Ah, it’s Little Tiger!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pointed at Jin Caiwei and grinned. I didn’t expect this little tiger Jin Caiwei to still be alive. I’d even held her when she couldn’t yet take human form.

Hearing “Lu Yang” expose her identity outright, Jin Caiwei instantly became vigilant. Her hair stood on end, and her pupils shifted to bright yellow tiger eyes, looking like a startled kitten.

He’s only at the Nascent Soul Stage! How could he possibly discern my race?!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly realized that she was using Lu Yang’s identity and shouldn’t be able to recognize Jin Caiwei, so she pointed at the jade pendant on Jin Caiwei’s chest. “Oh, I meant the little tiger on your jade tablet is so cute.”

The tiger tally jade tablet on Jin Caiwei’s chest was a gift from the Old Qiongqi.

Seeing it was a misunderstanding, Jin Caiwei finally breathed a sigh of relief.

“Immortal Fairy, who is this person?” In the mental space, Lu Yang could tell the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was trying to cover up.

“Do you remember that back in the Qiongqi Tribe’s ancient tomb, there was a coffin containing the Old Qiongqi? The Old Qiongqi had a daughter named Jin Caiwei. She got along well with the Qilin Immortal but didn’t have good relations with Little Ling and Lianyi.

“Back then, this immortal found it strange. The Old Qiongqi died of old age. Jin Caiwei was only at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, so she should have died before the Old Qiongqi. However, the ancient tomb didn’t contain Jin Caiwei’s tomb.

“Now I understand. This little tiger didn’t die. She broke through and became a half-immortal, then slumbered, and has now awakened.”

“Half-immortal?!” Lu Yang was taken aback. What’s with another half-immortal popping out of nowhere? Aren’t half-immortals supposed to be rare? Why are they sprouting like white radishes?

This time, things were different from they had been with Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi. Jin Caiwei didn’t remember the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, and without any message left behind by the Qilin Immortal, they couldn’t find a way to get close.

Dean Qi was unaware of the relationship between this human, demon, and immortal. Seeing Jin Caiwei agree with Lu Yang’s viewpoint, he revealed an intrigued smile.

He knew Jin Caiwei’s level. Her attainments in the field of ancient history far surpass my own. This implies that Lu Yang’s account was true. The Mountain-Splitting Axe was indeed the magical treasure the Heaven Mandate Immortal used when he blocked roads and demanded tolls.

“It appears that Young Friend Lu Yang is highly well-versed in ancient history. I happen to have another question here and would like to seek answers from both of you.”

Listening by the side, the Xia Emperor was astonished. So that’s really the origin of the Mountain-Splitting Axe?

“Go ahead.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy found herself a chair and placed it beside Jin Caiwei before sitting down.

Jin Caiwei was a cautious person, unwilling to interact with strangers. Yet for some reason, when “Lu Yang” sat beside her, she unexpectedly didn’t feel uncomfortable.

Dean Qi asked earnestly, “Legends say that in ancient times, after the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Epoch Immortal became immortals, they had a battle on the moon. Unfortunately, few were qualified to witness it. Do you two know the process or who ultimately won?”

Jin Caiwei pondered for a moment and replied seriously, “I’ve heard of this matter. It’s said that the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s and the Epoch Immortal’s cultivation techniques were fundamentally at odds, forcing them to wage a battle to prove their Dao Hearts.

“In that battle, the Heaven Mandate Immortal activated the Heaven-Splitting Axe, its power astonishing the world, seemingly capable of truly separating heaven and earth. As a living being that was the Jianmu, the Epoch Immortal had a natural affinity for trees. He controlled ancient trees to endlessly reach for the skies, stretching beyond sight.

“The two immortals’ techniques were astounding. It was a collision of ultimate destruction and ultimate vitality—a resplendent scene to be remembered through the ages. Swathes of ancient trees were chopped down by the Heaven Mandate Immortal, while countless broken branches regenerated unceasingly. The entire moon transformed into an ocean of ancient trees. Spectators of that battle trembled and didn’t dare to approach, fearing they might be caught in the residual shockwaves.

“In the end, the battle between the two ended in a draw.”

Although she hadn’t witnessed the battle, she had heard her father describe it afterward. The process can’t be wrong.

To this day, recalling the scenes everyone described sent chills down her spine. The combat power of immortals is too terrifying.

“Ah? Was the process like that? Wasn't it just the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Epoch Immortal getting drunk that day? The Heaven Mandate Immortal boasted about how fast he could swing his axe, while the Epoch Immortal boasted about how well he cultivated the Tree-Planting Mantra and made saplings grow rapidly. The two were unwilling to concede and had a competition on the moon. Wasn’t that it?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scratched the back of her head. The scenes in my memory don’t quite match Little Tiger’s description.

She continued, “After that, the Heaven Mandate Immortal kept swinging his axe, and the Epoch Immortal kept performing the Tree-Planting Mantra. Both were panting heavily from exhaustion.

“They even scared off the Jade Rabbit Tribe living on the moon at the time.”
